This article is about **the [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") once known as Kylo Ren**. You may be looking for **the [pirate](/wiki/Pirate/Legends "Pirate/Legends") [Kybo Ren](/wiki/Gir_Kybo_Ren-Cha "Gir Kybo Ren-Cha")**.

For other uses, see **[Ben](/wiki/Ben_(disambiguation) "Ben (disambiguation)")**.

[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Character)

:   "*Forgive me. I feel it again. The pull to the light. Supreme Leader senses it. Show me again. The power of the darkness. And I will let nothing stand in our way. Show me… Grandfather… and I will finish… what you started.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren, to the helmet of Darth Vader — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8a/ThePullToTheLight.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250403184900)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:ThePullToTheLight.flac "File:ThePullToTheLight.flac"))[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

**Ben Solo** was a [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") [human](/wiki/Human "Human") [male](/wiki/Gender "Gender") who turned to the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force") and became known as **Kylo Ren**, the "**Jedi Killer**" who rose to power as [master](/wiki/Ren "Ren") of the [Knights of Ren](/wiki/Knights_of_Ren "Knights of Ren") and [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader") of the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order") during the [New Republic Era](/wiki/New_Republic_Era "New Republic Era"). Though neither [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") nor [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith"), Ren was trained in the ways of both orders and embodied the conflict between the dark and the [light side of the Force](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force "Light side of the Force"), making him dangerously unstable. Despite his actions as Ren, Solo's connection to the light—combined with the love of his [parents](/wiki/Parent "Parent") and his [connection](/wiki/Force-bond "Force-bond") to the [scavenger](/wiki/Scavenger "Scavenger") [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker")—helped the fallen Jedi to reject the dark side shortly before his [death](/wiki/Death "Death") in [35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY").

A scion of the legendary [Skywalker family](/wiki/Skywalker_family "Skywalker family"), Solo was the son of [General](/wiki/General "General") [Han Solo](/wiki/Han_Solo "Han Solo") and [Princess](/wiki/Princess "Princess") [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo"), as well as the nephew of [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker"), and grandson of the [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One") [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"). [Born](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") in [5 ABY](/wiki/5_ABY "5 ABY"), Solo possessed raw strength in [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force") and was trained in the [Jedi arts](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") as Skywalker's [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") from [15 ABY](/wiki/15_ABY "15 ABY") to [28 ABY](/wiki/28_ABY "28 ABY"). Having inherited his bloodline's potential with the Force, Solo surpassed the other apprentices of his Master who hoped to see him rise not only as the first in a new generation of [Jedi Knights](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight"), but also as a future leader in the restored [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order"). Unbeknownst to Solo at the [time](/wiki/Time "Time"), he shared a powerful bond with Rey, [granddaughter](/wiki/Palpatine_family "Palpatine family") of the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"), with whom he formed a powerful [dyad in the Force](/wiki/Force_dyad "Force dyad").

Following the revelation of his grandfather's identity as the Sith [Lord](/wiki/Lord "Lord") [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Vader, Solo became disillusioned with his family and the Jedi Order, both of which he renounced after the [destruction](/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Jedi_Temple "Destruction of the Jedi Temple") of the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_of_Luke_Skywalker "Jedi Temple of Luke Skywalker") on [Ossus](/wiki/Ossus "Ossus"). Adopting the persona of Kylo Ren, the former Jedi took control of the Knights of Ren by [killing](/wiki/Skirmish_on_Mimban "Skirmish on Mimban") their [leader](/wiki/Ren_(human) "Ren (human)") and subsequently championed the First Order's cause of rebuilding the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"). Though trained in the ways of the dark side by Supreme Leader [Snoke](/wiki/Snoke "Snoke"), Ren was unaware that his new Master was an [artificial](/wiki/Bioengineering "Bioengineering") [Strand-Cast](/wiki/Strand-Cast "Strand-Cast") created by Sidious, the fallen [Galactic Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") and [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith") who was secretly [resurrected](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") on the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Exegol](/wiki/Exegol "Exegol") in the [Unknown Regions](/wiki/Unknown_Regions "Unknown Regions") of [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy").

The [outbreak](/wiki/Hosnian_Cataclysm "Hosnian Cataclysm") of the [First Order-Resistance War](/wiki/First_Order-Resistance_War "First Order-Resistance War") in [34 ABY](/wiki/34_ABY "34 ABY") resulted in a chain of events that culminated in Ren's rise to power, from [encountering](/wiki/Battle_of_Takodana "Battle of Takodana") Rey on [Takodana](/wiki/Takodana "Takodana") and [killing](/wiki/Battle_of_Starkiller_Base "Battle of Starkiller Base") Han Solo on [Starkiller Base](/wiki/Starkiller_Base "Starkiller Base"), to [usurping](/wiki/Battle_of_Oetchi "Battle of Oetchi") Snoke's role as Supreme Leader and [confronting](/wiki/Battle_of_Crait "Battle of Crait") Skywalker on [Crait](/wiki/Crait "Crait"). During the last [days](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day") of the First Order's war with the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance"), Ren was [lured](/wiki/Palpatine%27s_broadcast "Palpatine's broadcast") to Exegol where Sidious offered to make the Skywalker heir his [successor](/wiki/Emperor "Emperor") if he succeeded in killing Rey and ending the legacy of the Jedi. Through the sacrifice and forgiveness of his mother, Leia Organa, as well as the memory of his father and the bond he shared Rey, Ben Solo found his way back to the light and renounced the dark persona of Kylo Ren. After the Emperor's destruction during the [Battle of Exegol](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol"), Solo sacrificed his life to save Rey, ultimately becoming one with the Force like his grandfather, uncle, and mother before him. Solo's death marked the end of the Skywalker bloodline, but his sacrifice ensured the survival of their legacy through Rey, who took the name Skywalker.

## Biography

### Pre-natal history and earliest years

#### A voice from the future

:   "*Let the past die.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren, as heard by Darth Vader[[15]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_25-15)

 [![The avatar of Darth Vader heard the voice of his grandson Kylo Ren saying, "Let the past die. Kill it if you have to](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/LetThePastDie-2017DarthVader25.png/revision/latest?cb=20211120170734) [![The avatar of Darth Vader heard the voice of his grandson Kylo Ren saying, "Let the past die. Kill it if you have to](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/LetThePastDie-2017DarthVader25.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20211120170734)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/LetThePastDie-2017DarthVader25.png/revision/latest?cb=20211120170734) 

The avatar of Darth Vader heard the voice of his grandson Kylo Ren saying, "Let the past die. Kill it if you have to."

 

Kylo Ren, the future [dark side](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force") persona of Ben Solo, was the subject of [Force visions](/wiki/Force_vision "Force vision") prior to[[15]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_25-15) [his](/wiki/Gender "Gender")[[4]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_DB-4) [birth](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction"). Shortly after the [Battle of Fortress Vader](/wiki/Battle_of_Fortress_Vader "Battle of Fortress Vader"), the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") [Darth Vader](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") persona of the famed [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") Anakin Skywalker, explored the dark side [portal](/wiki/Portal "Portal") constructed by [Darth Momin](/wiki/Darth_Momin "Darth Momin") in [Fortress Vader](/wiki/Fortress_Vader "Fortress Vader"); within the portal, the spirit of Vader slaughtered illusions of [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") as he heard the voice of Ren saying that it was [time](/wiki/Time "Time") to "let the past [die](/wiki/Death "Death")."[[15]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_25-15)

Ren's voice was also heard by the Jedi [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") [Ezra Bridger](/wiki/Ezra_Bridger "Ezra Bridger");[[16]](#cite_note-A_World_Between_Worlds-16) in [1 BBY](/wiki/1_BBY "1 BBY"),[[17]](#cite_note-Mission_date-17) Bridger [traveled](/wiki/Mission_to_the_Lothal_Jedi_Temple "Mission to the Lothal Jedi Temple") to the [World Between Worlds](/wiki/World_Between_Worlds "World Between Worlds"), a mystical plane that existed between time and [space](/wiki/Realspace "Realspace") where he heard the voice of Ren saying that he would "finish what his grandfather started."[[16]](#cite_note-A_World_Between_Worlds-16)

#### The birth of Ben Solo

:   "*I am in command of my own body, thank you very much.*"  
    "*Tell that to the little bandit.*"  
    "*I think you mean the little* angel*.*"
:   ―Leia Organa and Han Solo[[3]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-3)

In [4 ABY](/wiki/4_ABY "4 ABY"),[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) [Princess](/wiki/Princess "Princess") [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo") and [General](/wiki/General "General") [Han Solo](/wiki/Han_Solo "Han Solo") were among those who led the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic") in a decisive victory over the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") at the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor"). Their victory resulted in the deaths of the [Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor"), [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"), and Organa's biological [father](/wiki/Parent "Parent"), Anakin Skywalker;[[18]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-18) Skywalker ceased to be [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Vader when he saved his son, [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker"), and redeemed himself after [decades](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade") of subjugating [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy").[[19]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_DB-19)

 [![The birth of Ben Solo, son of Han Solo and Leia Organa, marked the dawn of a new era in galactic history.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/TheSkywalkerSoloFamily-BattleOfJakkuLastStand4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250123161257) [![The birth of Ben Solo, son of Han Solo and Leia Organa, marked the dawn of a new era in galactic history.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/TheSkywalkerSoloFamily-BattleOfJakkuLastStand4.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250123161257)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/TheSkywalkerSoloFamily-BattleOfJakkuLastStand4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250123161257) 

The birth of Ben Solo, son of Han Solo and Leia Organa, marked the dawn of a new era in galactic history.

 

Soon after the battle, Organa and Solo [married](/wiki/Marriage "Marriage") and conceived their son, Ben Solo. During her pregnancy, the [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") Organa could sense her son through [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force"), and felt both the [light side](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force "Light side of the Force") and the dark within him.[[3]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-3) Ben was born in [5 ABY](/wiki/5_ABY "5 ABY"),[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) one [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") and four [days](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day") after the Battle of Endor,[[20]](#cite_note-Lost_Stars-20) in [Hanna City](/wiki/Hanna_City "Hanna City"), [Chandrila](/wiki/Chandrila "Chandrila"). His birth was on the same day that the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War") was formally ended with the signing of the [Galactic Concordance](/wiki/Galactic_Concordance "Galactic Concordance") between the Empire and the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic"), the [government](/wiki/Politics "Politics") that arose after the Battle of [Endor](/wiki/Endor "Endor"). Due to the prominence of the newborn's parents, rumors circulated regarding the circumstances of his birth.[[3]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-3) Solo was Force-sensitive and possessed prodigious strength by virtue of his [Skywalker lineage](/wiki/Skywalker_family "Skywalker family"),[[1]](#cite_note-TSWB-1) a trait that he shared with his mother,[[21]](#cite_note-Royal_Rebel-21) uncle, and grandfather.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5)

Ben Solo's name was chosen by his father.[[22]](#cite_note-Han_Solo_BG-22) In [13 BBY](/wiki/13_BBY "13 BBY"),[[23]](#cite_note-Solo_timeline-23) the surname Solo was coined for Han on [Corellia](/wiki/Corellia "Corellia") by [chief](/wiki/Chief "Chief") [recruitment officer](/wiki/Imperial_Recruitment_Officer "Imperial Recruitment Officer") [Drawd Munbrin](/wiki/Drawd_Munbrin "Drawd Munbrin"), who required a full name when Han enlisted for the [Carida Academy](/wiki/Carida_Academy "Carida Academy") to become a [pilot](/wiki/Pilot "Pilot").[[24]](#cite_note-Solo-24) The inspiration for the child's first name was "Ben Kenobi," the alias of the late and legendary [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi");[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25) Kenobi used that name while in [exile](/wiki/Exile_(punishment) "Exile (punishment)") on [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine") after the [fall](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") of the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") at the [end](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar "Mission to Mustafar") of the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"); under this alias, Kenobi [rescued](/wiki/Rescue_of_Princess_Leia_(9_BBY) "Rescue of Princess Leia (9 BBY)") a young Leia Organa from [Fortress Inquisitorius](/wiki/Fortress_Inquisitorius "Fortress Inquisitorius") after being [kidnapped](/wiki/Ambush_on_Alderaan "Ambush on Alderaan") by the [Inquisitorius](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius")[[26]](#cite_note-Part_IV-26) and he later sacrificed his life while [rescuing](/wiki/Rescue_of_Princess_Leia "Rescue of Princess Leia") Organa from the first [Death Star](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station") [battle station](/wiki/Battle_station "Battle station")[[27]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-27) in 1 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system").[[28]](#cite_note-Galactic_Atlas-28)

As the son of an adopted [Alderaanian](/wiki/Alderaanian "Alderaanian") princess, Ben Solo would have inherited the title of Prince of [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan") if that planet and the [House of Organa](/wiki/House_of_Organa "House of Organa") that ruled it had not been [destroyed](/wiki/Destruction_of_Alderaan "Destruction of Alderaan") by the Empire before he was born.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7) Upon his birth, he was considered a member of the [Elder Houses](/wiki/Elder_Houses "Elder Houses") and entitled through hereditary succession to ceremonial titles, such as the [Supreme Governor](/wiki/Supreme_Governor "Supreme Governor") of [Birren](/wiki/Birren "Birren").[[11]](#cite_note-Bloodline-11)

#### Early years

:   "*I know where you come from. Before you called yourself Kylo Ren.*"
:   ―Lor San Tekka[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

 [![Solo was initially raised on his homeworld Chandrila, the first capital of the New Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/SoloFamily-PoeDameronAnnual2.png/revision/latest?cb=20230718031959) [![Solo was initially raised on his homeworld Chandrila, the first capital of the New Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/SoloFamily-PoeDameronAnnual2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20230718031959)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/SoloFamily-PoeDameronAnnual2.png/revision/latest?cb=20230718031959) 

Solo was initially raised on his homeworld Chandrila, the first capital of the New Republic.

 

Ben Solo was prone to crying as an [infant](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling"), particularly in the first [months](/wiki/Standard_month "Standard month") of his life,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) and had difficulty falling [asleep](/wiki/Sleep "Sleep"). He would settle to sleep when he was held by his father[[30]](#cite_note-Last_Shot-30) or upon sensing the presence of his parents or their friend, Han's [Wookiee](/wiki/Wookiee "Wookiee") [First Mate](/wiki/First_Mate "First Mate") [Chewbacca](/wiki/Chewbacca "Chewbacca"). Organa was with Solo for multiple milestones: when he took his first steps, when he said his first word, and when he first instinctively harnessed the power of the Force to [telekinetically](/wiki/Telekinesis "Telekinesis") throw a toy across the room in anger.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) As a toddler, Solo continued to demonstrate his ability to use the Force without either anger or training to bring objects to himself.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7)

Though Han lacked the Force bond that Organa had with their son, he had a fatherly bond with Ben.[[3]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-3) One night, when Ben was two years old, [Chancellor](/wiki/Chancellor_(New_Republic) "Chancellor (New Republic)") [Mon Mothma](/wiki/Mon_Mothma "Mon Mothma") contacted the Solo house in an attempt to speak with Organa while Han and Ben were asleep following multiple nights of insomnia. The household [protocol droid](/wiki/Protocol_droid "Protocol droid"), [T-2LC](/wiki/T-2LC "T-2LC"), awakened the father and son by activating a holo-projection of the chancellor; Han then soothed Ben's crying until they both slept.[[30]](#cite_note-Last_Shot-30)

At that time, the [Solo family](/wiki/Solo_family "Solo family") utilized the [class-3](/wiki/Class_three_droid "Class three droid") [culinary septoid droid](/wiki/Culinary_septoid_droid "Culinary septoid droid") [BX-778](/wiki/BX-778 "BX-778") to help them with the household chores. While supervising Ben at T-2LC's direction, a virus within BX-778 activated and caused the [droid](/wiki/Droid "Droid") to consider cutting Ben's throat in order to stop the toddler's temper tantrum. The droid's programming was restored as a result of Han destroying the [Phylanx Redux Transmitter](/wiki/Phylanx_Redux_Transmitter "Phylanx Redux Transmitter"), erasing the command to kill organics that BX-778 had been infected with. The child was not consciously aware that his life had been endangered[[30]](#cite_note-Last_Shot-30) and he may not have remembered it later; however, the incident may have been retained subconsciously as a near-death experience.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7)

 [![Ben Solo's early childhood was full of love and affection torwards his family and their friends.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/BenSoloPast-LegacyOfVader2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250312095632) [![Ben Solo's early childhood was full of love and affection torwards his family and their friends.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/BenSoloPast-LegacyOfVader2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20250312095632)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/BenSoloPast-LegacyOfVader2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250312095632) 

Ben Solo's early childhood was full of love and affection torwards his family and their friends.

 

Solo grew close to his parents' friends in his childhood; in particular, he showed great affection toward [Lando Calrissian](/wiki/Landonis_Balthazar_Calrissian "Landonis Balthazar Calrissian"), whom he referred to as "Unca Wanwo"[[30]](#cite_note-Last_Shot-30)—and later "Uncle Lando" when he was older[[31]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_50-31)—and who told him stories of Han's days as a smuggler.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7) Chewbacca, whom Solo referred to as "Uncle Chewie," mentored him as he learned how to fly a [speeder](/wiki/Speeder "Speeder") and fire a [blaster](/wiki/Blaster "Blaster"),[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) and he sometimes provided childcare when the boy's parents were occupied with their respective careers.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7)

Solo heard many stories about the time of the Galactic Civil War from his family. His father told him about the time he was frozen in [carbonite](/wiki/Carbonite "Carbonite") while being held as a [prisoner](/wiki/Prisoner "Prisoner") of the [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt "Hutt") [gangster](/wiki/Gangster "Gangster") [Jabba Desilijic Tiure](/wiki/Jabba_Desilijic_Tiure "Jabba Desilijic Tiure"); he learned about about the challenges that the Rebel Alliance faced in the aftermath of the [Battle of Hoth](/wiki/Battle_of_Hoth "Battle of Hoth") from his mother; and Calrissian told Solo about the [Syndicate War](/wiki/Syndicate_War "Syndicate War") as well as the [Scourge crisis](/wiki/Scourge_crisis "Scourge crisis"). Solo was surprised that all of those events occurred in only one year. He would also come to know that Luke Skywalker confronted Darth Vader on more than one occasion. By the time of his Jedi apprenticeship, Solo knew that Vader and [Emperor](/wiki/Emperor "Emperor") Palpatine were both [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith"). He had also been told the Emperor died on the [second Death Star](/wiki/DS-2_Death_Star_II_Mobile_Battle_Station "DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station").[[31]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_50-31)

In [9 ABY](/wiki/9_ABY "9 ABY"),[[32]](#cite_note-AhsokaDate-32) Ben's name was included on a list of heroes on the gauntlet of [Baylan Skoll](/wiki/Baylan_Skoll "Baylan Skoll"), a former Jedi Knight and an ally to the efforts to find the missing [Grand Admiral](/wiki/Grand_Admiral "Grand Admiral") [Thrawn](/wiki/Mitth%27raw%27nuruodo "Mitth'raw'nuruodo") of the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire").[[33]](#cite_note-Part_Two-33)

 [![Han Solo's gold dice became a favorite toy of Ben who, as a toddler, wanted to be like his father.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f3/Kylo_Ren_dice.png/revision/latest?cb=20210410215502) [![Han Solo's gold dice became a favorite toy of Ben who, as a toddler, wanted to be like his father.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f3/Kylo_Ren_dice.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210410215502)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f3/Kylo_Ren_dice.png/revision/latest?cb=20210410215502) 

Han Solo's gold dice became a favorite toy of Ben who, as a toddler, wanted to be like his father.

 

In his youth, Solo's parents had active lives in their respective professions.[[1]](#cite_note-TSWB-1) Restless with settling in one place for long, Han began mentoring young pilots;[[11]](#cite_note-Bloodline-11) he hoped to someday help Ben learn how to repair the [hyperdrive](/wiki/Hyperdrive "Hyperdrive") of the *[Millennium Falcon](/wiki/Millennium_Falcon "Millennium Falcon")* and acquire a [starship](/wiki/Starship "Starship") of his own. He also hoped that Ben would someday choose the same simple path of adventurer rather than the path of a Jedi like his uncle and grandfather.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7) Ben enjoyed playing with the [gold](/wiki/Gold "Gold") [dice](/wiki/Han_Solo%27s_dice "Han Solo's dice") that belonged to his father and would often follow him around. The boy aspired to become a pilot like his father[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) and inherited piloting skills from both his father[[35]](#cite_note-StealthMission-35) and his maternal grandfather. Meanwhile, Organa was a respected [senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") of the New Republic, and as she worked to repair the galaxy[[11]](#cite_note-Bloodline-11) and prepare for the future conflict she sensed, she became occupied with routine senatorial duties.[[1]](#cite_note-TSWB-1)

His parents' increasing reliance upon a droid caretaker and their busy lives contributed to Solo developing a sense of loneliness. Although he was told his parents were away doing important work, a benefit his mother hoped he would realize and appreciate in time, the child had difficulty accepting and believing it.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7)

#### Sowing doubts and darkness

:   "*I have been every voice, you have ever heard, inside your head.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious, to Kylo Ren[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

 [![Resurrected on Exegol, Darth Sidious conspired to turn Anakin Skywalker's grandson to the dark side of the Force.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/SidiousRevealsRey-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200401082421) [![Resurrected on Exegol, Darth Sidious conspired to turn Anakin Skywalker's grandson to the dark side of the Force.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/SidiousRevealsRey-TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200401082421)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/SidiousRevealsRey-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200401082421) 

Resurrected on Exegol, Darth Sidious conspired to turn Anakin Skywalker's grandson to the dark side of the Force.

 

Growing up, Solo was unaware of his Sith heritage as the grandson of Darth Vader. Only his parents and uncle, Jedi Master Luke Skywalker, knew the truth of Anakin Skywalker's past. Organa decided to delay telling Solo the truth about Vader until he was older and her brother could explain how had returned to the light side as Anakin Skywalker.[[11]](#cite_note-Bloodline-11) However, Solo perceived that his family was keeping something from him.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7)

Solo's doubts about his family were encouraged by voices that communicated with him [telepathically](/wiki/Telepathy "Telepathy") throughout his young life, one of which he knew as [Snoke](/wiki/Snoke "Snoke"). The voice used his insecurities and fears against him[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) and would terrify him, claiming that he could not survive without the voice because he was weak. It also provided warnings of danger and told him secrets,[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) which he regarded as comfort and guidance.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Solo did not tell anyone about the voice.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10)

In truth, Darth Sidious was the apex of the dark influence.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Invested in the powerful bloodline of his last apprentice, Sidious intended to convert Solo to the dark side as he did with the child's grandfather. He therefore used Snoke as a proxy to hold sway over Solo. In addition, Sidious infiltrated Solo's mind through the Force, influencing his thoughts and actions in order to turn him against his family and the light side.[[36]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-36)

#### Troubled youth

:   "*When I found you, I saw what all masters live to see.* Raw*, untamed power…and beyond that, something truly special. The potential of your bloodline. A new* Vader*…*"
:   ―Snoke, to Kylo Ren[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

 [![Solo was manipulated and befriended by Supreme Leader Snoke, a creation of Sidious used by the Sith in part to convert the Skywalker heir to the dark side.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/SnokeThrone-TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20250329003018) [![Solo was manipulated and befriended by Supreme Leader Snoke, a creation of Sidious used by the Sith in part to convert the Skywalker heir to the dark side.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/SnokeThrone-TLJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250329003018)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/SnokeThrone-TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20250329003018) 

Solo was manipulated and befriended by Supreme Leader Snoke, a creation of Sidious used by the Sith in part to convert the Skywalker heir to the dark side.

 

Despite being happy in his youth,[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) Solo had rough upbringing; As the Force awakened in young Solo, his parents recognized that he needed guidance despite their efforts to build a normal life for him.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) In childhood, Ben Solo had unintentionally destroyed objects with the Force when angry,[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) and eventually Solo developed feelings of abandonment from his parents because of their busy lives.[[38]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-38) He also was led to believe that his parents thought he was disturbed, having overheard their conversations about him and his lack of control over his innate Force abilities.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

Beginning from his early childhood, Solo was drawn toward the dark side of the Force by Snoke.[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39) Snoke would utilize Solo's feelings of abandonment, desperate need for a teacher, and fascination with his family legacy to seduce him.[[40]](#cite_note-Snoke_Bio_Gallery-40) Having known of Snoke's interest in her son's potential for power, Organa sought to protect Solo from the mysterious [dark side adept](/wiki/Dark_side_adept "Dark side adept"). However, she did not inform her husband about Snoke's designs on their son, believing that, as a non-Force-sensitive, Han would not understand Organa's responsibility to shield Ben.[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39)

Beyond Snoke's influence, Organa recognized similarities between her son and her father; therefore, she counted on her brother to train Solo and prevent him from following his grandfather down the path of the dark side.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) It was because of Solo's heritage of Anakin Skywalker's grandson, Snoke saw a focal point within the boy, believing he had the right balance of both light and the dark, and desired to claim him as his own apprentice.[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39)

### Jedi training

#### Apprentice of Luke Skywalker

:   "*For many years, there was balance and then I saw Ben. My nephew with that mighty Skywalker blood. In my hubris, I thought I could train him; I could pass on my strengths. Han was…* Han *about it, but… Leia trusted me with her son. I took him and a dozen students, and began a training temple.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

 [![Apart from his mother, Ben Solo became the first apprentice of his uncle Luke Skywalker, and proved to be the most gifted student of the Jedi Master.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/Luke_and_Ben.png/revision/latest?cb=20220627024734) [![Apart from his mother, Ben Solo became the first apprentice of his uncle Luke Skywalker, and proved to be the most gifted student of the Jedi Master.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/Luke_and_Ben.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220627024734)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/Luke_and_Ben.png/revision/latest?cb=20220627024734) 

Apart from his mother, Ben Solo became the first apprentice of his uncle Luke Skywalker, and proved to be the most gifted student of the Jedi Master.

 

In [15 ABY](/wiki/15_ABY "15 ABY"),[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) prior to his tenth [birthday](/wiki/Birthday "Birthday"), Solo decided he would begin his [Jedi training](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") and joined Skywalker's initiative to restore the Jedi Order. It was apparent to Skywalker that his nephew was inherently powerful with the Force despite his lack of training in the Jedi arts.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7) Solo learned the ways of the Jedi, in its many forms, under the tutelage of Skywalker who impressed on his pupil the importance of practicing discipline and control. Solo gave his best efforts to gain his Master's approval, although at times their familial bond caused him to address Skywalker as uncle instead of Master. Skywalker had committed his life to reestablishing the Jedi Order's teachings, which had virtually nothing to do with family ties; therefore, he taught Solo that detachment and distance were necessary to gaining the pure focus that every Jedi aspired to achieve.[[41]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-41)

Solo and Skywalker traveled across the galaxy to search for lost lore of the Force, accumulating artifacts and learning more about the Jedi Order's ancient history in the hope of fully restoring it.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) Through his training, Solo developed a strong sense of devotion to the ways of the Jedi;[[42]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-42) he endeavored to gain greater knowledge of the Force and ways of the Jedi Order,[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) desired to prove himself worthy of inheriting the mantle of a Jedi Knight,[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7) and learned a great deal of the teachings about the light side of the Force.[[38]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-38)

As the grandson of the Chosen One and nephew of the last Jedi, Solo felt immense pressure to live up to the Skywalker family legacy, a burden that weighed heavily upon him and ultimately fueled his insecurities.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) Under Skywalker, Solo learned much, leading the young Jedi to acknowledge and idolize his uncle for the knowledge of the Force and power he possessed, considering him a legend. However, Solo had misgivings about Skywalker's teaching methods, feeling as though despite all of what he learned, he was never able to utilize it, and he privately disagreed with his mentor's decision to store and lock away the Jedi knowledge they uncovered within the new Jedi temple.[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25)

 [![Solo constructed his own lightsaber during his apprenticeship under Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/79/BenSoloLightsaber-SWTLC.png/revision/latest?cb=20220916013742) [![Solo constructed his own lightsaber during his apprenticeship under Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/79/BenSoloLightsaber-SWTLC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220916013742)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/79/BenSoloLightsaber-SWTLC.png/revision/latest?cb=20220916013742) 

Solo constructed his own lightsaber during his apprenticeship under Skywalker.

 

As a Padawan, Solo constructed his own [blue-bladed lightsaber](/wiki/Kylo_Ren%27s_lightsaber "Kylo Ren's lightsaber")[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25) and became skilled with its use, ultimately proving to be the most gifted student with a lightsaber Skywalker would ever train.[[38]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-38) Solo would also keep a [calligraphy set](/wiki/Ben_Solo%27s_calligraphy_set "Ben Solo's calligraphy set"),[[43]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-43) a set which once belonged to his namesake Obi-Wan Kenobi,[[44]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_100_Objects-44) within he would record and fill with his own Jedi insights,[[43]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-43) in his quarters during his time with Skywalker.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

Solo was taught by Skywalker to also exercise a level of restraint when he grew more powerful within the Force, a way his uncle attempted to manage his progress in Jedi training.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) Skywalker placed his hope for the future of the Jedi in Solo, convinced for a time he would not die the last of the Jedi Knights.[[42]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-42) At one point, Solo believed in his own destiny as a Jedi, with Skywalker encouraging his belief and resolve.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) Solo and Skywalker traveled the galaxy extensively, gathering lost Jedi knowledge, including [ancient Jedi texts](/wiki/Sacred_Jedi_texts "Sacred Jedi texts") filled with arcane [writings](/wiki/Writing "Writing") and [holocrons](/wiki/Holocron "Holocron") filled with teachings from forgotten bygone eras of the Force.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7)

#### New generation of Jedi

:   "*We were… learning. We all studied together. I was first, but they came not long after. Voe, Hennix, and Tai.*"
:   ―Ben Solo, on the other Jedi apprentices[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13)

 [![Solo was part of a new generation of Jedi trained by his uncle, Luke Skywalker, who sought to restore the Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/LukeTeachingJedi-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250306232725) [![Solo was part of a new generation of Jedi trained by his uncle, Luke Skywalker, who sought to restore the Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/LukeTeachingJedi-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250306232725)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/LukeTeachingJedi-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250306232725) 

Solo was part of a new generation of Jedi trained by his uncle, Luke Skywalker, who sought to restore the Jedi Order.

 

Aside from his mother, whose Jedi training was cut short[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5), and [Grogu](/wiki/Din_Grogu "Din Grogu"), a former Jedi youngling who abandoned his training to return to his friend and adoptive father [Din Djarin](/wiki/Din_Djarin "Din Djarin"),[[45]](#cite_note-BOBF_7-45) Solo was the first student in Skywalker's initiative to rebuild the Jedi Order[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) on [Ossus](/wiki/Ossus "Ossus"),[[41]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-41) where the [Jedi Temple of Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_of_Luke_Skywalker "Jedi Temple of Luke Skywalker") was built to serve as an academy for the new generation of Jedi.[[46]](#cite_note-BOBF_6-46) Skywalker, like his sister,[[11]](#cite_note-Bloodline-11) had tried to shield Solo from the secrets of their family. His efforts to protect his nephew inadvertently left Solo feeling isolated, especially after Skywalker took it upon himself to train multiple apprentices at the same time.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5)

Over the course of their travels, Skywalker gathered disciples, young lost souls adrift with no way to harness their Force-sensitive powers as a result of the Jedi purge,[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7) who went on to become his first students by [16 ABY](/wiki/16_ABY "16 ABY").[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2)[[43]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-43)[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13)[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13)

In addition to several new recruits, [Hennix](/wiki/Hennix "Hennix"), [Tai](/wiki/Tai "Tai"), and [Voe](/wiki/Voe "Voe") were apprenticed to Skywalker; as such, they became acquainted with his first[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13) and strongest pupil.[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47) As younglings, they would sit on the [temple](/wiki/Jedi_temple "Jedi temple") grounds and learn about the Force through Skywalker's lectures while simultaneously honing their skills by levitating rocks.[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13) Together they were all trained in lightsaber combat, meditation, and telekinesis.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7)

Amongst all these students, in terms of Force powers and lightsaber skill, Solo was the most gifted;[[38]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-38) Solo's natural affinity with the Force did not go unnoticed by his peers, particularly Voe, who struggled to hone her skills despite training just as hard as Skywalker's nephew. While training on the temple grounds, Voe watched as Solo levitated a large rock with ease, and wondered why he was far stronger than her. According to Skywalker, however, strength had nothing to do with how the Force worked. He likened using the Force to opening a door, explaining that the Force flowed more easily through those who were open to its energy. Notwithstanding Skywalker's view on the Force, Solo surpassed his peers in every aspect of their training, including [lightsaber combat](/wiki/Lightsaber_combat "Lightsaber combat") and [meditation](/wiki/Meditation "Meditation").[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13)

 [![Solo found a rival within Voe, a fellow student, during his time at Skywalker's Jedi temple.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0c/AllTooEasy-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200213221335) [![Solo found a rival within Voe, a fellow student, during his time at Skywalker's Jedi temple.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0c/AllTooEasy-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200213221335)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0c/AllTooEasy-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200213221335) 

Solo found a rival within Voe, a fellow student, during his time at Skywalker's Jedi temple.

 

His relationships with the other students were different. Hennix could make Solo laugh, and Tai tried to help him cope with the pressures of being a Skywalker. Solo assured his fellow Jedi student that he held nothing back, but through the Force Tai perceived a side to Solo that he hid from the others, including himself. Solo listened, but said nothing while Tai expressed his belief that everyone should be themselves.[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13) In Voe, despite being friends, Solo found a rival to push himself against during their training, Voe trying to surpass and beat her fellow Jedi at nearly everything within their training.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7) At one point, he defeated Voe in a sparring match. As their training progressed, Solo suspected that Voe resented him for his power.[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13)

Though he befriended the other Padawans while training with them under Skywalker's watch, Solo also suspected that they viewed him as a symbol of preferential treatment, benefitting from his Skywalker bloodline instead of earning his place in the restored Jedi Order. This belief led Solo to feel like an outcast rather than part of a new generation of Jedi.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7) At some point during his training, Solo would face a group of [IG-RM assassin droids](/wiki/IG-RM_bodyguard_and_enforcer_droid "IG-RM bodyguard and enforcer droid") alongside his uncle.[[48]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_10-48)

#### Exploration and discovery

:   "*I'm glad you came along, Ben.*"  
    "*Yes, Master Skywalker. So am I.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker and Ben Solo[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25)

 [![With Lor San Tekka's help, Solo and Skywalker discovered an ancient outpost of the Jedi Order on distant Elphrona.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Elphrona-TheRiseOfKyloRen2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200108200611) [![With Lor San Tekka's help, Solo and Skywalker discovered an ancient outpost of the Jedi Order on distant Elphrona.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Elphrona-TheRiseOfKyloRen2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200108200611)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Elphrona-TheRiseOfKyloRen2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200108200611) 

With Lor San Tekka's help, Solo and Skywalker discovered an ancient outpost of the Jedi Order on distant Elphrona.

 

Around [19 ABY](/wiki/19_ABY "19 ABY"),[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) Solo accompanied his uncle to uncover knowledge of the Jedi Order.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7) [Lor San Tekka](/wiki/Lor_San_Tekka "Lor San Tekka"), a traveler noted for his expertise on the Jedi Order, informed Skywalker about the discovery of an [ancient Jedi outpost](/wiki/Elphrona_Outpost "Elphrona Outpost") on the planet [Elphrona](/wiki/Elphrona "Elphrona"). Embarking on a [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Elphrona "Mission to Elphrona") to investigate San Tekka's findings, Skywalker brought his apprentice with him, knowing that, like himself, Solo was interested in discovering Jedi artifacts. Along the way, Solo was contacted by Snoke without Skywalker's knowledge. Snoke, having sensed anxiety in Solo, inquired after the boy's state of mind. They conversed telepathically while Skywalker and San Tekka talked about the outpost, noting that it may have dated as far back as the [High Republic Era](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era"), when the Jedi greatly expanded their activity throughout the galaxy.[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25)

Solo digressed about the length of their journey, traveling to the edge between the known galaxy and unexplored space. He believed that his Master would only collect what they found but never use any of it, to which Snoke stated that the Jedi had a history of hoarding knowledge, believing themselves to be masters of the Force. As Solo's unrest grew, he became melancholic at having nothing to do on this mission except to follow Skywalker's lead. Though he expressed admiration for his uncle as a teacher, Solo confided in Snoke his belief that Skywalker was holding him back in his evolution as a Jedi. Snoke told Solo that his Master only saw him as a child, but, in time, he would become aware of his apprentice's true potential.[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25)

 [![Solo, Skywalker, and San Tekka were confronted by the Knights of Ren, a group of dark side warriors who sought to claim the outpost and its treasures for their own gain.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/KnightsOfRenCircleLorLukeBen-TheRiseOfKyloRen2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200108210925) [![Solo, Skywalker, and San Tekka were confronted by the Knights of Ren, a group of dark side warriors who sought to claim the outpost and its treasures for their own gain.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/KnightsOfRenCircleLorLukeBen-TheRiseOfKyloRen2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200108210925)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/57/KnightsOfRenCircleLorLukeBen-TheRiseOfKyloRen2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200108210925) 

Solo, Skywalker, and San Tekka were confronted by the Knights of Ren, a group of dark side warriors who sought to claim the outpost and its treasures for their own gain.

 

Their private conversation was interrupted by Skywalker and San Tekka; as they drew closer to Elphrona, Skywalker talked about how they not only had a chance to gain new insights into the ancient Jedi, but also how the mission could give Solo an opportunity to indulge his fascination with ancient weapons, knowing that his pupil was particularly interested in them. Solo smiled when his Master expressed how pleased he was to have his apprentice by his side, and told Skywalker that he felt the same.[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25)

The outpost that they discovered was well preserved and the entrance intact. Both master and apprentice were impressed by it, though Skywalker warned that they should exercise caution while exploring the outpost, recounting a similar situation that nearly ended with his death in years past. The outpost was a repository of holocrons and other artifacts that Skywalker likened to a treasure trove. Solo had been inspecting a [lightsaber rifle](/wiki/Lightsaber_rifle "Lightsaber rifle") up close when he and his Master grew cold upon sensing the power of the dark side.[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25)

 [![Though the Knights were defeated by Skywalker, the warrior known as Ren sensed the darkness within Solo.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4e/BenLukeAndRen-TheRiseOfKyloRen2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200213222415) [![Though the Knights were defeated by Skywalker, the warrior known as Ren sensed the darkness within Solo.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4e/BenLukeAndRen-TheRiseOfKyloRen2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200213222415)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4e/BenLukeAndRen-TheRiseOfKyloRen2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200213222415) 

Though the Knights were defeated by Skywalker, the warrior known as Ren sensed the darkness within Solo.

 

A group of marauders, dressed in black, had entered the outpost after the two Jedi and their explorer companion. A warrior calling himself "[Ren](/wiki/Ren_(human) "Ren (human)")" spoke on the group's behalf, declaring that the outpost and its contents were claimed by the [Knights of Ren](/wiki/Knights_of_Ren "Knights of Ren"). Rejecting the Knights' claim, Skywalker drew his [green-bladed lightsaber](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker%27s_green_lightsaber "Luke Skywalker's green lightsaber") and introduced himself as the last Jedi, and therefore, the heir to all that belonged to the Order. Solo also activated his [lightsaber](/wiki/Lightsaber "Lightsaber"), but remained out of the ensuing fight, as Skywalker instructed him to protect San Tekka.[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25)

Ren conceded the battle after his Knights were defeated by Skywalker. During the confrontation, however, he sensed that the dark side was strong with Solo. He invited Solo to seek out the Knights in the future, offering to teach the young apprentice about aspects of the Force contrary to Jedi teachings.[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25)

#### A teacher in the making

:   "*He's going to make a fine Jedi one day, Luke. And learning the responsibilities of the temple while his Master is away will do him a world of good.*"
:   ―Lor San Tekka, to Luke Skywalker, referring to Ben Solo[[41]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-41)

 [![Solo, though still a Padawan, took on greater responsibilities that included assisting Skywalker's other apprentices with their Jedi training.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/BenVsVoeTraining-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.png/revision/latest?cb=20221009170829) [![Solo, though still a Padawan, took on greater responsibilities that included assisting Skywalker's other apprentices with their Jedi training.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/BenVsVoeTraining-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20221009170829)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/BenVsVoeTraining-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.png/revision/latest?cb=20221009170829) 

Solo, though still a Padawan, took on greater responsibilities that included assisting Skywalker's other apprentices with their Jedi training.

 

Solo was one of Skywalker's senior pupils by the time he became a teenager; as such, he was entrusted with some of his Master's responsibilities, such as the supervision of training sessions in which the younger students practiced with [training lightsabers](/wiki/Training_lightsaber "Training lightsaber").[[41]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-41) In [21 ABY](/wiki/21_ABY "21 ABY"),[[49]](#cite_note-21_ABY-49) Lor San Tekka visited the temple on Ossus to speak with Skywalker. Solo went to [Skywalker's hut](/wiki/Luke%27s_hut_(Ossus) "Luke's hut (Ossus)") to inform him of San Tekka's arrival, inadvertently interrupting Skywalker's meditation. Embarrassed at his intrusion, Solo accidentally referred to Skywalker as uncle instead of Master. Having been lectured by Skywalker on the need to exercise discipline and control, Solo composed himself and addressed Skywalker by his formal title as he informed him about their visitor. After Skywalker welcomed his old friend to the temple, San Tekka addressed Solo directly to inquire on the progress of his training. Solo's efforts at formality amused his Master, who assured San Tekka that Solo was a better student than he could have hoped for.[[41]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-41)

Skywalker told Solo to return to his studies while he and San Tekka spoke in private. Returning to the temple grounds, Solo replaced the [Twi'lek](/wiki/Twi%27lek "Twi'lek") [Enyo](/wiki/Enyo "Enyo") as an [instructor](/wiki/Instructor "Instructor") for a class of younglings who were exercising with [training lightsabers](/wiki/Training_lightsaber "Training lightsaber"). He ended the training session after his Master signaled him to return to his hut. San Tekka had invited Skywalker to travel with him to an [archeological](/wiki/Archaeology "Archaeology") site on [Yoturba](/wiki/Yoturba "Yoturba"), and also noted that Solo could benefit from his Master's absence by taking on more responsibilities at the temple.[[41]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-41)

#### A future leader of the Jedi Order

:   "*Considering… Well, your family, your skill in the Force, and that you'll be one of the first students to complete your training… It seems likely that you could hold a position of leadership in the Jedi Order to come.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker, to Ben Solo[[31]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_50-31)

 [![By passing on his experience to Solo, Skywalker hoped to guide his nephew on the path to becoming a true Knight of the Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1c/MasterAndApprentice-2020StarWars50.png/revision/latest?cb=20250122064428) [![By passing on his experience to Solo, Skywalker hoped to guide his nephew on the path to becoming a true Knight of the Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1c/MasterAndApprentice-2020StarWars50.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250122064428)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1c/MasterAndApprentice-2020StarWars50.png/revision/latest?cb=20250122064428) 

By passing on his experience to Solo, Skywalker hoped to guide his nephew on the path to becoming a true Knight of the Jedi Order.

 

During his training on Ossus, Solo was asked by his Master to accompany him on a walk through the temple grounds. At the time, Solo was practicing his skills in telekinesis, using the Force to levitate several objects such as his lightsaber, his [calligraphy set](/wiki/Ben_Solo%27s_calligraphy_set "Ben Solo's calligraphy set"), and a few [books](/wiki/Book "Book") around him inside [his hut](/wiki/Ben_Solo%27s_hut "Ben Solo's hut"). As they walked, Skywalker told Solo that he was almost ready to undergo the [Jedi Trials](/wiki/Jedi_Trials "Jedi Trials"), the completion of which would mark the end of their time together as Master and apprentice. According to Skywalker, Solo would no longer have to listen to a master since he would be free to make his own decisions as a fully-trained Jedi Knight. In addition, Skywalker acknowledged Solo's potential to become a future leader in the Jedi Order that he was working to restore, given his nephew's status as a Skywalker, his strength in the Force, and the fact that he stood poised to be among the first in his generation to complete his instruction in the Jedi arts. Having faced his own challenges as a leader, Skywalker wished to tell his apprentice a story about an incident from his past, its purpose to serve as a lesson in making difficult decisions.[[31]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_50-31)

Skywalker's story centered on his discovery and subsequent use of the [Grim Rose](/wiki/Grim_Rose "Grim Rose"), an ancient weapon that he discovered upon returning to the [Living Sea](/wiki/Living_Sea "Living Sea") on the planet [Gazian](/wiki/Gazian "Gazian"). Solo learned that Skywalker had considered using the Grim Rose to assassinate Emperor Palpatine; using a sample of Palpatine's blood, the weapon could be used to target and kill the Emperor. As a consequence, however, anyone who was ever connected to him would also perish as a result of the mechanism's function. Solo theorized that the weapon had the capacity to destroy the Sith. Being aware of Vader's connection to Palpatine, Solo was certain that the weapon would have scanned Vader as well, ultimately resulting in the deaths of both Sith Lords. Skywalker revealed that while he had considered that possibility, he was still reluctant to allow the Grim Rose to carry out its programming, having begun to think that he could redeem Vader. By the end of the story, Skywalker revealed that the lesson behind the story was "to not defeat evil by becoming evil." Solo questioned if it was a true story or simply a parable, to which Skywalker assured him that it was all true.[[31]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_50-31)

### Fall to the dark side

#### Shattering revelation

:   "*Senator Casterfo's accusation is true. My father was Darth Vader.*"
:   ―Leia Organa[[11]](#cite_note-Bloodline-11)

 [![By his early twenties, Solo was still an apprentice under his uncle, Luke Skywalker, when he learned about the darkest secret of his family in the form of Darth Vader.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/40/Bloodline-LiarPoster.png/revision/latest?cb=20250225004030) [![By his early twenties, Solo was still an apprentice under his uncle, Luke Skywalker, when he learned about the darkest secret of his family in the form of Darth Vader.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/40/Bloodline-LiarPoster.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250225004030)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/40/Bloodline-LiarPoster.png/revision/latest?cb=20250225004030) 

By his early twenties, Solo was still an apprentice under his uncle, Luke Skywalker, when he learned about the darkest secret of his family in the form of Darth Vader.

 

When the Skywalker family's secret lineage was revealed[[11]](#cite_note-Bloodline-11) in [28 ABY](/wiki/28_ABY "28 ABY"),[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) Solo was twenty-three years old and still in the care of his uncle as he traversed the path toward becoming a Jedi Knight.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7) Elsewhere in the galaxy, the truth about the parentage of Solo's mother was revealed by Organa's political enemies in the [New Republic Senate](/wiki/New_Republic_Senate "New Republic Senate"). Organa had yet to tell her son about Darth Vader and she worried about how he would react after finding out about it in such a public way.[[11]](#cite_note-Bloodline-11) To honor his sister's wishes, Luke Skywalker had likewise avoided to provide Solo an honest account of Vader's redemption. Just as Organa expected, upon becoming aware of the truth across the [HoloNet](/wiki/HoloNet "HoloNet"), Solo was shocked; the revelation felt like a betrayal for him and crushed the image he had of Anakin Skywalker by realizing that his parents and uncle never shared the truth with him despite knowing it for decades, leaving him to discover the Skywalker family's most carefully guarded secret along with the rest of the galaxy. Solo also believed that his family, by concealing his ancestry from him, justified the dark impulses that he suppressed throughout his young life. Organa sent a tearful and desperate message to her son soon after the news broke, but it was too late to prevent Solo's disillusionment with his family.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7)

 [![Snoke believed that Ben Solo was a focal point between the light and the dark side of the Force.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2c/TheRiseOfKyloRen2_MuirVariantArt.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200101011113) [![Snoke believed that Ben Solo was a focal point between the light and the dark side of the Force.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2c/TheRiseOfKyloRen2_MuirVariantArt.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20200101011113)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2c/TheRiseOfKyloRen2_MuirVariantArt.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200101011113) 

Snoke believed that Ben Solo was a focal point between the light and the dark side of the Force.

 

Snoke saw Solo as a focal point between the light side and the dark side—an ideal embodiment of a Force warrior—and wanted to take him as an apprentice of his own.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) Though his origins were a mystery even to his own subordinates,[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) Snoke was created by the phantom Emperor Darth Sidious[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) and designed by the [Sith Eternal](/wiki/Sith_Eternal "Sith Eternal") [cultists](/wiki/Sith_cultist "Sith cultist") to mold Solo into an heir worthy of inheriting the legacy of the Sith.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5)

Snoke utilized the anger Solo felt at this revelation to cap off his decade long manipulations, promising Solo with his guidance and the latter's power, he would become a figure that would even surpass his grandfather, Darth Vader. Solo felt like he no longer had to compete with his family or the Jedi who came before him anymore, but instead surpass them and live up to the power of his grandfather, feeding into Snoke's doctrine to turn the young man into a weapon of the dark side.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7)

Unbeknownst to Solo, his descent to the dark side was part of Darth Sidious' plan to turn him against the new Jedi Order. The reborn Sith Lord had been using Snoke as a proxy to groom Solo for his future as Vader's heir, believing that his inner conflict made him an easily malleable, but worthy apprentice. Although Solo would not become a true Sith, his raw strength with the Force made him powerful with the dark side nonetheless.[[36]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-36)

#### A fateful night

:   "*He would bring destruction, pain, death, and the end of everything I love because of what he will become. And for the briefest moment of pure instinct, I thought I could stop it. It passed like a fleeting shadow. And I was left with shame and with consequence. And the last thing I saw were the eyes of a frightened boy whose master had failed him.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker, about Ben Solo[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

 [![Skywalker had a premonition that his nephew would herald death, destruction, and the end of everything he loved.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Wakey_wakey_Ben.png/revision/latest?cb=20180510222951) [![Skywalker had a premonition that his nephew would herald death, destruction, and the end of everything he loved.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Wakey_wakey_Ben.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/258?cb=20180510222951)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1e/Wakey_wakey_Ben.png/revision/latest?cb=20180510222951) 

Skywalker had a premonition that his nephew would herald death, destruction, and the end of everything he loved.

 

Skywalker eventually became aware of the darkness growing in his nephew as he observed glimpses during Solo's training. He went to his nephew's bedroom one evening to confront him, and found him asleep. Standing over his sleeping student, Skywalker reached out and sensed that Solo had already turned through Snoke's influence, and saw the death and destruction Solo would someday bring to everything Skywalker loved. The immediacy and severity of the threat caused the Jedi Master to instinctively draw his lightsaber, intending for a brief moment to kill his apprentice to prevent his vision from coming to pass, but the impulse vanished in an instant. Skywalker was immediately filled with shame and saw Solo had awakened to see his uncle standing over him with his lightsaber raised. Solo, unaware of the brevity of Skywalker's instinct, witnessed it long enough to fear for his life and realized what his uncle had seen in his mind. He panicked and drew his own lightsaber to strike his uncle first, but Skywalker quickly blocked his nephew's killing blow. In an act of desperation, Solo used the Force to collapse the entire hut on his master.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

 [![Driven by anger and confusion, Solo destroyed the Jedi temple along with most of his fellow students.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/88/DestructionOfTheJediTemple-TheRiseOfKyloRen1.png/revision/latest?cb=20191224031329) [![Driven by anger and confusion, Solo destroyed the Jedi temple along with most of his fellow students.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/88/DestructionOfTheJediTemple-TheRiseOfKyloRen1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191224031329)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/88/DestructionOfTheJediTemple-TheRiseOfKyloRen1.png/revision/latest?cb=20191224031329) 

Driven by anger and confusion, Solo destroyed the Jedi temple along with most of his fellow students.

 

Solo emerged from the ruins believing he had killed Skywalker, and he raged in anger and confusion over why his uncle had attacked him. The night sky was clear as Solo shouted questions and pointed his ignited lightsaber at the [Jedi temple](/wiki/Jedi_temple "Jedi temple"). As his eyes changed to constricted pupils and irises clouded with red, Solo briefly[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47) surrendered to the dark side and summoned a [storm](/wiki/Force_power "Force power") that could [destroy the temple](/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Jedi_Temple "Destruction of the Jedi Temple").[[51]](#cite_note-Encyclopedia:_Kylo-51) He then noticed the red storm clouds[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47) he had summoned[[51]](#cite_note-Encyclopedia:_Kylo-51) appear above the temple, which rained lightning upon the temple and set the buildings [ablaze](/wiki/Fire "Fire").[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47)

The fire that Solo started when he lashed out destroyed most of the students along with the temple,[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5)[[38]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-38) which collapsed[[43]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-43) and burned to the ground.[[42]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-42) The lightning strike caused an explosion that knocked back Solo and scattered debris and the bodies of dead students. When Solo attempted to run inside the burning temple, he was thrown back by another explosion. He surveyed the death and destruction around him and, horrified, said that he never wanted this. However, a voice inside of Solo's head told him that the fault lay not with himself, but rather with Skywalker and the Jedi.[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47) He assumed that a [holocron](/wiki/Holocron "Holocron") containing a message from the former Jedi [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master"), [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda"), was destroyed in the blaze.[[52]](#cite_note-Galactic_Starcruiser-52)

#### A dark path

:   "*The Knights of Ren could be your first step on that path. They always seek powerful people to join their ranks. But be warned… the price of admission is steep.*"
:   ―Snoke, to Ben Solo[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25)

 [![Solo, who felt that his master had betrayed him, renounced the Jedi Order and sought a new path under Snoke's guidance.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/TaiConfrontsBenSolo-TheRiseOfKyloRen1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191231084312) [![Solo, who felt that his master had betrayed him, renounced the Jedi Order and sought a new path under Snoke's guidance.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/TaiConfrontsBenSolo-TheRiseOfKyloRen1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191231084312)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/TaiConfrontsBenSolo-TheRiseOfKyloRen1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191231084312) 

Solo, who felt that his master had betrayed him, renounced the Jedi Order and sought a new path under Snoke's guidance.

 

Returning from an off-world mission, the Jedi students Hennix, Tai and Voe confronted Solo and questioned his involvement in the temple's demise. Solo dejectedly informed them about Skywalker's actions and responded angrily when he assumed Voe was questioning his power in comparison to their master's. Solo told them the temple was a lie that was now over. As Solo turned to leave, the apprentices brandished their lightsabers at him, causing Solo to fight back with his [Force powers](/wiki/Force_power "Force power"), injuring Hennix. Defeating them, he boarded his starship [*Grimtaash*](/wiki/Grimtaash_(starship) "Grimtaash (starship)"), whilst the trio followed in their own spacecraft, the *[Verity](/wiki/Verity "Verity")*. Though Solo had the opportunity to kill them, he only incapacitated their ship before making his escape, and eventually arrived at [Amaxine space station](/wiki/Amaxine_Space_Station "Amaxine Space Station") where Solo met with Snoke.[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47)

 [![Snoke encouraged Solo to adopt a new name, one that he would be known by throughout the galaxy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/TheFutureKyloRen-RiseOfKyloRen2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200217035230) [![Snoke encouraged Solo to adopt a new name, one that he would be known by throughout the galaxy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/TheFutureKyloRen-RiseOfKyloRen2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200217035230)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/TheFutureKyloRen-RiseOfKyloRen2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200217035230) 

Snoke encouraged Solo to adopt a new name, one that he would be known by throughout the galaxy.

 

Having rejected his future as a Jedi, Solo expressed interest in learning what he could from the Knights of Ren. Snoke not only supported Solo's new path, but also encouraged the fallen Jedi to take the opportunity of forging his own identity absent of Skywalker's influence. Solo had long felt the pressure of living up to the legends he was named after, and therefore wished to be rid of his given name as well as his father's surname. Even before he departed to search for the Knights of Ren, Solo began entertaining the idea of using a name he coined as a child. Snoke approved, believing that the new name represented Solo's true nature and would become known to the entire galaxy one day. Returning to the place where he last saw the Knights, Solo made contact with Ren by using the latter's [helmet](/wiki/Helmet "Helmet") as a direct line of communication, and was told to seek them out on [Varnak](/wiki/Varnak "Varnak") in the [Mid Rim](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories"). By then, the other Jedi students had caught up to Solo, intending to prevent him from going any further down the path of the dark side.[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25)

#### Confrontation on Elphrona

:   "*I went back there to see if I could find a path to you and the other Knights, but I was followed somehow. By three* Jedi*. Students of Luke Skywalker.* […] *And the temple's gone. Burned. I destroyed it. That's why the other students came after me. To kill me.*"
:   ―Ben Solo, to Ren[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13)

 [![Seeking the Knights of Ren, Solo returned to Elphrona where he was confronted by a trio of Jedi apprentices.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/VoeAttacksBenSolo-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220510022616) [![Seeking the Knights of Ren, Solo returned to Elphrona where he was confronted by a trio of Jedi apprentices.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/VoeAttacksBenSolo-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220510022616)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/VoeAttacksBenSolo-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220510022616) 

Seeking the Knights of Ren, Solo returned to Elphrona where he was confronted by a trio of Jedi apprentices.

 

The [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Elphrona "Battle of Elphrona") moved outside of the outpost. Solo simultaneously parried Voe and Hennix's lightsabers, and Tai attempted a mental probe with the Force before Solo telekinetically threw him against a wall. Leaping high into the air, Solo told the other students to let him go. Voe refused to end their pursuit and followed him up a steep rock face, saying he had to face justice for betraying the Jedi, especially their master, and becoming a murderer. Solo reacted with fury and used the Force to throw her over the cliff. As Hennix witnessed the attempted murder, he scaled the rocks without seeing that Solo had halted Voe's descent and struggled to keep her suspended. Hennix, believing he was avenging Voe, called Solo a monster and threw his lightsaber. Reacting instinctively, Solo dropped Voe and deflected Hennix's blade back towards its owner before refocusing his attention on Voe. She was saved when Tai slowed her fall before she landed on him, but Hennix was unable to defend himself when his own lightsaber struck and killed him.[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13)

Voe identified Hennix's scream and told Tai they had to stop Solo. After descending the cliff, Solo told the pair to get inside the outpost. Tai asked what had happened to Hennix, but Solo told them it did not matter. Before Voe and Tai could recover, Solo seized them both with the Force. He used the Force to throw them into the outpost and collapsed the entrance to trap them inside.[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13)

#### Trials of Knighthood

:   "*But Snoke vouched for you, and you're strong in the shadow, and that's not nothing. Let's spend some time, see if you like us, see if we like you. Maybe you'll find that good death after all.*"
:   ―Ren, to Ben Solo[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13)

 [![After defeating the Jedi on Elphrona, Solo tracked the Knights of Ren to the planet Varnak.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8f/ElphronaOutpostDestruction-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200213072502) [![After defeating the Jedi on Elphrona, Solo tracked the Knights of Ren to the planet Varnak.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8f/ElphronaOutpostDestruction-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200213072502)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8f/ElphronaOutpostDestruction-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200213072502) 

After defeating the Jedi on Elphrona, Solo tracked the Knights of Ren to the planet Varnak.

 

With the Jedi subdued, Solo completed his journey to Varnak, where he found Ren and the other Knights lounging in a [cantina](/wiki/Cantina "Cantina"). Knowing that Snoke had sent Solo to them, Ren informed the young Jedi that he would have to offer them a sacrifice before he could join their ranks. As with Snoke, Ren was doubtful that Skywalker died by Solo's hand, although Solo confirmed that at this point he was responsible for the destruction of the temple and deaths of other Jedi. Ren, however, needed to know if the Jedi that Solo killed held any significance to him, so he asked Solo to recount the details of his confrontation with Tai, Hennix, and Voe. As Solo began telling his story, his thoughts drifted to years past when he was younger—a child surrounded by other young students whom Skywalker had taken under his wing.[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13)

Solo recounted his experiences with the three Jedi who followed him to Elphrona, beginning with Voe. He remembered how she treated everything between them as a competition, throughout their time together as Skywalker's apprentices. For Solo, however, nothing with Voe was a contest as he outperformed her in every aspect of their training, despite all of Voe's attempts to reach the level of Solo's skill. Through Solo's recollection of her, Ren deduced that Voe was focused on his strength, whereas Hennix concentrated more on solving the mysteries of the Force as though it were a puzzle. Solo remembered Hennix for his humor and intelligence, but was more cryptic about Tai. Though Solo would not speak of him in detail to Ren, he remembered the way Tai encouraged him to be himself despite the pressure of being who he was—the scion of a legendary family.[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13)

Having learned enough about the other students of Skywalker, Ren directed Solo to return to the more recent past regarding his confrontation with the trio that pursued him in the wake of the temple's destruction. Solo took responsibility for Hennix's death, telling Ren that he killed his fellow Jedi. Ren, however, remained skeptical as were the other Knights. Solo protested, believing he met their qualifications, and although Ren agreed that Hennix was technically a death caused by Solo, he knew that the young fallen Jedi was conflicted about it. Nevertheless, Ren allowed Solo to accompany the Knights, at least for the time being, given that he was strong with the dark side as well as the fact that Snoke had already vouched for him. Ren also suspected that, in the course of Solo's journey with the Knights, the former Jedi would eventually make a sacrifice that was worthy of the Knights of Ren.[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13)

 [![Though conflicted over his choices, Solo's descent into darkness continued as he began traveling with the Knights of Ren.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/KyloRenBetaTestVersion-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200213221602) [![Though conflicted over his choices, Solo's descent into darkness continued as he began traveling with the Knights of Ren.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/KyloRenBetaTestVersion-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200213221602)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/KyloRenBetaTestVersion-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200213221602) 

Though conflicted over his choices, Solo's descent into darkness continued as he began traveling with the Knights of Ren.
