As far as Ren was concerned, Solo's appearance as a Jedi made him unsuitable to be seen in the company of the Knights. As such, Solo was made to set aside his tattered [Jedi robes](/wiki/Jedi_apparel "Jedi apparel") for a set of black clothes. Once dressed in his new attire, Solo was told by Ren that they would now depart from Vanrak and find something to burn.[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13)

By then, Tai and Voe had managed to create an opening in the destroyed entrance of the Jedi outpost. Tai, having seen glimpses in Solo's mind, knew that his former peer was seeking to join the Knights, believing his truth path was with the dark side warriors. His faith in Solo began to erode upon discovering the dead body of Hennix, whose lightsaber was claimed by Voe as a replacement for her weapon, which was destroyed during her battle with Solo.[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13)

#### The fall of Ben Solo

:   "*Using Snoke as my proxy, I reached into the boy's mind, influencing his choices. I turned him against the new Jedi Order that was rising in my absence. I severed his bonds to his family and broke his ties to the light. Once reborn as Kylo Ren, he was mine to control.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious[[36]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-36)

 [![The Knights of Ren acknowledged Solo as their new master for having killed Ren in single combat.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/31/KnightsOfRenAcceptBen-TheRiseOfKyloRen4.png/revision/latest?cb=20200428041008) [![The Knights of Ren acknowledged Solo as their new master for having killed Ren in single combat.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/31/KnightsOfRenAcceptBen-TheRiseOfKyloRen4.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200428041008)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/31/KnightsOfRenAcceptBen-TheRiseOfKyloRen4.png/revision/latest?cb=20200428041008) 

The Knights of Ren acknowledged Solo as their new master for having killed Ren in single combat.

 

Journeying to the [Minemoon](/wiki/Minemoon "Minemoon") of [Mimban](/wiki/Mimban "Mimban") in the Mid Rim, the Knights of Ren, along with Ben Solo, found themselves amidst [Mimbanese](/wiki/Mimbanese "Mimbanese") [miners](/wiki/Miner "Miner"). Trailed by the Jedi Tai and Voe, Solo confronted the former as the latter repelled the Knights' attack on the Mimbanese. Tai attempted once again to bring Solo back into the light, but before Solo could respond, Ren used the Force to snap Tai's neck. Ren taunted Solo, claiming that Snoke was wrong about him and that he could never survive against someone who actually wanted him dead. They engaged in a lightsaber duel, and as Solo fell towards the dark side, a storm of lightning accompanied him. Those connected to him across the galaxy were able to feel the disturbance in the Force, including Solo's mother, Organa; Snoke; Darth Sidious; and his dyad counterpart, Rey. After successfully killing Ren and taking control of his knights, Solo returned to face Voe, snatched Voe's weapon, and killed her by igniting Ren's lightsaber through her chest.[[9]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_4-9)

 [![Although Solo succeeded in bleeding his lightsaber's kyber crystal, he fractured it in the process.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1f/KyloBleedsCrystal-TheRiseOfKyloRen4.png/revision/latest?cb=20200315181940) [![Although Solo succeeded in bleeding his lightsaber's kyber crystal, he fractured it in the process.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1f/KyloBleedsCrystal-TheRiseOfKyloRen4.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200315181940)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1f/KyloBleedsCrystal-TheRiseOfKyloRen4.png/revision/latest?cb=20200315181940) 

Although Solo succeeded in bleeding his lightsaber's kyber crystal, he fractured it in the process.

 

Solo then returned to the *Night Buzzard* and retreated to a workbench within to modify his lightsaber. Deeply frustrated with his family's expectations of himself, Solo used the [kyber crystal](/wiki/Kyber_crystal "Kyber crystal") from his saber to [bleed](/wiki/Bleeding "Bleeding") his hatred for the legacy of his family into it, renouncing his origins to the distant Darth Sidious and Snoke's approval. His eyes briefly turning yellow and red, the [crystal](/wiki/Crystal "Crystal") cracked in its master's grip with a surge of fiery energy.[[9]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_4-9)

Afterward, he had to modify his weapon to contain the power of the broken crystal, which produced a red blade with an unstable and fiery appearance,[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) a design after the weapon of an ancient Sith Lord, Darth Atrius.[[36]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-36) After bleeding his kyber crystal and modifying his weapon, the newly-turned dark side warrior brandished his [crossguard lightsaber](/wiki/Crossguard_lightsaber "Crossguard lightsaber") and took on the [name](/wiki/Ren "Ren") Kylo Ren.[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2)

#### The rise of Kylo Ren

:   "*Now you will be who you are. Who you were always meant to be.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious, to Ben Solo[[9]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_4-9)

 [![Kylo Ren was the master of the Knights of Ren and the apprentice of Supreme Leader Snoke.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/Knights_of_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20160416230650) [![Kylo Ren was the master of the Knights of Ren and the apprentice of Supreme Leader Snoke.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/Knights_of_Ren.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20160416230650)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/Knights_of_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20160416230650) 

Kylo Ren was the master of the Knights of Ren and the apprentice of Supreme Leader Snoke.

 

Kylo Ren sacrificed everything in his pursuit of power through the dark side, choosing to isolate himself from the people he loved as Ben Solo.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) In addition to becoming a champion of the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order"),[[4]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_DB-4) the Empire's successor that Snoke ruled as [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader"),[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) Ren gained the title master of the Knights of Ren,[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) having inherited his predecessor's command with Snoke's blessing.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) Through his new master's training, Solo became nothing more than a distant memory in the life of Ren. He was the Supreme Leader's most gifted apprentice as well as the embodiment of a new generation of dark side warriors that emerged to fill the void left by the fall of the Sith,[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) which became extinct with the deaths of Sidious and Vader as the last [Sith Master](/wiki/Sith_Master "Sith Master") and [Sith apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice") under the [Rule of Two](/wiki/Rule_of_Two "Rule of Two").[[43]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-43) During his training, Snoke warned Ren that, as his dark side powers grew, an equal of the light side—whom Snoke believed would be Skywalker but later reasoned was Rey—would arise to challenge him.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

Unbeknownst to Ren, Skywalker survived but was also forever changed upon witnessing the destruction of the Jedi Order by his nephew.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) Ren's actions sent shock waves through his family. With his Jedi temple destroyed, Skywalker vanished into exile. Those closest to him believed that he went in search of the [first Jedi Temple](/wiki/First_Jedi_Temple "First Jedi Temple"),[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) which he eventually discovered on the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Ahch-To](/wiki/Ahch-To "Ahch-To").[[53]](#cite_note-Rey's_Story-53) Organa and Solo separated, with Solo returning to smuggling with Chewbacca. Organa returned to a life of war,[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) forming a band of [soldiers](/wiki/Soldier "Soldier") known as the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance") when the New Republic Senate refused to take the emerging threat of the First Order seriously.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) Though Solo believed there was too much of Darth Vader in Ben and that they lost their son forever, Organa never gave up hope that there was still good in him.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

By decree of the Supreme Leader, Ren's true name could never be spoken. Ren sought to put his past behind him, become immune to the temptations of the light, and claim his birthright by ruling the weaker beings of the galaxy. He typically wore a [combat helmet](/wiki/Kylo_Ren%27s_helmet "Kylo Ren's helmet"), patterned after the battle gear of the Knights of Ren, in order to conceal his identity and give him a more intimidating presence. This helmet also contained a vocal modifier, which lowered the pitch of Ren's voice considerably. Ren's actions at Skywalker's temple earned him the nickname "Jedi Killer," a name whispered amongst the First Order ranks who knew Ren had prevented the return of the Jedi Order.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) No longer a Jedi but neither a Sith, Ren strove to harness the pain of his emotional conflict in order to fuel his extraordinary powers and destroy the last traces of the Jedi tradition.[[54]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_Bio_Gallery-54)

 [![The legacy of Darth Vader would cast a dark shadow over the life of his only grandchild.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/85/HelmetWarrantyVoided-TFAT2.png/revision/latest?cb=20170907154521) [![The legacy of Darth Vader would cast a dark shadow over the life of his only grandchild.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/85/HelmetWarrantyVoided-TFAT2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170907154521)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/85/HelmetWarrantyVoided-TFAT2.png/revision/latest?cb=20170907154521) 

The legacy of Darth Vader would cast a dark shadow over the life of his only grandchild.

 

Ren's desire to put the light side behind him was a key part of how he viewed his heritage. He came to idolize Darth Vader and kept his grandfather's [burned helmet](/wiki/Darth_Vader%27s_armor "Darth Vader's armor") as a shrine to the legacy of the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith"),[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) hoping to destroy the last Jedi as Vader had once intended and stamp out the last remnants of the light side of the Force.[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39) Though Skywalker had redeemed Vader during the Battle of Endor—allowing his father, Anakin to fulfill the ancient prophecy of the [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One")[[42]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-42)—Ren and Snoke both believed that Darth Vader was Anakin's true self and that his redemption had simply been a single yet fatal error in an otherwise important life.[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39) Ren regarded Darth Vader as his real grandfather and wished to emulate him. While he later realized he had never managed to contact the Sith Lord he hoped to make proud,[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) Ren, at this time, believed that he had made contact with the [spirit](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit") of his grandfather at least once; he later beseeched Vader's helmet to "show [him] *again*, the power of the darkness."[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

Beyond becoming the regime's greatest warrior,[[55]](#cite_note-TFA_Sticker-55) Ren became an influential member of the First Order's power structure by virtue of his position as Supreme Leader Snoke's apprentice and enforcer, mirroring his grandfather's status in Sidious' Empire. Though he had direct access to the Supreme Leader and could command [military](/wiki/First_Order_military "First Order military") officers, he existed outside of the official military command structure. This led to some tension with the First Order's upper ranks, who contended with him despite being wary that his agenda trumped military objectives. This arrangement deliberately mirrored the Galactic Empire's relationship with Darth Vader, who existed outside of the formal military hierarchy but could nonetheless command the [Imperial Military](/wiki/Imperial_Military "Imperial Military") in his own objectives. This tension was particularly palpable with General [Armitage Hux](/wiki/Armitage_Hux "Armitage Hux"), the commander of [Starkiller Base](/wiki/Starkiller_Base "Starkiller Base"), the First Order [superweapon](/wiki/Superweapon "Superweapon") capable of destroying entire [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system"). Ren, who was part of an unofficial Starkiller Base command triumvirate with Hux and [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") [Phasma](/wiki/Phasma "Phasma") of the First Order military, had little regard for Hux as a warrior.; Hux's military experience was mostly theoretical and based on simulated but nonetheless respected battlefield scenarios.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50)

Hux, likewise, was a man of science and had little understanding of Ren's mystical ways. Both vied for the attention of the Supreme Leader.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) Over time Ren's reputation came to rival that of Hux and Phasma, both of whom were noted among the First Order ranks for their power and influence. Nevertheless, soldiers such as Captain [Cardinal](/wiki/Archex "Archex") held Ren in high regard, believing he would be the one to lead the First Order to victory.[[56]](#cite_note-Phasma-56) However, although he was highly regarded by some figures of the First Order command, others were less impressed with the young Knight of Ren. [Agent](/wiki/Agent "Agent") [Terex](/wiki/Terex "Terex"), an officer of the [First Order's security branch](/wiki/First_Order_Security_Bureau "First Order Security Bureau"), was disdainfully dismissive of Ren's attempt to emulate Darth Vader, whom he had met and considered a truly terrifying figure.[[57]](#cite_note-Poe_Dameron_11-57)

### Dark side training

#### Apprentice of Snoke

:   "*Use your fear. Let it crystallize into anger. Turn that anger into* power*.*"
:   ―Snoke, to Kylo Ren[[58]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Snoke-58)

 [![Snoke trained Ren to turn his fear into anger, and his anger into power.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ec/Rarlech-AORSnoke1.png/revision/latest?cb=20240424104530) [![Snoke trained Ren to turn his fear into anger, and his anger into power.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ec/Rarlech-AORSnoke1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240424104530)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ec/Rarlech-AORSnoke1.png/revision/latest?cb=20240424104530) 

Snoke trained Ren to turn his fear into anger, and his anger into power.

 

Sometime later, Snoke took Ren to a [rocky planet](/wiki/Unidentified_planet_(Rarlech_system) "Unidentified planet (Rarlech system)") in the [Rarlech system](/wiki/Rarlech_system "Rarlech system"). As the two stood at the edge of a cliff, Snoke turned to Ren and asked if he was afraid. Ren replied by saying he wasn't. Snoke, using the Force, pushed Ren off the cliff and held him in the air. He proceeded to say that he knew Ren was afraid, as he should have been because he had no control. Instead, Ren was obfuscated and powerless. Snoke continued by saying that feeling that was good. Powerless men turned to anger and could lash out blindly with rage. But powerful ones can harness their anger and use it strike. Either they strike or fall. Snoke then released Ren, letting him fall. He told Ren to use the fear in him, turn it into anger, and make that anger become power. Following the guidance of Snoke, Ren was able to use the Force to survive the fall. He then asked Snoke if he would have rescued him if he wasn't able to save himself. Snoke answered by saying that Ren's former master, Luke Skywalker would have, but in doing so would hinder Ren's progress. Snoke wanted Ren to find his true power and potential if the latter wished to rule the galaxy alongside him.[[58]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Snoke-58)

After leaving the rocky world, the duo arrived on [Dagobah](/wiki/Dagobah "Dagobah"). As they prepared to depart from the shuttle, Ren was about to bring his helmet when Snoke ordered him to leave it behind. Ren tried to tell Snoke that he wanted to bring it, but the incensed Supreme Leader slapped him in the face, drawing blood, and once again ordered Ren to leave it, telling him that he couldn't pretend to be Vader where they were going.[[58]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Snoke-58)

#### The Cave of Evil

:   "*I feel cold, death, and more.*"  
    "*The cave is power. And darkness. And you will enter.*"  
    "*What's in there?*"  
    "*Only what you've been too weak to bury. Or you can run away, if you'd like.*"
:   ―Snoke and Kylo Ren[[58]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Snoke-58)

 [![Kylo Ren battled a vision of Luke Skywalker in the Cave of Evil.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/KyloVsVisionLuke-AORSnoke1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190912203652) [![Kylo Ren battled a vision of Luke Skywalker in the Cave of Evil.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/KyloVsVisionLuke-AORSnoke1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20190912203652)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/KyloVsVisionLuke-AORSnoke1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190912203652) 

Kylo Ren battled a vision of Luke Skywalker in the Cave of Evil.

 

Following the incident on board their shuttle, Snoke and Ren proceeded towards the [Cave of Evil](/wiki/Cave_of_Evil "Cave of Evil") on Dagobah. Ren commented that he could still sense his uncle from his time on Dagobah training with [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda"). Snoke nodded and told Ren that one of the most formidable Jedi began his training here. Ren then asked Snoke why he spoke of Skywalker with respect. Snoke said that Skywalker had earned his respect and fear. Ren told Snoke that Skywalker was weak. Snoke replied that Skywalker was not weak, merely misguided. If Snoke had had Skywalker by his side, the galaxy would have belonged to him a lot earlier. They then went to the cave, from which Ren could sense a coldness radiating, along with death and other things. Snoke explained that was where all the fears Ren had been too weak to bury resided. He could go in or run away. But Ren's mind was already made up. He ventured in.[[58]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Snoke-58)

Once inside, Ren had a vision of his uncle Luke, saying that he didn't want to fight Ren. Ren told him that he did not care and activated his lightsaber. Snoke sensed the decision Ren had made and told him that it was good and that Skywalker would have murdered him in his sleep because he feared Ren and how formidable he'd become. As the two dueled, Snoke advised Ren to use his hatred, rise above what was holding him back, and strike against the light within him. Ren did so and impaled the vision of Luke. Thinking he was finished, Ren told Snoke that he was done. But Snoke told him that the vision had just started.[[58]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Snoke-58)

 [![Despite his anger and rage, Ben Solo could not bring himself to strike down the apparitions of his parents, Han Solo and Leia Organa.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b7/BenSoloAndParents-AORSnoke1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191101133331) [![Despite his anger and rage, Ben Solo could not bring himself to strike down the apparitions of his parents, Han Solo and Leia Organa.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b7/BenSoloAndParents-AORSnoke1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20191101133331)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b7/BenSoloAndParents-AORSnoke1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191101133331) 

Despite his anger and rage, Ben Solo could not bring himself to strike down the apparitions of his parents, Han Solo and Leia Organa.

 

Ren then caught sight of his parents, begging him to quit his actions. He tried to kill the light within him by saying that Ben wasn't his name, but Leia insisted it was and that he was loved. Outside the cave, Snoke could sense the conflict within Ren, but then he sensed Ren ignite his lightsaber. He told Ren to kill the connection and snuff it out. But, in the cave, Ren hadn't killed his parents; instead, he used his lightsaber to slice a tree. This action proved that though he hated his uncle, he loved his mother and father, and it foreshadowed what he would do to Snoke, who couldn't sense that he had not killed the vision of his parents. Ren then destroyed the Cave of Evil, surprising Snoke, who told Ren that the cave had stood for thousands of years and that he had planned to bring other apprentices there. Ren answered by telling Snoke that the past was the past and that Snoke would no longer need any more apprentices.[[58]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Snoke-58)

### Enforcer of the First Order

#### Mission to Karaxis

:   "*You will go to* Karaxis*—both of you. Do not forget how integral they are to our plans. Travel there…show them* strength*.*"
:   ―Snoke, to Kylo Ren and Armitage Hux[[59]](#cite_note-Hyperspace_Stories_8-59)

 [![Ren oversaw the subjugation of the Karaxian people, forcing their world to submit to the rule of the First Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/KyloKillsAKaraxian-HyperspaceStories8.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240306225623) [![Ren oversaw the subjugation of the Karaxian people, forcing their world to submit to the rule of the First Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/KyloKillsAKaraxian-HyperspaceStories8.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240306225623)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/KyloKillsAKaraxian-HyperspaceStories8.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240306225623) 

Ren oversaw the subjugation of the Karaxian people, forcing their world to submit to the rule of the First Order.

 

In addition to his role as Snoke's apprentice, Kylo Ren was also an enforcer of the First Order. When the [Karaxians](/wiki/Karaxian "Karaxian") refused to submit to the First Order in spite of the military occupation of [Karaxis](/wiki/Karaxis "Karaxis"), Snoke sent Ren to their homeworld as a show of force. However, the [mission to Karaxis](/wiki/Mission_to_Karaxis "Mission to Karaxis") forced Ren to work alongside his rival, General Hux, whom the Supreme Leader also sent to Karaxis. While confident of his support with Snoke, who protected the general from Ren's wrath, Hux agreed to let Ren lead the mission. Upon their arrival in a [city](/wiki/City "City") on Karaxis, Ren intimidated and threatened the Karaxian leadership by using the Force to harm them. He also threatened to kill Hux when the general undermined him by openly challenging his methods. After interrogating one of the Karaxian leaders, whose mind he probed through the Force, Ren learned the location of the individual who could convince the local population to serve the First Order—a Karaxian known as [Kelvin Mann](/wiki/Kelvin_Mann "Kelvin Mann").[[59]](#cite_note-Hyperspace_Stories_8-59)

Ren searched the nearby [mountains](/wiki/Mountain "Mountain") for Mann and was attacked by the Karaxian's supporters. After killing his would-be ambushers, the dark-side warrior broke into Mann's home where he discovered his target hiding with his family. While threatening to harm them unless Mann agreed to support the First Order, Ren sensed a powerful presence in the Force. At first he believed a member of Mann's family was Force-sensitive, but after probing Mann's mind he realized that none of them were strong with the Force. Ultimately, Ren was forced to return to the city before he could pinpoint the exact location of the power source that he sensed: Hux had allowed a local creature, known as a [bramalish](/wiki/Bramalish "Bramalish"), to break through the city wall. The general believed he could use the threat of the creature to pressure the Karaxians into submission. However, the [First Order stormtroopers](/wiki/First_Order_stormtrooper "First Order stormtrooper") under Hux's command were not able to force the bramalish out of the city.[[59]](#cite_note-Hyperspace_Stories_8-59)

 [![The Karaxians surrendered to Ren after he protected their city from a bramalish, allowing the First Order to establish its authority over Karaxis.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/14/KyloPushesBramalish-HyperspaceStories8.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240402001747) [![The Karaxians surrendered to Ren after he protected their city from a bramalish, allowing the First Order to establish its authority over Karaxis.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/14/KyloPushesBramalish-HyperspaceStories8.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240402001747)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/14/KyloPushesBramalish-HyperspaceStories8.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240402001747) 

The Karaxians surrendered to Ren after he protected their city from a bramalish, allowing the First Order to establish its authority over Karaxis.

 

Ren returned to the city in time to prevent Hux's death, using the Force to telekinetically freeze the bramalish before it could crush the general with its [foot](/wiki/Foot "Foot"). Despite their rivalry, Ren and Hux worked together to force the bramalish to leave the city. Mann, who accompanied Ren to the city, agreed to convince his people to submit to the First Order's authority.[[59]](#cite_note-Hyperspace_Stories_8-59)

After the mission Ren returned to his master's flagship, the [*Mega*-class Star Dreadnought](/wiki/Mega-class_Star_Dreadnought "Mega-class Star Dreadnought") *[Supremacy](/wiki/Supremacy "Supremacy")*, where he reported his discovery of a presence in the Force on Karaxis. He remained uncertain about the source, however, and speculated as to whether it was the Force or simply an echo of it. He was certain that the power he felt did not emanate from a person. Snoke chastised his apprentice for being too undisciplined in the ways of the Force to locate the "presence," but reasoned that with more time and training Ren would grow into his role as a dark-side warrior whose duty was to extinguish the light side of the Force where ever he encountered it.[[59]](#cite_note-Hyperspace_Stories_8-59)

#### Colonization of the Unknown Regions

:   "*They also said that someone called* Kylo Ren *was leading the First Order army. Does that name mean anything to you?*"  
    "*You could say that. General Organa will want to hear about this immediately.*"
:   ―Kazuda Xiono and Ello Asty[[60]](#cite_note-The_Children_from_Tehar-60)

 [![Ren became known for his aggressive tactics, including the massacre of civilians.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/Decisive_Blow_SoR.png/revision/latest?cb=20190125052903) [![Ren became known for his aggressive tactics, including the massacre of civilians.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/Decisive_Blow_SoR.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20190125052903)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/Decisive_Blow_SoR.png/revision/latest?cb=20190125052903) 

Ren became known for his aggressive tactics, including the massacre of civilians.

 

As one of the commanders of the First Order's military, Ren was heavily involved in its campaign to colonize the Unknown Regions, where the former Imperials had been rebuilding their strength since the Battle of Jakku.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) Aided by mysterious alien navigators known as the [Attendants](/wiki/Attendants "Attendants"), the First Order had been able to navigate beyond the frontier of the known galaxy, allowing them to survive and rebuild their power.[[43]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-43) Several threats lurked in the Unknown Regions, hermetic kingdoms who were confronted by the growing new power. On Supreme Leader Snoke's instruction, the new military undertook a major offensive against several of these kingdoms to seize their worlds and resources to fuel their rise.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

At some point, Ren led an army to the world of [Tehar](/wiki/Tehar "Tehar"), where they subjugated the local population by [massacring](/wiki/Attack_on_Tehar "Attack on Tehar") a village. However, the siblings [Kel](/wiki/Kel "Kel") and [Eila](/wiki/Eila "Eila") survived the destruction of their village and fled Tehar after stowing away on a cargo ship. Since the children bore the knowledge of its aggressive actions against the people on Tehar, the First Order [placed](/wiki/Hunt_for_Eila_and_Kel "Hunt for Eila and Kel") a large bounty of twenty thousand credits on their heads, telling informants that Kel and Eila were members of a high-ranking First Order family from outside its military hierarchy.[[60]](#cite_note-The_Children_from_Tehar-60)

Kel and Eila eventually made their way to [Castilon](/wiki/Castilon "Castilon") and sought refuge on a [supertanker fuel depot](/wiki/Supertanker_fuel_depot "Supertanker fuel depot") known as the *[Colossus](/wiki/Colossus "Colossus")*. After meeting the Resistance [spy](/wiki/Spy "Spy") [Kazuda Xiono](/wiki/Kazuda_Xiono "Kazuda Xiono"), Eila told him about Ren's involvement in the raid on her village. Though she knew little about the warrior dressed in black, apart from his name and affiliation with the army that invaded Tehar, Ren's lightsaber reminded Eila of the legends about the Jedi who carried the same weapons. Xiono, who was also unaware of Ren's identity, passed this information to the Resistance while reporting to [Ello Asty](/wiki/Ello_Asty "Ello Asty").[[60]](#cite_note-The_Children_from_Tehar-60)

### The search for Skywalker

#### Hunting the last Jedi

:   "*If Skywalker returns, the new Jedi will rise.*"
:   ―Snoke[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

Both Ren and the Supreme Leader understood that if Skywalker and the Jedi were to ever return, they would be a grave threat to the future of the First Order. The people who were closest to Skywalker believed he had gone in search of the first Jedi temple, the location of which had been lost. A partial map was recovered from the archives of the Galactic Empire, but it was missing a key piece of the puzzle. The First Order soon discovered that the missing map fragment was in the possession of Lor San Tekka,[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) a member of the [Church of the Force](/wiki/Church_of_the_Force "Church of the Force").[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50)

#### GUHL-J03870

:   "*General Hux… I know where we must go… and I know this is the key. We are so close.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren[[61]](#cite_note-Pest_Control-61)

 [![Despite their rivalry, Kylo Ren and General Armitage Hux worked together during the hunt for Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/Ren_and_Hux_meeting.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210122035805) [![Despite their rivalry, Kylo Ren and General Armitage Hux worked together during the hunt for Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/Ren_and_Hux_meeting.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210122035805)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/Ren_and_Hux_meeting.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210122035805) 

Despite their rivalry, Kylo Ren and General Armitage Hux worked together during the hunt for Skywalker.

 

Later, Ren, Hux and two First Order [admirals](/wiki/Admiral "Admiral") gathered in a conference room aboard the *Finalizer* over the planet [GUHL-J03870](/wiki/GUHL-J03870 "GUHL-J03870"). They were discussing travel to a planet in the [Western Reaches](/wiki/Western_Reaches "Western Reaches"). While in the conference, the [creature](/wiki/Unidentified_GUHL-J03870_creature "Unidentified GUHL-J03870 creature") that the stormtrooper, [FN-2187](/wiki/Finn "Finn"), was chasing turned off the lights, interrupting the conference. Ren, his temper under control, felt something nearby: something from the planet that should not be on board. He activated his lightsaber to illuminate the room and looked around, but whatever it was had now gone.[[61]](#cite_note-Pest_Control-61)

After the conference, Ren transmitted orders to Phasma via private frequency. But he had to make sure she got them, so he walked over to the captain's quarters and called her from outside. Only Phasma's helmet appeared through the opened doors. Pleased by her punctuality, Ren relayed what he sensed to Phasma, for he planned to have a discreet search throughout the *Finalizer*. He ordered her to take a [squad](/wiki/Squad "Squad") of trainees to investigate the planet for any Resistance activity. Anything Phasma may find, she must deliver to Ren. Then the dark warrior left.[[61]](#cite_note-Pest_Control-61)

#### Marooned with Hux

:   "*How did we…? Did you…did you save me?*"  
    "*Not intentionally. I saved myself. You were just nearby. Communications are out.*"  
    "*Which means I have no choice but to talk to you instead of literally anyone else.*"
:   ―Armitage Hux and Kylo Ren[[62]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Hux-62)

 [![A shuttle carrying Kylo Ren and General Hux was sabotaged by conspirators within the First Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/WakeUpHux-AORHux1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190926002134) [![A shuttle carrying Kylo Ren and General Hux was sabotaged by conspirators within the First Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/WakeUpHux-AORHux1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190926002134)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/WakeUpHux-AORHux1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190926002134) 

A shuttle carrying Kylo Ren and General Hux was sabotaged by conspirators within the First Order.

 

At one point before the [attack on Tuanul](/wiki/Attack_on_Tuanul "Attack on Tuanul"), an [*Xi*-class light shuttle](/wiki/Xi-class_light_shuttle "Xi-class light shuttle") carrying Kylo Ren and General Hux crash-landed on a [distant world](/wiki/Unidentified_planet_(Bylsma) "Unidentified planet (Bylsma)"). Their shuttle was consequently destroyed and the pilot died in the crash, although Ren survived the incident by protecting himself with the Force. By saving himself, however, he inadvertently saved Hux's life as well. The destruction of their vessel along with its communications system left them marooned and unable to contact the First Order. Realizing that a [saboteur](/wiki/Unidentified_radar_technician "Unidentified radar technician") was responsible for their predicament, the two rivals began bickering over which of them was at fault. Ren chided Hux as he believed the general was targeted by a conspirator in his own army, to which Hux responded by mocking Ren for his temper and efforts emulate Darth Vader. Ren drew his lightsaber at the mention of his parents and contemplated ridding himself of Hux once and for all, aware that it would be some time before the First Order located their position. However, Hux reminded him of the one person who would learn the truth: Ren's master, Supreme Leader Snoke. Although he did not understand why Hux was important to Snoke's plans, Ren conceded the point that there would be a penalty for killing the Supreme Leader's favored general, and therefore deactivated his lightsaber, sparing Hux.[[62]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Hux-62)

Following their argument, Ren and Hux were attacked by a [norwood](/wiki/Norwood "Norwood"), a large creature native to the planet that they were stranded on. Drawing his lightsaber once more, Ren took a defensive stance and told Hux to stay behind him, only to see that the general had already fled in the opposite direction of the beast. Though abandoned by Hux, Ren stood his ground and managed to incapacitate the norwood by using the Force to smack its head against a tree. Believing himself victorious, Ren called Hux a coward and told him to come out from wherever he was hiding, but a second norwood ambushed him and ultimately rendered the dark warrior unconscious, at which point the Alderaanian exile [Bylsma](/wiki/Bylsma_(Alderaanian) "Bylsma (Alderaanian)") emerged and prevented the norwoods from killing Ren.[[62]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Hux-62)

 [![Ren used his powers to survive the crash, inadvertently saving Hux in the process.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/SavedByTheForce-AORHux1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190926002542) [![Ren used his powers to survive the crash, inadvertently saving Hux in the process.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/SavedByTheForce-AORHux1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190926002542)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/SavedByTheForce-AORHux1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190926002542) 

Ren used his powers to survive the crash, inadvertently saving Hux in the process.

 

Hux, who had been hiding in the trees and watching as the event occurred, cautiously approached Bylsma from his hiding place. Recognizing the old man's uniform, Hux came to the conclusion that Bylsma was an Alderaanian [palace guard](/wiki/Alderaan_Guard "Alderaan Guard"). Bylsma confirmed as much and revealed that he had fled into exile after the destruction of Alderaan. He stranded himself on a distant planet and severed his connections to the larger galaxy, fearing that his new home would suffer Alderaan's fate if he attempted to use his ship's communications, but as a result, Bylsma had no knowledge of the events that unfolded after the disaster. Hux used Bylsma's ignorance of recent galactic history in order to gain his trust. In addition, he used Ren's heritage to his advantage, informing Bylsma that the man whom the norwoods attacked was, in fact, a fellow son of Alderaan. More to the point, he was the son of Leia Organa, the princess of Alderaan. Bylsma, who had known both the princess and her adoptive father, saw the physical resemblance between Ren and his mother and wondered if Ren was anything like the princess he once served. Hux assured him that Ren was indeed like his mother, even if he would have denied it.[[62]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Hux-62)

Bylsma built a stretcher and carried Ren to his home, where Hux convinced the retired soldier to give him access to the ship's communications so that they could be rescued. After regaining consciousness, Ren played along with Hux's deception until a shuttle arrived to retrieve them. The shuttle ramp lowered revealing Captain Phasma and a squad of stormtroopers, leading to the norwoods' immediate death by blaster fire. Ren boarded the shuttle in silence alongside Hux, who told the captain to spare the old man's life but to disable his communications array, leaving Bylsma truly stranded and alone. They reported directly to Snoke via hologram after their return to Starkiller Base; although Ren offered to punish the culprit responsible for sabotaging the shuttle, Hux insisted on handling the matter personally, given that the conspiracy was directed at him. Snoke approved the general's request, causing Ren to question the Supreme Leader's faith in Hux. Ren, who could sense Hux's ambition to kill and replace Snoke, and therefore, deemed him untrustworthy, was certain that his master knew it as well. Snoke dismissed Ren's concerns, however, and explained why Hux—a vicious and unforgiving man, consumed by ambition and driven by spite, molded as such through years of abuse—was ultimately a useful asset.[[62]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Hux-62)

### Walking in Darth Vader's shadow

#### Confronting old enemies of Vader

:   "*But still, we are walking in Darth Vader's shadow. This is the field where he fought. There is glory here.*"  
    "*Glory? Nah. There's none of that buried out there. There are only wasted lives…*"
:   ―Kylo Ren and Ruthford[[63]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Kylo-63)

 [![Kylo Ren confronted the Benathy decades after their battle with his grandfather.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e2/IWillSucceedWhereYouFailed-AORKyloRen1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190926181825) [![Kylo Ren confronted the Benathy decades after their battle with his grandfather.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e2/IWillSucceedWhereYouFailed-AORKyloRen1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20190926181825)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e2/IWillSucceedWhereYouFailed-AORKyloRen1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190926181825) 

Kylo Ren confronted the Benathy decades after their battle with his grandfather.

 

The First Order deployed an army, under the command of Kylo Ren, to the [Benathy](/wiki/Benathy "Benathy") homeworld in [Wild Space](/wiki/Wild_Space "Wild Space"), intending to put an end to their [expansionist campaign](/wiki/Benathy_expansion "Benathy expansion"). Ren, who was aware that his grandfather once [fought](/wiki/Battle_against_the_Benathy "Battle against the Benathy") against the Benathy decades earlier during the reign of the Galactic Empire, saw his mission as an opportunity to succeed where Darth Vader failed—by forcing the Benathy to submit to the First Order. Captain [Ruthford](/wiki/Ruthford "Ruthford"), a veteran [Imperial stormtrooper](/wiki/Stormtrooper "Stormtrooper") who joined the First Order, accompanied Ren as his military [advisor](/wiki/Advisor "Advisor"). Having served with Ren's grandfather against the Benathy, Ruthford opined that Vader managed to subdue the aliens but at the cost of thousands on both sides, resulting in a pyrrhic victory. But where Ruthford was disillusioned by his past experience with the Benathy, believing their conflict with the Empire was pointless and a waste of lives, Ren saw only glory as he walked across the field of battle where Vader once stood, the shadow of his grandfather's legacy looming over him.[[63]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Kylo-63)

Despite the army behind him, the First Order's troops were ordered to stand by while Ren conducted negotiations with the Benathy's ruler, [King](/wiki/King "King") [Kristoff](/wiki/Kristoff "Kristoff"), attempting to secure their capitulation without bloodshed. Desiring to expand the Benathy's domain, Kristoff not only conquered four nearby planets but also had them purged of all life, leading Ren to demand that the Benathy cease their expansion immediately. Compared to Ren, the late Vader commanded the king's respect, but only to a degree because while Vader killed [Kristoff's predecessor](/wiki/Unidentified_Benathy_king "Unidentified Benathy king") he failed to defeat their [Zillo Beast](/wiki/Zillo_Beast "Zillo Beast"), which the Benathy worshiped as a god. Nevertheless, Ren continued his efforts to resolve their situation through diplomacy and even attempted to dominate the king's will by way of the Force. The [mind trick](/wiki/Mind_trick "Mind trick") failed, however. Kristoff openly mocked Ren's negotiating skills, causing Ruthford to caution him against provoking the dark warrior. At that point, Ren stabbed the king through the head with his lightsaber, concluding negotiations in favor of open [battle](/wiki/Battle_against_the_Benathy_(First_Order) "Battle against the Benathy (First Order)").[[63]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Kylo-63)

 [![With the death of their Zillo Beast god, the Benathy bent the knee to Kylo Ren and the First Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/KneelBeforeRen-AORKyloRen1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190926183308) [![With the death of their Zillo Beast god, the Benathy bent the knee to Kylo Ren and the First Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/KneelBeforeRen-AORKyloRen1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190926183308)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/KneelBeforeRen-AORKyloRen1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190926183308) 

With the death of their Zillo Beast god, the Benathy bent the knee to Kylo Ren and the First Order.

 

Leading by example like his grandfather before him, Ren fought alongside his stormtroopers as they engaged the Benathy and personally killed numerous enemy combatants until their deity arrived. Despite Ruthford's skepticism, Ren was undaunted and ordered his men to keep fighting. After their initial efforts to kill the beast failed, he improvised a plan to kill the creature to the dismay of Ruthford, who could no longer restrain himself from expressing his disapproval of Ren's desire to match Vader's achievements. In his view, there was no competition between Ren and Vader because the latter was long since dead.[[63]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Kylo-63)

Despite the captain's lack of faith in him, Ren commanded a shuttle to bring him to the jaws of the Zillo Beast, diving head-first into its mouth. Convinced that Ren was dead, Ruthford was in the middle of recommending the option of retreat to a nearby admiral when the Zillo Beast suddenly collapsed and died. Ren had killed the creature from within, where it was vulnerable, and managed to cut his way out, emerging from its corpse covered in the blood of the Benathy's deity. Declaring that their god was now dead, the dark warrior commanded the Benathy to submit to the First Order, and they did by kneeling in submission to him. In the end, he not only gained the allegiance of the Benathy, but also Captain Ruthford's respect.[[63]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Kylo-63)

#### Mission to Pillio

:   "*Tell me where Lor San Tekka took the map.*"  
    "*…Bayora. He took it to Bayora.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren and Del Meeko[[64]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-64)

 [![Ren personally oversaw the First Order's efforts to locate and destroy the last Jedi, his uncle and former Master Luke Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fd/MissionPillioKylo.png/revision/latest?cb=20171221230623) [![Ren personally oversaw the First Order's efforts to locate and destroy the last Jedi, his uncle and former Master Luke Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fd/MissionPillioKylo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20171221230623)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fd/MissionPillioKylo.png/revision/latest?cb=20171221230623) 

Ren personally oversaw the First Order's efforts to locate and destroy the last Jedi, his uncle and former Master Luke Skywalker.

 

The hunt for Skywalker caused Ren to undertake a [journey](/wiki/Mission_to_Pillio_(First_Order) "Mission to Pillio (First Order)") the planet [Pillio](/wiki/Pillio "Pillio"). Although San Tekka was not found on the world, the First Order's allies captured and detained [Del Meeko](/wiki/Del_Meeko "Del Meeko"), a veteran of the Galactic Civil War who served the Empire and New Republic, in turn, as a member of [Inferno Squad](/wiki/Inferno_Squad "Inferno Squad"). Upon his arrival, the dark warrior was greeted by [Protectorate](/wiki/Protectorate_(title) "Protectorate (title)") [Gleb](/wiki/Gleb "Gleb") of [Jinata Security](/wiki/Jinata_Security "Jinata Security"). Dismissive of the formalities, he instructed the [Aqualish](/wiki/Aqualish "Aqualish") [officer](/wiki/Officer "Officer") to lead him to Meeko. He found the former soldier wounded and alone on the [bridge](/wiki/Bridge_(starship) "Bridge (starship)") of the [*Raider II*-class corvette](/wiki/Raider_II-class_corvette "Raider II-class corvette") [*Corvus*](/wiki/Corvus_(Raider_II-class) "Corvus (Raider II-class)").[[64]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-64)

Ignoring the prisoner's sarcasm, Ren used the Force to [probe](/wiki/Mind_probe_(Force_power) "Mind probe (Force power)") through Meeko's [mind](/wiki/Brain "Brain"), determined to learn where San Tekka took the map. For all of Meeko's efforts to resist the probe, invading his mind was a relatively simple task for Ren, who saw memories ranging across the former [commando](/wiki/Commando "Commando")'s life—from his service on [Scarif](/wiki/Scarif "Scarif") as a [coastal defender stormtrooper](/wiki/Coastal_defender_stormtrooper "Coastal defender stormtrooper") to his participation in the Battle of Endor and the [skirmish](/wiki/Skirmish_on_Vardos "Skirmish on Vardos") on [Vardos](/wiki/Vardos "Vardos"). He also learned that Meeko encountered Skywalker on Pillio and subsequently discovered his faith in the Force. Ultimately, Meeko was unable to resist Ren's powers and revealed that San Tekka took the map with him to [Bayora](/wiki/Bayora "Bayora").[[64]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-64)

Having gained the information he sought, Ren turned the prisoner over to [First Order officer](/wiki/First_Order_officer "First Order officer") [Gideon Hask](/wiki/Gideon_Hask "Gideon Hask"), one of Meeko's former teammates in the Inferno Squad prior the Empire's fall, who executed Meeko shortly thereafter.[[64]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-64)

#### Raid on Jakku

:   "*The map to Skywalker. We know you found it. And now you're going to give it to the First Order.*"  
    "*The First Order rose from the dark side. You did not.*"  
    "*I'll show you the dark side.*"  
    "*You may try. But you cannot deny the truth that is your family.*"  
    "*You're so right.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren and Lor San Tekka[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

 [![Ren demanded that Lor San Tekka give him the map to Skywalker, but the old explorer refused&mdash;and paid for it with his life.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e3/Lor_San_Tekka_brought_before_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20190604061240) [![Ren demanded that Lor San Tekka give him the map to Skywalker, but the old explorer refused&mdash;and paid for it with his life.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e3/Lor_San_Tekka_brought_before_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190604061240)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e3/Lor_San_Tekka_brought_before_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20190604061240) 

Ren demanded that Lor San Tekka give him the map to Skywalker, but the old explorer refused—and paid for it with his life.

 

Eventually, the First Order learned that San Tekka was on [Jakku](/wiki/Jakku "Jakku"). Ren, who knew San Tekka from childhood as the explorer was once an old ally of Organa and Skywalker, brought the [*Resurgent*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Resurgent-class_Star_Destroyer "Resurgent-class Star Destroyer") *[Finalizer](/wiki/Finalizer "Finalizer")* in his search for the map. The First Order's military attacked the village of [Tuanul](/wiki/Tuanul "Tuanul"), where San Tekka lived. Once the First Order stormtroopers, under the command of Phasma, rounded up the denizens of the village, Ren arrived on the battlefield and confronted San Tekka, lamenting how old the former explorer had become, to which San Tekka replied that Ren's fall to the dark side was far worse. Ren demanded that San Tekka give the map to the First Order, but San Tekka refused to submit to the will of the dark side and reminded the one-time Jedi that Ren could not deny the truth of his heritage, at which point Ren struck him down with his lightsaber while sarcastically agreeing with him.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

Moments later, he was shot at from afar by [Commander](/wiki/Commander "Commander") [Poe Dameron](/wiki/Poe_Dameron "Poe Dameron"), a [starfighter](/wiki/Resistance_Starfighter_Corps "Resistance Starfighter Corps") pilot in the Resistance who was sent to Jakku by General Organa to find the map before the First Order. Ren used the Force to [freeze](/wiki/Force_Stasis "Force Stasis") the blaster bolt midair, and Dameron was soon brought before him. The dark warrior realized that Tekka gave the map to Dameron and ordered that the [troopers](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper") bring the pilot onto Ren's [command shuttle](/wiki/Kylo_Ren%27s_command_shuttle "Kylo Ren's command shuttle"), before giving the order to kill the rest of the villagers. One stormtrooper, FN-2187, hesitated and ultimately chose not to fire on the civilians, an act that Ren noticed as he could sense his fear before boarding his shuttle.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

#### Locating BB-8

:   "*Sir… we were unable to acquire the droid on Jakku. It escaped capture… aboard a stolen YT Corellian model freighter.*"  
    "*The droid… stole a freighter?*"
:   ―Dopheld Mitaka and Kylo Ren[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

 [![Ren used the Force to extract the location of the map from Poe Dameron's mind.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/Kylo_tortures_Poe_Dameron.png/revision/latest?cb=20200624101324) [![Ren used the Force to extract the location of the map from Poe Dameron's mind.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/Kylo_tortures_Poe_Dameron.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/269?cb=20200624101324)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/Kylo_tortures_Poe_Dameron.png/revision/latest?cb=20200624101324) 

Ren used the Force to extract the location of the map from Poe Dameron's mind.

 

Dameron was [brought](/wiki/Prison "Prison") aboard the *Finalizer* for interrogation, where he was placed into an [interrogation](/wiki/Torture "Torture") [chair](/wiki/Interrogation_chair "Interrogation chair").[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) The device, used by Ren to extract information from his prisoners, was based on similar devices once used by the [Inquisitors](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius") of the Galactic Empire.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) First Order interrogators were unable to break Dameron, but they did learn that he was the best pilot in the Resistance, a feat that Ren noted once he began interrogating the pilot personally. Though the dark knight was impressed that Dameron had not yet been broken, Ren began to use the Force to mentally extract the information from Dameron's mind. The pilot, who resisted the Force attack, finally was forced to reveal that he had hidden the map inside his [BB unit](/wiki/BB-series_astromech_droid "BB-series astromech droid"), [BB-8](/wiki/BB-8 "BB-8"), who was likely still on Jakku. Ren informed General Hux of the new development and left the recovery of the droid in the hands of the military.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

Shortly after leaving Dameron under the guard of several stormtroopers, Ren arrived on the *Finalizer*'s bridge upon hearing that the Resistance pilot [escaped](/wiki/Escape_from_the_Finalizer "Escape from the Finalizer") aboard a [TIE fighter](/wiki/TIE/fo_space_superiority_fighter "TIE/fo space superiority fighter"). Hux confirmed this with the additional information of Dameron having had help from someone within the First Order's ranks. Ren realized that it could only have been FN-2187, after remembering how the conflicted soldier had hesitated in Tuanul, and he said as much to Hux. The TIE fighter was eventually shot down after a brief skirmish, and it crash-landed on Jakku.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

 [![Dameron escaped with the help of FN-2187, causing Ren to doubt the loyalty of Hux's stormtroopers.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/Phasma_Hux_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20170908043445) [![Dameron escaped with the help of FN-2187, causing Ren to doubt the loyalty of Hux's stormtroopers.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/Phasma_Hux_Ren.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170908043445)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/Phasma_Hux_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20170908043445) 

Dameron escaped with the help of FN-2187, causing Ren to doubt the loyalty of Hux's stormtroopers.

 

The First Order recognized that Dameron and the deserter designated FN-2187 were looking for the droid, so Hux ordered a [squadron](/wiki/Squadron "Squadron") to be sent to Jakku to recover it first. Hux soon spoke to the Supreme Leader, who ordered them to capture the droid if they could, but destroy it if they must. Ren questioned the capability of Hux's soldiers and training methods, wondering aloud whether the Supreme Leader would be better off using an army of [clones](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning")[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) as the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic")[[65]](#cite_note-Episode_II-65) and the early Empire had once done.[[66]](#cite_note-Episode_III-66) Hux told him that they were more than capable, and warned Ren not to let his personal mission to find Skywalker interfere with the Supreme Leader's orders.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

Later that day,[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) a nervous [Lieutenant](/wiki/Lieutenant "Lieutenant") [Dopheld Mitaka](/wiki/Dopheld_Mitaka "Dopheld Mitaka")[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) informed Ren that the [astromech droid](/wiki/Astromech_droid "Astromech droid") escaped aboard a [YT-1300 light freighter](/wiki/YT-1300_light_freighter "YT-1300 light freighter"). At first, Ren found it unlikely for a single droid to be capable of stealing a ship but allowed Mitaka to continue. Further intelligence suggested the probability of FN-2187, who had now branded himself with the name Finn, abetting the droid's evacuation from Jakku. Enraged that the [traitor](/wiki/Treason "Treason") had robbed him of the means to find Skywalker, Ren ignited his lightsaber and destroyed the [computer](/wiki/Computer "Computer") terminal in front of him. The dark warrior calmed down, asking if there was "anything else." Mitaka replied that the defector and the droid had help from a [girl](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker"). Ren used the Force to drag Mitaka towards him, grabbed him by the neck, and demanded to know who the girl was.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

### Return of the past

#### The pull to the light

:   "*The droid we seek is aboard the* Millennium Falcon*. In the hands of your father… Han Solo.*"  
    "*He means nothing to me.*"  
    "*Even you, master of the Knights of Ren… have never faced such a test.*"  
    "*By the grace of your training, I will not be seduced.*"  
    "*We shall see. We shall see.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren and Snoke[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

 [![The Supreme Leader told Ren that BB-8 was in the hands of Han Solo and warned the dark warrior he was about to face his greatest test.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Kylo_Ren_and_Snoke.png/revision/latest?cb=20200624101847) [![The Supreme Leader told Ren that BB-8 was in the hands of Han Solo and warned the dark warrior he was about to face his greatest test.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Kylo_Ren_and_Snoke.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20200624101847)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Kylo_Ren_and_Snoke.png/revision/latest?cb=20200624101847) 

The Supreme Leader told Ren that BB-8 was in the hands of Han Solo and warned the dark warrior he was about to face his greatest test.

 

With the droid gone, the *Finalizer* made its way to Starkiller Base. Once there, Ren and Hux spoke to Supreme Leader Snoke, who communicated to his subordinates via an enlarged [hologram](/wiki/Hologram "Hologram"). Snoke remained concerned that Skywalker's return would be a threat to the First Order, so Hux proposed that they finally use the weapon as intended and destroy the New Republic one and for all. Without the Republic, Hux knew that the Resistance would be vulnerable and could be stopped before they found Skywalker. The Supreme Leader gave the general his permission and Hux left to oversee preparations, while Ren remained behind.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

Both Snoke and Ren could sense that the Force was awakening[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) from dormancy once again,[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) and the Supreme Leader told his apprentice that the droid was in the hands of Han Solo; the old smuggler had the astromech aboard his ship, the *Millennium Falcon*. Ren claimed Solo meant nothing to him and that he would not be "seduced" by the light[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) as his grandfather once was,[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39) not while he had Snoke's training. Even so, the Supreme Leader warned that this would be Ren's greatest test.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

Though Ren believed he would not be seduced, he nonetheless felt the pull of the light side.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) In his personal quarters aboard the *Finalizer*,[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) Ren spoke to the helmet of Darth Vader, searching for guidance and hoping that the legacy of the Dark Lord could remind him of the power of the dark side. He swore that if Vader could somehow show him that dark power, then Ren would finish what the Sith started and destroy the last of the Jedi.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

#### Capture of Rey

:   "*You. You're afraid. That you will never be as strong as Darth Vader.*"
:   ―Rey, to Kylo Ren[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

 [![Ren witnessed the power that Starkiller Base unleashed upon the Hosnian system, destroying the New Republic and sending billions to their deaths.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/Destruction_of_Hosnian_System.png/revision/latest?cb=20160122044436) [![Ren witnessed the power that Starkiller Base unleashed upon the Hosnian system, destroying the New Republic and sending billions to their deaths.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/Destruction_of_Hosnian_System.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20160122044436)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/Destruction_of_Hosnian_System.png/revision/latest?cb=20160122044436) 

Ren witnessed the power that Starkiller Base unleashed upon the Hosnian system, destroying the New Republic and sending billions to their deaths.

 

The First Order soon learned that Solo, Rey, Finn, and BB-8 had landed on [Takodana](/wiki/Takodana "Takodana"), and were in the [castle](/wiki/Takodana_Castle "Takodana Castle") of the ancient [pirate](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate") [Maz Kanata](/wiki/Maz_Kanata "Maz Kanata"), whom Ren hoped would help deliver the droid to the Resistance. Before the First Order departed, General Hux unleashed the Starkiller weapon against the Republic. After giving a speech to his forces about the end of a regime that he believed could not contain the galactic chaos, Hux commanded that the weapon be fired. Ren watched from the bridge of the *Finalizer*[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) as the weapon's [phantom energy](/wiki/Phantom_energy "Phantom energy")[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39) left the surface of Starkiller Base and made their way[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) to the Republic's [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") of [Hosnian Prime](/wiki/Hosnian_Prime "Hosnian Prime"),[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) where they [destroyed](/wiki/Hosnian_Cataclysm "Hosnian Cataclysm") the entire [Hosnian system](/wiki/Hosnian_system "Hosnian system").[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

 [![Ren discovered Rey on Takodana and took her prisoner once he realized she had seen the map to Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/ReyRen-TFAintltrailer.png/revision/latest?cb=20160415123532) [![Ren discovered Rey on Takodana and took her prisoner once he realized she had seen the map to Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/ReyRen-TFAintltrailer.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160415123532)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/ReyRen-TFAintltrailer.png/revision/latest?cb=20160415123532) 

Ren discovered Rey on Takodana and took her prisoner once he realized she had seen the map to Skywalker.

 

With the Republic severely damaged, Ren led his forces to Takodana, where the stormtroopers [attacked](/wiki/Battle_of_Takodana "Battle of Takodana") Kanata's castle. Solo, Finn, and BB-8 were briefly captured by the First Order before Dameron and the Resistance Starfighter Corps arrived to recover the droid. When Rey and the astromech tried to escape through the forest, they split up as she led the stormtroopers away from the droid. Ren soon arrived on the battlefield and found her in the woods. She fired at him with [her blaster](/wiki/Rey%27s_blaster "Rey's blaster"), but he followed her and deflected the shots with his lightsaber. Finally, Ren froze her in place with a [telekinetic](/wiki/Telekinesis "Telekinesis") attack.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

Using the Force to enter Rey's mind, Ren saw that she had seen the map he sought. Believing the First Order would not need the droid since he could view Rey's memories, he used the Force to render her unconscious and captured her. He ordered the First Order to retreat and their forces left Takodana. The droid ultimately made it out of the forests and into the hands of the Resistance.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

 [![Ren probed Rey's mind for the map to Skywalker and sensed her loneliness in the process.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/Mind_Probe_SWDA.png/revision/latest?cb=20170920000517) [![Ren probed Rey's mind for the map to Skywalker and sensed her loneliness in the process.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/Mind_Probe_SWDA.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170920000517)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/Mind_Probe_SWDA.png/revision/latest?cb=20170920000517) 

Ren probed Rey's mind for the map to Skywalker and sensed her loneliness in the process.

 

Ren brought Rey to Starkiller Base via his command shuttle and restrained her in an interrogation chair. When she awoke, she asked where her friends were, and Ren told her he had no idea and pointed out that would be a relief to her. He sensed she still wanted to kill him, and she said it was because she was being hunted by a creature in a mask. He removed his mask to show his young face and asked about the droid, but the girl only gave him BB-8's technical specifications. Ren told her that he knew about the map and that the First Order had recovered the rest of it from the archives of the Empire.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

Ren warned Rey that he could take whatever he wanted from her before probing her mind with the Force while she resisted his mental attack.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) At the time, Ren was unaware that he and Rey formed a [prophesized](/wiki/Doctrine_of_the_Dyad "Doctrine of the Dyad") [dyad in the Force](/wiki/Force_dyad "Force dyad"), but he sensed they had an innate connection.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) In her mind, he discovered her name,[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39) felt her loneliness and fear, and saw an [ocean](/wiki/Ocean "Ocean") and an island that she had dreamed about during her life as a [scavenger](/wiki/Scavenger "Scavenger") in the [junkyards](/wiki/Starship_Graveyard "Starship Graveyard"). When he sensed Han Solo, Ren could tell that Rey looked at the smuggler as a father figure, but he said that Solo would have only disappointed her. Rey grew more resistant to his mental attack and turned it against him, using the same ability to see that Ren was afraid he would never be as strong as Darth Vader was.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

#### Snoke's new strategy

:   "*Supreme Leader, I can get the map from the girl. I just need your guidance.*"  
    "*If what you say about this girl is true… Bring her to me.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren and Snoke[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

 [![Snoke ordered Hux to target the Starkiller at the Resistance, and told Ren to bring Rey before him.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/Snoke_speaks_to_Kylo_Ren_and_Hux.png/revision/latest?cb=20160320231828) [![Snoke ordered Hux to target the Starkiller at the Resistance, and told Ren to bring Rey before him.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/Snoke_speaks_to_Kylo_Ren_and_Hux.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160320231828)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/Snoke_speaks_to_Kylo_Ren_and_Hux.png/revision/latest?cb=20160320231828) 

Snoke ordered Hux to target the Starkiller at the Resistance, and told Ren to bring Rey before him.

 

Stunned by the reversal, Ren left Rey behind in the interrogation chamber and spoke to the Supreme Leader, who reacted with incredulity that a mere scavenger resisted him. Ren told Snoke that Rey was even stronger with the Force than she realized. The Supreme Leader asked what happened to the droid, and General Hux, who had just entered the chamber, told Snoke that Ren believed he only needed Rey and allowed the droid to escape. Concerned that the Resistance might have the full map to Skywalker, Snoke ordered Hux to unleash the Starkiller weapon against the [Resistance base](/wiki/Resistance_base "Resistance base") on the planet [D'Qar](/wiki/D%27Qar "D'Qar"). Ren swore that he could still find the map in Rey's mind as long as he had his master's guidance, so the Supreme Leader ordered Rey to be brought to him.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

On his way to Rey's holding cell, Ren learned that the girl had somehow broken out. The guard who had been ordered to watch her could not fathom how he ended up in his quarters. When asked by a First Order officer if "stronger methods" were needed, Ren declined; any further simple questioning might enable the guard to remember something important. In the meantime, Rey must be found.[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39)

When Ren returned to the cell,[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) he needed to see if Rey had truly used her emerging Force abilities to escape. Inspection revealed the interrogation bench was deserted, every one of its restraints left open as if to mock Ren.[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39) Enraged, he ignited his lightsaber and destroyed the room, causing two passing stormtroopers to quickly back away.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

#### Han Solo's last stand

:   "*I'm being torn apart. I want to be free of this pain. I know what I have to do… but I don't know if I have the strength to do it. Will you help me?*"  
    "*Yes. Anything.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren and Han Solo[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

Ren commanded the First Order troops to be on alert for Rey as she began making her way through the base, as he knew that the longer she was able to tap into her powers while escaping, the more dangerous she would become. [A trooper](/wiki/Unidentified_First_Order_stormtrooper_(Starkiller_Base) "Unidentified First Order stormtrooper (Starkiller Base)") reported sensor readings in [Hangar 718](/wiki/Hangar_718 "Hangar 718"), which meant Rey could be there. But investigations turned up nothing. Nonetheless, Ren wanted every hangar on lockdown to prevent Rey from commandeering a ship. Right in the middle of that order, he was interrupted by a familiar presence: Han Solo. His father was on Starkiller Base.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

Ren ordered for a search of the *Millennium Falcon*, for the ship had shortly been sighted at the edge of a cliff. By the time he arrived on the scene, everything checked clear and not a single hidden trap could be found. He boarded the *Falcon* and sat on the pilot's seat, looking for anything that may lead him to Solo's whereabouts. Just then, he spotted Resistance [X-wings](/wiki/T-70_X-wing_starfighter "T-70 X-wing starfighter") flying past and [assaulting](/wiki/Battle_of_Starkiller_Base "Battle of Starkiller Base") the [thermal oscillator](/wiki/Thermal_oscillator "Thermal oscillator"),[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39) hoping to destroy it and set off a chain reaction that would cause the planet to implode before the weapon could destroy D'Qar. Ren rushed to the oscillator, commanding his troops to find the intruders.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) He knew Solo had to be nearby,[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39) as well as the fact that he did not come alone.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

 [![Ren was confronted by his estranged father, Han Solo, who tried to convince his son to reject the dark side and return home.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/92/KyloRenandHanSolo-KyloDB.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200401153819) [![Ren was confronted by his estranged father, Han Solo, who tried to convince his son to reject the dark side and return home.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/92/KyloRenandHanSolo-KyloDB.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/253?cb=20200401153819)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/92/KyloRenandHanSolo-KyloDB.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200401153819) 

Ren was confronted by his estranged father, Han Solo, who tried to convince his son to reject the dark side and return home.

 

As Ren advanced on the walkway, he stopped upon hearing the voice of his father, calling out to him from behind, using his birth name. He turned about face and said he had been waiting for this eventuality. Solo told him to remove the mask so he could see the face of his son once more. Ren removed the mask but told Solo that he had destroyed Ben, who Ren thought was weak and foolish, much like his father before him. Solo refused to acknowledge Ren's pessimistic stance on the matter, retorting that his son was very much alive and Snoke was simply using Ren for his power, and that once Snoke had exhausted Ren's usefulness, he would be disposed of.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

Ren, while neither denying nor confirming what Solo said about Snoke to be true, stated that it was too late for him. Solo pleaded with Ren to come home to his true family, claiming that he and Organa desperately missed the presence of their son. Ren, conflicted by the pull towards the light, broke down in tears and told his father that he was being torn apart by the constant struggle between the dark and the light inside him and wanted to be free of the pain that he was feeling. He knew what he had to do to put a permanent end to his inner turmoil, although Ren was uncertain whether or not he could perform the necessary act to do so. Asking for his father's assistance in ceasing the struggle, Solo agreed, not knowing that it was the light that Ren felt conflicted by.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

 [![Although Ren found the resolve to kill his own father, the act of patricide only worsened the conflict within him.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/05/Kylo_impales_Solo.png/revision/latest?cb=20160416064326) [![Although Ren found the resolve to kill his own father, the act of patricide only worsened the conflict within him.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/05/Kylo_impales_Solo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/264?cb=20160416064326)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/05/Kylo_impales_Solo.png/revision/latest?cb=20160416064326) 

Although Ren found the resolve to kill his own father, the act of patricide only worsened the conflict within him.

 

Ren, who was being watched from afar by Chewbacca, Rey, and Finn, took out his lightsaber and Solo grabbed hold of it. As the Starkiller finished draining the [star](/wiki/Star "Star") it orbited to power the weapon, and the light on the planet died out, Ren ignited his lightsaber and impaled his father through the torso. A mortally wounded Han Solo touched his son's face one last time before falling to his death in the bowels of the oscillator.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) Despite Ren's role in his death, Han died refusing to believe that his son was lost to the dark side forever.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7)

Unbeknownst to Ren, he had carried out a Sith [trial of ascendancy](/wiki/Trial_of_ascendancy "Trial of ascendancy"), a trial that required the sacrifice of a loved one to unlock newfound depths of dark power.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) The act of patricide had an unsettling effect on Ren, as did Solo's gesture of compassion which tormented Ren far more than killing his own father.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7) Rather than make him stronger in the dark side, as he had thought, it had weakened his spirit.[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39) He became unbalanced,[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) and was more miserable and weak than before.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7) The shock had been so profound, he did not register Chewbacca's roar of anguish[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39) nor Rey's scream of horror.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

Enraged by the loss of his best friend, Chewbacca fired a powerful shot from his Wookiee [bowcaster](/wiki/Bowcaster "Bowcaster") and hit Ren in the left side, seriously injuring the dark knight.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) Quickly, Ren used the Force to reduce the effects of the wound, lest it may result in his premature death.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) Chewbacca killed several other stormtroopers in the area as Rey and Finn, who were high above in the oscillator, began firing into the area as well. The Wookiee then ignited charges that he and Solo set throughout the oscillator, causing a massive explosion that breached the oscillator and gave Dameron and the remaining Resistance pilots an opportunity to destroy it. As Ren composed himself from his injury, he made [eye](/wiki/Eye "Eye") contact with Finn and Rey. Anger swelling within him, he was resolved to find them before they could escape.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

#### Duel in the forest

:   "*We're not done yet.*"  
    "*You're a monster.*"  
    "*It's just us now. Han Solo can't save you.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren and Rey[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)
