 [![Ren pursued Rey and Finn into the forest despite the wound he sustained from Chewbacca's bowcaster.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/64/Enrage-Awakenings.png/revision/latest?cb=20191202022901) [![Ren pursued Rey and Finn into the forest despite the wound he sustained from Chewbacca's bowcaster.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/64/Enrage-Awakenings.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191202022901)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/64/Enrage-Awakenings.png/revision/latest?cb=20191202022901) 

Ren pursued Rey and Finn into the forest despite the wound he sustained from Chewbacca's bowcaster.

 

Ren followed Rey and Finn into the forest outside of the oscillator, as they made their way back to the nearby *Millennium Falcon*. He confronted them, lightsaber drawn, and said that they still had unfinished business from which Han Solo could not save them. Outraged by Ren's patricidal actions, Rey denounced the dark warrior as a monster and tried to attack him with her blaster, but he used the Force to throw her into a tree and knock her unconscious. Now it was just Ren and the traitor who had earned his ire.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

Finn ignited the [Skywalker lightsaber](/wiki/Skywalker_lightsaber "Skywalker lightsaber") that had been given to him for safekeeping by Maz Kanata—a lightsaber that once belonged to Luke Skywalker, and to Anakin before him. Ren demanded that Finn give him the lightsaber, claiming it belonged to him, but instead the former stormtrooper engaged him in a lightsaber duel. It was a short but brutal contest, in which Ren kept striking his bowcaster injury in order to fuel his anger and power. In the end, Finn, who nonetheless landed one blow on Ren's right shoulder, was no match for Ren's power. Ren overwhelmed and disarmed his opponent, ending the fight with a punch and a lightsaber blow across Finn's back that left the one-time stormtrooper comatose.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

With the duel seemingly over, Ren turned his attention towards his grandfather's lightsaber and attempted to use the Force to draw it into his hand. Instead, it flew past him and landed in the hands of Rey, who used the Force to call it to her—as it was her destiny to wield the lightsaber of Anakin Skywalker. Rey ignited the weapon and engaged Ren in a tense duel. At first, Ren had the upper hand, remaining on the offensive as he pressed his attack against the retreating scavenger. Their blades became locked, and Ren told the emerging Force-sensitive that she needed a teacher. It was he, Ren said, who could show her the ways of the Force. At that moment, Rey realized she could call upon the powers of the Force and began using that to her advantage.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) Unaware, Rey instead gave in to her raw power, anger[[67]](#cite_note-Rey_Bio_Gallery-67) rage,[[54]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_Bio_Gallery-54) and fury.[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39) She turned the tide of the fight and pushed her own offensive against the dark warrior, who she was finally able to disarm.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) Ren realized that he dueled an opponent with more anger than he, or with an emotion that he didn't even recognize anymore.[[68]](#cite_note-TFA_junior_novel-68) In doing so, she slashed her blade across his face, knocking him down and disfiguring him in the process.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

 [![Although Ren initially had the upper hand, Rey defeated him by embracing the power of the Force.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/Rey_vs_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20160303172711) [![Although Ren initially had the upper hand, Rey defeated him by embracing the power of the Force.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/Rey_vs_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160303172711)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c3/Rey_vs_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20160303172711) 

Although Ren initially had the upper hand, Rey defeated him by embracing the power of the Force.

 

Phasma briefly bore witness to Ren and Rey's duel but did not provide aid to the dark side warrior, as she was busy [searching](/wiki/Hunt_for_Rivas "Hunt for Rivas") for the officer she had framed for the fall of Starkiller Base, [Sol Rivas](/wiki/Sol_Rivas "Sol Rivas").[[69]](#cite_note-Captain_Phasma_1-69) With Rey having rejected an amorphous, dark voice in her mind that demanded she kill Ren,[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39) the young woman and Ren were separated for long enough that, before they could engage any further, the surface of the planet began to break apart—the Resistance was victorious, and the destruction of the oscillator triggered the Starkiller's implosion. Ren and Rey were separated by a deep chasm, so Rey left the dark warrior behind, recovered Finn, and fled the planet with Chewbacca aboard the *Millennium Falcon*.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

As the planet continued to collapse, Snoke ordered General Hux to find Ren and bring the young knight before the Supreme Leader so the young warrior's training could be completed.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) Hux and several troopers tracked Ren's signal and took him aboard a shuttle, leaving before the planet exploded.[[68]](#cite_note-TFA_junior_novel-68) Immediately following Starkiller Base's destruction, Ren received treatment for the long scars on his body, though it was too late to erase them completely.[[43]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-43)

### Let the past die

#### A child in a mask

:   "*Yes. There it is. You have too much of your father's heart in you, young Solo.*"  
    "*I* killed *Han Solo. When the moment came I didn't hesitate.*"  
    "*And look at you. The deed split your spirit to the bone.*"
:   ―Snoke and Kylo Ren[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

 [![Ren remained at war within himself, having sustained hidden emotional wounds in addition to physical ones.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1f/Supreme_Leader_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20180224092636) [![Ren remained at war within himself, having sustained hidden emotional wounds in addition to physical ones.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1f/Supreme_Leader_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180224092636)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1f/Supreme_Leader_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20180224092636) 

Ren remained at war within himself, having sustained hidden emotional wounds in addition to physical ones.

 

Following the Resistance's [evacuation](/wiki/Battle_of_D%27Qar "Battle of D'Qar") of the base on D'Qar, Ren was summoned to Supreme Leader Snoke's [throne room](/wiki/Snoke%27s_throne_room "Snoke's throne room") on the *Supremacy*.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) The blows inflicted on him, by Rey and Chewbacca, though stitched up some by [microsutures](/wiki/Microsutures "Microsutures"), were still as fresh as ever, causing him some discomfort,[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) though he tried to hide this. Kneeling before his master, he listened as Snoke loudly recalled the raw, untamed power that Ren possessed, abilities which had originally brought him to the dark sider's attention. Knowing the potential of the powerful Skywalker bloodline, the Supreme Leader revealed his belief that Ren could fulfill his grandfather's dark legacy.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

But in light of his apprentice's most recent setback, Snoke retracted his faith in Ren's power.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) He chastised the dark warrior, calling him weak and sentimental,[[4]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_DB-4) just like his late father.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) The struggle within Ren as he prepared to strike down Han Solo had been sensed by Snoke from afar.[[70]](#cite_note-Last_Jedi_1-70) It was the trauma from this action that caused him to be outmatched by an untrained scavenger, who had never before wielded a lightsaber. Snoke had never seen such a pathetic display.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

 [![Ren's failure cost him the respect of his Master Snoke, who derided his apprentice as a sentimental child hiding in a mask.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b7/I_gave_everything_I_have_to_you.png/revision/latest?cb=20180820060812) [![Ren's failure cost him the respect of his Master Snoke, who derided his apprentice as a sentimental child hiding in a mask.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b7/I_gave_everything_I_have_to_you.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180820060812)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b7/I_gave_everything_I_have_to_you.png/revision/latest?cb=20180820060812) 

Ren's failure cost him the respect of his Master Snoke, who derided his apprentice as a sentimental child hiding in a mask.

 

Fury building within him, Ren rose to attack his master, but Snoke quickly suppressed the attack with a surge of [lightning](/wiki/Force_lightning "Force lightning"), throwing the dark side apprentice back. As long as Luke Skywalker lived, Snoke seethed—as long as the Jedi remained—so did hope across the galaxy. Ren would never be able to destroy it because he was a mere child hiding in a mask—nothing like the feared Darth Vader,[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) who would have been ashamed of his grandson.[[70]](#cite_note-Last_Jedi_1-70) Leaving the throne room, Ren erupted in a rage of self-pity and smashed his helmet against the surrounding metal. He then ordered his ship to be readied, resuming his quest to eradicate the Resistance.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

#### Chasing the Resistance

:   "*Follow my lead.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren, to his wingmen[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

As Hux had anticipated through new tracking technology, the First Order armada emerged from hyperspace to find the Resistance fleet unprepared and defenseless in the [Oetchi system](/wiki/Oetchi_system "Oetchi system"). The [Battle of Oetchi](/wiki/Battle_of_Oetchi "Battle of Oetchi") commenced as the warship *Supremacy* led the charge, its powerful [turbolasers](/wiki/Turbolaser "Turbolaser") showering the fleet with unyielding blasts. To complement the barrage, the *Supremacy* scrambled its short-distance fighters, with Ren spearheading the assault in his [personal TIE silencer](/wiki/Kylo_Ren%27s_TIE_silencer "Kylo Ren's TIE silencer"). Covered by [three wingmen](/wiki/Kylo_Ren%27s_personal_squadron "Kylo Ren's personal squadron"), until the third pilot was quickly destroyed, the dark apprentice intercepted the Resistance's [MC85 Star Cruiser](/wiki/MC85_Star_Cruiser "MC85 Star Cruiser") [*Raddus*](/wiki/Raddus_(MC85_Star_Cruiser) "Raddus (MC85 Star Cruiser)"), capital ship of the fleet. Before the rebel pilots could launch a counterattack, he destroyed the *Raddus* hangar, leaving them unable to resist the fighter wing.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

 [![Ren sensed his mother's presence as he led a starfighter strike mission against her flagship during the Battle of Oetchi.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/Kylo_Ren_Pilots_Silencer.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180106202404) [![Ren sensed his mother's presence as he led a starfighter strike mission against her flagship during the Battle of Oetchi.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/Kylo_Ren_Pilots_Silencer.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/267?cb=20180106202404)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/Kylo_Ren_Pilots_Silencer.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180106202404) 

Ren sensed his mother's presence as he led a starfighter strike mission against her flagship during the Battle of Oetchi.

 

With the Resistance flagship crippled, Ren turned his fighter to face the bridge of the craft, readying his rockets. At this moment he sensed his mother's presence aboard the *Raddus*—with his mother likewise sensing him too—and Ren, hesitating, held his thumb over the trigger in a moment of intense doubt. After a moment, he surrendered to his second thoughts and abandoned the trigger control. His [wingmen](/wiki/Poldin_LeHuse "Poldin LeHuse"), however, had no such qualms; ever loyal to the First Order, they launched their rockets in Ren's place upon the bridge.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

Ren watched the detonation with astonishment.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) He reached out again, but could not feel Organa anywhere. He believed that if he had had enough time, if he had not been taken by surprise, he would have protected his mother with the Force. Now, however, he had to conclude that she had died, along with all those present on the *Raddus*' bridge.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

Following this last offensive, Hux ordered the fighters back to the *Supremacy*, as the Resistance fleet had pulled out of the *Supremacy*'s protective radius in the intervening time. Ren, with his wingmen being blown up around him, had no other recourse but to comply.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

#### A growing connection

:   "*I'd never felt so alone.*"  
    "*You're not alone.*"  
    "*Neither are you. It isn't too late.*"
:   ―Rey and Kylo Ren[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

 [![Ren's mysterious connection with Rey grew more powerful with time, until they could see and hear each other across light-years.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/Why_is_the_Force_connecting_us.png/revision/latest?cb=20180511110442) [![Ren's mysterious connection with Rey grew more powerful with time, until they could see and hear each other across light-years.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/Why_is_the_Force_connecting_us.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180511110442)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/Why_is_the_Force_connecting_us.png/revision/latest?cb=20180511110442) 

Ren's mysterious connection with Rey grew more powerful with time, until they could see and hear each other across light-years.

 

As the First Order pursued the Resistance fleet, Ren was being treated for the injury he had taken to his face, a medical droid removing the microsutures that had been attached to it, when he sensed a disturbance. Before he knew it, a vision of Rey appeared before him. Taken aback, Ren could only watch as Rey reached for her blaster and shot him. However, no shot injured him. The still-shocked Ren pursued Rey when she ran away and found her soon after and tried to use the mind trick to force Rey to bring Luke to him, only to realize that they weren't actually in the same location and that Rey had not [projected](/wiki/Force_projection "Force projection") her appearance to him as the effort would kill her. He even discovered that Rey had found Luke Skywalker and was now studying under him, although he could not discern where as he was unable to see Rey's surroundings.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) Whereas the aspiring Jedi regarded their [connection](/wiki/Force-bond "Force-bond") as an inconvenience, Ren was intrigued by his bond with the former scavenger and sought to better understand it.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

The bond between Ren and Rey was unprecedented in its strength and raw power.[[43]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-43) It also had an effect on Ren's churning emotions,[[54]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_Bio_Gallery-54) and as it grew stronger in the Force, Rey started gaining new insights into Ren, who,[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) to Rey's surprise, no longer tried to hide his feelings of pain and misery from her.[[67]](#cite_note-Rey_Bio_Gallery-67) It was because of the bond and her new understanding of Ren's pain that Rey came to suspect that their destinies were intertwined.[[71]](#cite_note-Rey-71) Ren eventually revealed his recollection of the night he forsook Skywalker's teachings—how he awoke to the sound of a lightsaber, held by his uncle who intended to murder Ben Solo in his sleep—shaking Rey's faith in her Jedi Master. Although Rey called him a liar,[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) she sensed no deception from Ren. He genuinely believed that his former mentor had betrayed him and intended to kill him while he was defenseless.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

 [![After touching hands, Rey sensed the light in Ren and sought to redeem him despite Skywalker's warning.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/44/Luke_interrupting_Rey_and_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20180731154143) [![After touching hands, Rey sensed the light in Ren and sought to redeem him despite Skywalker's warning.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/44/Luke_interrupting_Rey_and_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/262?cb=20180731154143)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/44/Luke_interrupting_Rey_and_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20180731154143) 

After touching hands, Rey sensed the light in Ren and sought to redeem him despite Skywalker's warning.

 

After failing to discover the fate of her parents, Rey sought out Ren through their bond because he understood what it was like to feel alone and lost.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) They comforted each other, insisting that neither was alone and in that moment they touched hands. Rey then beheld a vision of the future, leading her to believe that Ren was fated to renounce the dark side and return to the light,[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) like his grandfather before him.[[64]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-64)

As a result of what she saw, Rey became convinced that her adversary could be turned from the dark side of the Force. She left Skywalker on his sanctuary and traveled to the *Supremacy* to see Ren, her actions guided by the belief that Ben Solo could be redeemed with her help. By touching hands, however, Ren experienced a vision of his own and thereby discerned the truth of Rey's father and mother: they were no one, merely a pair of junk traders who sold their daughter for drinking money before ultimately dying and being buried in a pauper's grave in the Jakku desert.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) This discovery convinced Ren that Rey would turn to the dark side and stand with him as they moved to confront his master together.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

#### Destiny fulfilled

:   "*My worthy apprentice, son of darkness, heir apparent to Lord Vader. Where there was conflict, I now sense resolve; where there was weakness, strength. Complete your training and fulfill your* destiny*.*"
:   ―Snoke's final words to Kylo Ren[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

 [![Snoke sentenced Rey to die by Ren's hand, but the newly resolved acolyte had other ideas.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/TLJ_And_kills_his_true_enemy.png/revision/latest?cb=20190521203159) [![Snoke sentenced Rey to die by Ren's hand, but the newly resolved acolyte had other ideas.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/TLJ_And_kills_his_true_enemy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/258?cb=20190521203159)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ca/TLJ_And_kills_his_true_enemy.png/revision/latest?cb=20190521203159) 

Snoke sentenced Rey to die by Ren's hand, but the newly resolved acolyte had other ideas.

 

Ren's emotions were fully open to Rey, who could feel that his conflict had grown worse since he killed his father. Clinging to the good she sensed within Ren, she reached out to the former Ben Solo and revealed her conviction in the vision she had when they touched hands through the Force. Solo was not fated to continue bowing before Snoke. Redemption was his destiny; of that Rey was certain. Ren, however, revealed that he also beheld a vision that convinced him it would be Rey who turned, because he now knew the truth behind Rey's parentage. Just before they entered the throne room where the Supreme Leader awaited their arrival, Rey sensed that much of Ren's churning emotions were about her.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

Snoke, who proclaimed that his faith in Ren had been restored, began appraising Rey, who remained defiant in spite of her inability to resist the dark master's Force powers. Although Rey remained certain that Ren would turn, her mental defenses began to crumble when Snoke revealed that he had been responsible for the intermittent connections she experienced with the Supreme Leader's apprentice, a revelation which came as a shock to Ren as well. It had all been a plot to draw Rey, the means to find Luke Skywalker, right into Snoke's hands. Nevertheless, Ren remained silent as Rey screamed,[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) trying in vain to stop Snoke from invading her mind.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

 [![Ren accomplished what his grandfather could not: killing and usurping the dark master as ruler of the galaxy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Death_of_the_Supreme_Leader.png/revision/latest?cb=20180730043005) [![Ren accomplished what his grandfather could not: killing and usurping the dark master as ruler of the galaxy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Death_of_the_Supreme_Leader.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/258?cb=20180730043005)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Death_of_the_Supreme_Leader.png/revision/latest?cb=20180730043005) 

Ren accomplished what his grandfather could not: killing and usurping the dark master as ruler of the galaxy.

 

Upon discovering Skywalker's location, Snoke planned to wipe him out from above as soon as the more immediate enemy had been dealt with. Rey summoned Skywalker's lightsaber to her hand, only for Snoke to redirect the hilt onto her head; Ren, eyes shut, merely tilted his head to the right to avoid being struck by the flying object. The Supreme Leader revealed through his [oculus](/wiki/Oculus_(device) "Oculus (device)") the Resistance being picked off one by one as they tried to flee aboard [transports](/wiki/U-55_orbital_loadlifter "U-55 orbital loadlifter") for safety. All that Ren's mother had fought for would be destroyed by the *Supremacy*'s guns. In response, an enraged Rey pulled Ren's lightsaber into her hands and charged at Snoke, who effortlessly overpowered her. Ren watched the lightsaber fall out of Rey's grip and shut off, sliding on the floor back to its owner's feet.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

Snoke, who had grown weary of his oft-conflicted apprentice, exulted at the newfound resolve that he suddenly felt emanating from Ren. Having promised to kill Rey with the cruelest stroke, he immobilized Rey and gave Ren the chance to execute the girl who defeated him on Starkiller Base. Ren retrieved his lightsaber, stood up and stepped towards Rey.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) He knew what must be done[[54]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_Bio_Gallery-54) and, as Rey predicted, he did indeed turn against his master.[[67]](#cite_note-Rey_Bio_Gallery-67) Knowing that Snoke could sense his every intent, he turned his lightsaber to Rey while simultaneously his uncle's weapon rotated to face in Snoke's direction. Snoke, who became distracted by the desire to appreciate Rey's impending doom with the Force rather than the approximation afforded by mundane senses, believed that Ren was about to kill his true enemy—a status he wrongly attributed to Rey.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

 [![Ren and Rey stood back-to-back against the Supreme Leader's vengeful Praetorian Guards.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/ReyKyloVsGuards.png/revision/latest?cb=20220417200753) [![Ren and Rey stood back-to-back against the Supreme Leader's vengeful Praetorian Guards.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/ReyKyloVsGuards.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/269?cb=20220417200753)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/ReyKyloVsGuards.png/revision/latest?cb=20220417200753) 

Ren and Rey stood back-to-back against the Supreme Leader's vengeful Praetorian Guards.

 

With a hidden gesture from Ren's free hand, the blue energy blade of Skywalker's lightsaber sprang forth, spearing Snoke through his waist. Almost instantly, Snoke's control on Rey was lost. The blade, which was still under Ren's control, carved through Snoke, cutting him in half before returning to Rey's grasp. After a moment of locking eyes with each other, Ren and Rey stood back-to-back to receive the retaliation of the fallen Supreme Leader's [Elite Praetorian Guards](/wiki/Praetorian_Guard "Praetorian Guard"), who charged towards the Force-sensitive duo from all sides with the intent of avenging his death. Although the two were eventually separated and forced to contend with multiple guards on their own, they both held their own and continued to strike down one Praetorian after another. Ren, who felt both excitement and a hunger for battle, personally killed half the Guards on his own but was disarmed by his fifth opponent, causing Rey to throw the Skywalker lightsaber to him. He swiftly thumbed it on and off, letting the blade pierce through the last Praetorian's head.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

#### Convictions and rejections

:   "*It's time to let old things die. Snoke, Skywalker. The Sith, the Jedi, the Rebels… Let it all die. Rey, I want you to join me. We can rule together and bring a new order to the galaxy.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

 [![Ren urged Rey to let the past die and join him, but she refused.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d3/Mine_mine_mine.png/revision/latest?cb=20180419180936) [![Ren urged Rey to let the past die and join him, but she refused.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d3/Mine_mine_mine.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180419180936)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d3/Mine_mine_mine.png/revision/latest?cb=20180419180936) 

Ren urged Rey to let the past die and join him, but she refused.

 

Rey, who stared at Ren through eyes filled with joy, beseeched him to help her save the Resistance fleet. To her disbelief and horror, Ren proposed that he and Rey join together and "let old things die," including the Resistance, and bring a new order to the galaxy.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) Neither fear nor anger influenced his decision; he had chosen to continue down the dark path with a deep resolve.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) Rey begged Ren to not give into the dark side, but the latter stood behind his convictions. To his frustration, he could see that Rey was still clinging to that futile hope of hers. He urged her to "let go," to admit the truth about her parents—a truth she had always known but hidden away for years. Rey struggled to control her emotions as she admitted that she knew this, that her parents were simply "nobody," but the revelation that she came from nothing threatened to overwhelm her. At that moment, Ren called Rey "nothing," and said she was not that to him.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) Ren, who saw Rey as an ally in destroying the past he hated,[[4]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_DB-4) wanted the former scavenger to join him. Motioning her to take his hand, he pleaded with her to stay with him so that they could rule the galaxy together.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

However, Rey used the Force to summon the Skywalker lightsaber to her grasp,[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) just as she had when fighting Ren on Starkiller Base.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) Ren, his entreaty rejected, raised his own hand to harness the Force around the lightsaber, causing it to stop midflight. Neither Ren or Rey relented as both continued to call upon the Jedi weapon with equal determination.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) In the midst of their standoff, the lightsaber's kyber crystal wailed through the Force, seeking resonance and harmony where there was nothing but dissonance.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) The crystal ultimately sheared apart, unleashing a wave of energy that tore the lightsaber in half before consuming the throne room in a flash of brilliant, blinding light. In addition to rendering both Force users unconscious, the shock wave of Force energy coincided with the sacrifice of [Vice Admiral](/wiki/Vice_Admiral "Vice Admiral") [Amilyn Holdo](/wiki/Amilyn_Holdo "Amilyn Holdo"), who crashed the *Raddus* into the *Supremacy* at lightspeed, splitting the First Order flagship in half before it could destroy all of the Resistance transports.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

### The reign of Kylo Ren

#### The New Supreme Leader

:   "*Get all our forces down to that Resistance base. Let's finish this.*"  
    "*Finish this? Who do you think you're talking to? You presume to command my army? Our Supreme Leader is dead! We have no ruler—*"  
    "*The Supreme Leader is dead.*"  
    "*Long live the Supreme Leader.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren and Armitage Hux[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

 [![After Snoke's death, General Hux was forced to proclaim Ren the new Supreme Leader.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d7/Long_Live_The_Supreme_Leader.png/revision/latest?cb=20180709191925) [![After Snoke's death, General Hux was forced to proclaim Ren the new Supreme Leader.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d7/Long_Live_The_Supreme_Leader.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/255?cb=20180709191925)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d7/Long_Live_The_Supreme_Leader.png/revision/latest?cb=20180709191925) 

After Snoke's death, General Hux was forced to proclaim Ren the new Supreme Leader.

 

Ren regained consciousness shortly after Hux reached the throne room. Having killed the Supreme Leader and his guards, Ren falsely accused Rey of murder, claiming that she was the one responsible for Snoke's death. Hux, who had contemplated shooting the fallen knight before he awoke, informed Ren that the girl escaped from the *Supremacy* using Snoke's private shuttle.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) Realizing that Rey had awoken before him, Ren pondered why she had spared his life, knowing he was at her mercy while in an unconscious state. It then occurred to Ren that Rey did, in fact, care about him. Regardless, he dismissed it as a sign of sentimental weakness that would eventually lead to Rey's destruction.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

Knowing that Rey would travel to [Crait](/wiki/Crait "Crait") in an effort to save the Resistance,[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) Ren ordered Hux to send their forces to the planet where they would end the war and his mother's movement for good. Hux scoffed at the notion of taking orders from his longtime rival and reminded Ren that the [army](/wiki/First_Order_Army "First Order Army") answered to their general. In addition, he pointed out that, without a Supreme Leader, the First Order was cast into a state of disarray. Before he could go on, the General's protests were suddenly silenced by Ren, who aggressively [Force choked](/wiki/Force_choke "Force choke") Hux into submission. Overtaken by fear, Hux grudgingly pledged his allegiance to Ren, whom he hailed as Snoke's successor.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) Even so, Ren remained distrustful of Hux and chose to keep the General close by as a safeguard against treachery.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

#### Battle of Crait

:   "*General Hux, advance. No quarter, no prisoners.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren, to Armitage Hux[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

 [![Ren led the First Order's assault on the Resistance's last redoubt, determined to end his mother's movement.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/SuperlaserSiegeCanonAdvance-TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20250215055646) [![Ren led the First Order's assault on the Resistance's last redoubt, determined to end his mother's movement.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/SuperlaserSiegeCanonAdvance-TLJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20250215055646)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/SuperlaserSiegeCanonAdvance-TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20250215055646) 

Ren led the First Order's assault on the Resistance's last redoubt, determined to end his mother's movement.

 

As far as the new Supreme Leader was concerned, the [Battle of Crait](/wiki/Battle_of_Crait "Battle of Crait") would prove to be the final battle in the war between the First Order and the Resistance. He would give no quarter to his enemies, nor take a single prisoner. Looming overhead in his command shuttle, Ren oversaw the deployment of [AT-ATs](/wiki/First_Order_All_Terrain_Armored_Transport "First Order All Terrain Armored Transport"), [AT-M6s](/wiki/All_Terrain_MegaCaliber_Six "All Terrain MegaCaliber Six"), and [AT-STs](/wiki/First_Order_All_Terrain_Scout_Transport "First Order All Terrain Scout Transport") to the salt-covered surface of Crait, gathered from what remained of the *Supremacy*. It would be a relatively straightforward operation, with Ren's forces marching on an [abandoned rebel base](/wiki/Crait_outpost "Crait outpost") which the Resistance had appropriated for its defense.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

When the First Order discovered a massive shield door impeding their advance into the enclosure, Ren further deployed a [superlaser siege cannon](/wiki/Superlaser_siege_cannon "Superlaser siege cannon")—a device likened to a battering ram that was equipped with miniaturized [Death Star](/wiki/Death_Star "Death Star") technology—to his advantage. In response, the Resistance launched a number of old [ski speeders](/wiki/V-4X-D_ski_speeder "V-4X-D ski speeder"), an ultimately futile attempt to stop the cannon. While the Resistance attempted to halt the First Order's progress, Chewbacca and Rey joined the fray in the *Millennium Falcon*, and Ren furiously sent every TIE fighter present to destroy his father's old ship.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

#### Showdown with Luke Skywalker

:   "*I'll destroy her, and you, and all of it.*"  
    "*No. Strike me down in anger and I'll always be with you. Just like your father.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren and Luke Skywalker[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

 [![Ren challenged his uncle Luke Skywalker to single combat, intending to finish what Darth Vader began by killing the last Jedi.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1f/Family_Reunion.png/revision/latest?cb=20250215054710) [![Ren challenged his uncle Luke Skywalker to single combat, intending to finish what Darth Vader began by killing the last Jedi.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1f/Family_Reunion.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/262?cb=20250215054710)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1f/Family_Reunion.png/revision/latest?cb=20250215054710) 

Ren challenged his uncle Luke Skywalker to single combat, intending to finish what Darth Vader began by killing the last Jedi.

 

Shortly after the First Order breached the base, Luke Skywalker appeared and Ren, in a futile attempt to eliminate his uncle, ordered all of his forces to fire at him. After Skywalker shrugged off the attack virtually unharmed, Ren ordered his command shuttle to be set down. Hux tried to advise him against what he considered a waste of time, but Ren thrashed the General against the wall with the Force, knocking him unconscious. The nearby pilot needed no further prodding and complied with the command.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

The time had come for Ren to face Skywalker personally. He slowly advanced until he was but a few meters from the old Jedi. He tauntingly asked if Skywalker had come to be his salvation. Skywalker answered half-heartedly in the negative. Then lightsabers were drawn. Skywalker made no effort to harm his nephew and only moved to avoid Ren's attacks. He apologized for failing in his duty as Ben Solo's mentor, but Ren took it with sarcasm and declared that the war had ended with the death of the Resistance. In addition, he stated that Skywalker would die as well, marking the end of the Jedi Order itself. He was wrong on all counts, according to Skywalker: the war had just begun, the Rebellion was reborn, and he would not die as the last of the Jedi.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

Ren felt that Skywalker was talking about Rey, the old man's supposed "chosen one."[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) He vowed that he would see her annihilated, along with Skywalker and the remnants of the Resistance. In response, Skywalker deactivated his lightsaber and warned his nephew against striking him down in anger, promising that he would always be with Ren, just like Han Solo. It was thus that he opened himself up for the final blow. Enraged, Ren charged at Skywalker once more until he slashed through him with no effect. Confused, he pointed his lightsaber in the Jedi Master's direction and moved forward until the blade harmlessly passed through his uncle again, revealing that Skywalker was not actually present for the battle; he had been [projecting himself](/wiki/Force_projection "Force projection") through the Force from Ahch-To. With one final chiding goodbye, the image vanished.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

 [![Rey chose to shut Ren out when the Force reconnected them, leaving the Supreme Leader alone and unable to revel in his achievements.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5a/Kylo_Ren_looking_at_Rey.png/revision/latest?cb=20180730014630) [![Rey chose to shut Ren out when the Force reconnected them, leaving the Supreme Leader alone and unable to revel in his achievements.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5a/Kylo_Ren_looking_at_Rey.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20180730014630)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5a/Kylo_Ren_looking_at_Rey.png/revision/latest?cb=20180730014630) 

Rey chose to shut Ren out when the Force reconnected them, leaving the Supreme Leader alone and unable to revel in his achievements.

 

At that moment, Ren realized what had his uncle had done: by distracting him, the old Jedi had bought time for the remaining members of the Resistance to escape. Hux had been right all along. Angered by the deception, Ren, Hux, and their forces scoured the now-empty base, but finding only a projection of his father's golden hanging dice, all Ren could do was kneel in defeat as they vanished from his hand. As the Resistance evacuated, Ren saw Rey once more as she boarded the *Millennium Falcon*; no words were said as she closed the door on him,[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) although Ren sensed that Rey felt neither hatred nor compassion for him.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) Both knew that this struggle between them was far from concluded.[[72]](#cite_note-TLJ_Adaptation_6-72) Ren had become the Supreme Leader, all but destroyed his mother's Resistance and struck down his uncle on the battlefield of Crait, but it did not feel like a victory to Ren.[[54]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_Bio_Gallery-54)

After Crait, Rey and Organa discussed Ren and his actions. Rey wanted to understand him and how Ren had turned to the dark side, but Organa told Rey that she would need to ask Ren to know. Rey told the general that Ren wanted her to join him and that, while she thought she could help him, all he had wanted was for her to be like him. Organa could see that Rey cared about her son and also that he had disappointed her, so she informed the young Jedi that Ren had made his decisions, adding that the only person who could save him was himself, but Organa was unsure if that was what her son wanted. Rey understood this, but she had held onto hope, although Organa believed that hope was a good trait.[[73]](#cite_note-Resistance_Reborn-73)

#### The legacy of Darth Vader

##### The dark prince

:   "*I thought I wanted to follow your path. You were the one I thought I understood. I thought I was your* legacy*. But I'm not you.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren, to Darth Vader's mask[[74]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_1-74)

 [![Kylo Ren proclaimed the end of Snoke's era and the beginning of his reign as the new Supreme Leader of the First Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6b/SupremeLeaderKyloRen-LegacyOfVader1.png/revision/latest?cb=20250208063758) [![Kylo Ren proclaimed the end of Snoke's era and the beginning of his reign as the new Supreme Leader of the First Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6b/SupremeLeaderKyloRen-LegacyOfVader1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250208063758)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6b/SupremeLeaderKyloRen-LegacyOfVader1.png/revision/latest?cb=20250208063758) 

Kylo Ren proclaimed the end of Snoke's era and the beginning of his reign as the new Supreme Leader of the First Order.

 

Shortly after the Battle of Crait, Ren boarded the *Finalizer* in space to meet Hux and many organized squads of stormtroopers and other First Order personnel. Ren introduced himself as the new Supreme Leader of the First Order by revealing Snoke's bisected corpse, using the Force to lift the remains into the air for his audience to see. Still asserting that the Resistance killed Snoke, Ren released Snoke's body into the vacuum of space while claiming he would bring the First Order to glory.[[74]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_1-74)

After his display of power, Ren reminisced alone about recent events and his encounters and memories with his father, mother, Snoke, and Rey. Though trying to affirm to himself that the past did not matter and that it was done, he could not let go of the images of those who were once close to him. Sending for Hux, Ren met with the General, telling him that he was a trusted advisor and that he needed advisement on military matters, which Snoke did not often discuss with Ren. Though Hux confirmed that Snoke had his plans, he implored Ren to take his own military direction as he now commanded the First Order's military. When Hux suggested that Ren fulfill the dreams of their forebears and rebuild the Empire, Ren told Hux that his own forebears shaped the known galaxy while Hux's bloodline produced lesser "lieutenants and lickspittles."[[74]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_1-74)

The two then conferred on resources, with Hux elaborating that they needed more ships as Starkiller Base's destruction left them without a shipyard and the Resistance's [unusual tactics](/wiki/Holdo_maneuver "Holdo maneuver") at the Battle of Oetchi destroyed the *Supremacy* and much of their fleet. With the destruction of the New Republic at Hosnian Prime and the dismantling of the Resistance, however, Hux believed the First Order would face little resistance other than local militias for their ambitions of conquest. Ren cut Hux's deliberations short, as he had not ordered him to perform any military action, instead ordering that a [throne](/wiki/Throne "Throne") be built for himself. Though Ren suggested that the throne could be anything he liked, such as one made of [aurodium](/wiki/Aurodium "Aurodium"), Ren told Hux to choose and to do nothing else until Ren had a worthy throne, cautioning Hux to get it right the first time.[[74]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_1-74)

##### The fires of Mustafar

:   "*You are the past. Darth Vader is the past. This entire* place *is the past. The past* strangles *me. Its expectations and legacies and vendettas. I will destroy every last vestige of it. I will* free myself*.*"  
    "*You foolish, ignorant* child*. Vader's power* was *his past.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren and Vaneé[[74]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_1-74)

 [![Ren visited his grandfather's fortress on Mustafar, where he encountered a Sith cult known as the Alazmec of Winsit.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/KyloAgainstCultists-LegacyOfVader1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250311010957) [![Ren visited his grandfather's fortress on Mustafar, where he encountered a Sith cult known as the Alazmec of Winsit.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/KyloAgainstCultists-LegacyOfVader1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250311010957)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/KyloAgainstCultists-LegacyOfVader1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250311010957) 

Ren visited his grandfather's fortress on Mustafar, where he encountered a Sith cult known as the Alazmec of Winsit.

 

Ren returned to solitude to confer with his grandfather's mask, questioning how Vader could have ruled for so long over weaklings and been satisfied. Ren asserted that he was not Vader, or his uncle, mother or father, and reaffirmed that though he had killed his past, he still was not free of it. He concluded the answer to be that his work killing the past was not complete, and that he would start with the burdensome legacy of his grandfather. Ren [traveled](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar_(Kylo_Ren) "Mission to Mustafar (Kylo Ren)") to [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar"), the [volcanic](/wiki/Volcano "Volcano") [throneworld](/wiki/Throneworld "Throneworld") of his late grandfather, in his [TIE silencer](/wiki/TIE/vn_space_superiority_fighter "TIE/vn space superiority fighter"). As he approached [Fortress Vader](/wiki/Fortress_Vader "Fortress Vader"), he was confronted by three warriors of the [Alazmec of Winsit](/wiki/Alazmec_of_Winsit "Alazmec of Winsit"),[[74]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_1-74) a [group](/wiki/Sith_cult "Sith cult") of [Sith cultists](/wiki/Sith_cultist "Sith cultist") that colonized Mustafar's [Corvax Fen](/wiki/Corvax_Fen "Corvax Fen")[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) region near the castle grounds of [Fortress](/wiki/Fortress "Fortress") Vader.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) One of the warriors fired an [arrow](/wiki/Arrow "Arrow") at Ren, who halted it inches from his face by use of the Force. Ren used his lightsaber to cut down his attackers, goading the remaining [Alazmec](/wiki/Alazmec "Alazmec") warriors to attack him and further pontificating on his importance. One of the warriors wounded Ren in the midsection. As Ren approached the entrance to the fortress, [blood](/wiki/Blood "Blood") from his wound would fall onto the [stone](/wiki/Stone "Stone"), detecting Vader's blood and opening for the dark warrior.[[74]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_1-74)

 [![Vaneé persuaded Ren to follow Vader's example by transforming the pain of his past into a source of dark power.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a7/RenSeesHologramOfVader-LegacyOfVader1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250311135508) [![Vaneé persuaded Ren to follow Vader's example by transforming the pain of his past into a source of dark power.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a7/RenSeesHologramOfVader-LegacyOfVader1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250311135508)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a7/RenSeesHologramOfVader-LegacyOfVader1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250311135508) 

Vaneé persuaded Ren to follow Vader's example by transforming the pain of his past into a source of dark power.

 

Ren was greeted by [Vaneé](/wiki/Vane%C3%A9 "Vaneé"), Vader's servant in life, now reduced to a head affixed inside a droid body. Asking about Ren's connection to Vader, Ren confirmed that Vader was his grandfather. When Vaneé asked how he might best serve Ren, Ren threatened him with death, to which Vaneé confirmed his similarity to Vader, asking why Ren might kill him. Ren claimed that Vaneé, like Vader and the fortress, represented the past, which strangled Ren with its expectations, legacies and vendettas. Vaneé, amused, called Ren foolish and ignorant, offering that Vader's past was what gave him his power. Showing Ren a hologram of Vader, Vaneé told how Vader never let go of his past, which was what made him so powerful in the dark side of the Force. After contemplating Vaneé's words, Ren deactivated his saber and demanded his new servant to show him more of Vader's past.[[74]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_1-74)

##### The sands of Tatooine

At the behest of Vaneé, Ren would [travel](/wiki/Mission_to_Tatooine_(Kylo_Ren) "Mission to Tatooine (Kylo Ren)") with his new servant to [Mos Espa](/wiki/Mos_Espa "Mos Espa") on the planet [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine"),[[75]](#cite_note-Mark2-75) where his grandfather spent his early days. Though Ren did not at first understand the planet's importance, Vaneé insisted that Vader's past experiences on the desert world, such as meeting [his future wife](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala"), joining the Jedi Order, losing [his mother](/wiki/Shmi_Skywalker_Lars "Shmi Skywalker Lars"), and using the dark side of the Force for the first time when [slaughtering](/wiki/Mission_to_rescue_Shmi_Skywalker_Lars "Mission to rescue Shmi Skywalker Lars") a [village](/wiki/Unidentified_Tusken_village "Unidentified Tusken village") of [Tuskens](/wiki/Tusken_Raider "Tusken Raider"), were key to his dark journey. Vaneé took Ren to Mos Espa's [Grand Arena](/wiki/Mos_Espa_Grand_Arena "Mos Espa Grand Arena"), where one of Anakin Skywalker's greatest triumphs took place: his [victory](/wiki/Boonta_Eve_Classic_(32_BBY) "Boonta Eve Classic (32 BBY)") in the [Boonta Eve Classic](/wiki/Boonta_Eve_Classic "Boonta Eve Classic") as an untrained child and a [slave](/wiki/Slavery "Slavery"), in which he was the only human to ever win. Ren did not at first believe that his grandfather was once a slave, but did believe that the Jedi would not take in Skywalker's mother. Vaneé speculated that like Vader, Ren's life was also one of prolonged pain, and though Ren quietly reflected on happy memories he shared with his family throughout his childhood, he agreed.[[76]](#cite_note-:0-76)

A trio of desert thugs approached Ren and Vaneé, having overheard the name "Skywalker", claiming to have heard that Luke Skywalker had recently took out an entire First Order fleet. The thugs then raised weapons, threatening to rob the duo of their [credits](/wiki/Credits "Credits"). Using the Force, Ren manipulated the bodies of two of the thugs to point ther blasters at their allies, killing two of them. Ren told the lone survivor to spread the word that talking of Luke Skywalker could get one killed. Using his lightsaber to erase Anakin Skywalker's name from the arena's wall, Ren asked Vaneé who owned his grandfather.[[76]](#cite_note-:0-76)

Vaneé brought Ren to the ruined [junk shop](/wiki/Watto%27s_junkshop "Watto's junkshop") of [Watto](/wiki/Watto "Watto"), the [Toydarian](/wiki/Toydarian "Toydarian") who owned Skywalker as a boy. Ren assumed that Vader must have returned to the shop to take revenge on Watto, but Vaneé denied this, as Vader was focused on other things. Vaneé did confirm that Watto acquired Skywalker from [Gardulla Besadii the Elder](/wiki/Gardulla_Besadii_the_Elder "Gardulla Besadii the Elder"), who still lived. Hoping to erase this part of his grandfather's story, Ren acquired a speeder and travelled to Gardulla's [palace](/wiki/Gardulla_the_Hutt%27s_Palace "Gardulla the Hutt's Palace"). After killing the guards and their [rancors](/wiki/Rancor "Rancor"), Ren entered the palace to meet the [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt "Hutt"). Assuming that Ren was sent by an employer to keep her criminal empire in check, Ren drew his lightsaber and sought to take revenge for Gardulla owning his grandfather. Though Ren deftly struck down the rest of Gardulla's guards, a small [being](/wiki/Unidentified_Force-sensitive_individual "Unidentified Force-sensitive individual") who sat at Gardulla's side took Ren's saber from him using the Force, claiming that the Force was weak with Ren. Gardulla revealed that she had taken precautions against Force-sensitive intruders after [Jabba Desilijic Tiure's](/wiki/Jabba_Desilijic_Tiure "Jabba Desilijic Tiure") [fate](/wiki/Rescue_of_Han_Solo "Rescue of Han Solo") thirty years prior. Gardulla had her guards incapacitate Ren and chain him in a dungeon, keeping him prisoner, taunting that Ren's grandfather's story was now his story too.[[76]](#cite_note-:0-76)

Later awakening, Ren futilely implored Gardulla to release him, instead receiving repeated electric shocks. Calling Ren "nothing", Ren remembered telling the Jedi apprentice Rey something similar during the Battle of Oetchi shortly after killing Snoke and his Praetorian Guards. Failing to bargain with and threaten Gardulla, Ren was instead shocked repeatedly and told to obey. Eventually, Gardulla stopped at the behest of her Force-sensitive bodyguard, agreeing that Ren was more useful alive than dead. At the press of a button, Ren's chamber became filled with a noxious red gas, causing him to dream in visions. In these visions, Ren witnessed Vader slaughtering many Rebel Alliance troops. Asking Vader for help, Vader only replied that everything that had made him magnificent, he had accomplished alone. Heeding Vader's words, Ren awakened and goaded Gardulla into causing him more pain, giving him the dark side power needed to free himself and destroy Gardulla's dungeon.[[76]](#cite_note-:0-76)

Wandering the suns-scorched desert, Ren encountered a [Canyon Krayt dragon](/wiki/Canyon_krayt_dragon "Canyon krayt dragon"), slaying it without a weapon and fashioning its hide into clothing. Attacking two other desert wanderers, Ren used their communications equipment to order the *Finalizer* to Tatooine. Finding a [dewback](/wiki/Dewback "Dewback"), Ren relocated Gardulla's fortress, ordering General Armitage Hux to hit his given location with a full spread of weapons in twenty minutes. Ren rushed the fortress, once again dispatching guards, reclaiming his lightsaber and escaping shortly before Hux carried out the attack.[[76]](#cite_note-:0-76)

Later, Ren met with Vaneé via hologram aboard the *Finalizer*, the latter having feared the worst after hearing of the First Order attack. Vaneé asked if Ren's understanding of Vader and his power had grown on Tatooine; Ren confirmed that it had, with there being power and purity in his being alone. Pleased, Vaneé told Ren that there was still more to be shown about Vader's life and legacy, and after confirming that their adventures would continue, told Ren that he would await him at the island of [Varykino](/wiki/Varykino "Varykino") on the planet [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo").[[76]](#cite_note-:0-76)

##### The waters of Naboo

Ren met Vaneé on Naboo at the ruined [Varykino Villa](/wiki/Varykino_Villa "Varykino Villa"), struggling to comprehend its importance as he did with Mos Espa on Tatooine. Vaneé regaled Ren with tales of Naboo's former glory, detailing its history as a powerful cultural hub with a [democratic monarchy](/wiki/Royal_House_of_Naboo "Royal House of Naboo"). Vaneé shared his knowledge of powerful individuals that once inhabited Naboo, such as [Marlowe](/wiki/Marlowe_San_Tekka "Marlowe San Tekka") and [Vellis](/wiki/Vellis_San_Tekka "Vellis San Tekka") [San Tekka](/wiki/San_Tekka_clan "San Tekka clan"), but especially Emperor Sheev Palpatine, explaining that Naboo fell into chaos and disrepair after the Galactic Civil War as galaxy felt that Naboo's citizens had profited from their association with Palpatine. Growing impatient, Ren did not see the importance of the dead Emperor's past. Vaneé explained that Naboo was where Vader fell in love with and wedded Ren's grandmother, Padmé Amidala, [Queen of Naboo](/wiki/Monarch_of_Naboo "Monarch of Naboo") and [Galactic Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator"). Though Ren rejected the idea of falling in love for the sake of power, Vaneé further explained that it was the loss of Padmé that granted Vader his dark power; his lack of limits for attachments allowed the Sith Lord strength and focus. Though Ren claimed to have no limits, Vaneé asked if Ren already had everything he needed and desired, causing Ren to once again reflect on his hopeful ally, Rey.[[77]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_4-77)

Their conversation was interrupted by a [man](/wiki/Sanga%27s_companion "Sanga's companion") and [woman](/wiki/Sanga "Sanga") in a boat, telling the two that the villa was cursed. At Ren's behest, the two explained that fifty years ago, a queen lived at the villa and returned dead under mysterious circumstances. They claimed that a "spirit of death" then came to the villa, destroying all memory of the queen and haunting Naboo, causing death to all who spoke of or even acknowledged her existence. Ren dismissed their superstition, but the two further explained that the story caused Naboo's elite to leave that part of Naboo, leaving "bad people" in their place. At that moment, [Storg Veruna](/wiki/Storg_Veruna "Storg Veruna") and his enforcers arrived, unhappy with the presence of trespassers on his property. In hand-to-hand combat, Ren dispatched Veruna and his guards easily, but the two visitors reacted in dismay, as the other Verunas, once a ruling family of Naboo who laid claim to much of the planet by force, would return to retaliate. As the two visitors fled in their boat, Ren told Vaneé that he was wrong, that Vader recognized that Naboo was a memory unworthy of his legacy, which led to its destruction. Finding the people of Naboo foolish in their obsession with the past, Ren used the Force to kill the two fleeing visitors. Though, Ren cryptically reflected that he could help Naboo.[[77]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_4-77)

Two days later, Ren met with Armitage Hux aboard the *Finalizer*. Asking the General if the First Order could still destroy a planet with the loss of both Starkiller Base and the *Supremacy*, Hux said that fully destroying a planet would be difficult, but that the First Order's present military forces were sufficient to raze a planet clear of all structures and life given enough time; Ren was pleased to hear this, hinting that he possibly had a planet in mind to destroy. Asking about the status of his throne, Ren left the bridge before a frustrated Hux could finish explaining its ongoing progress. Having commandeered Naboo's communications network, Ren announced to the planet that he was unimpressed with them and their obsessions with lineage and superstition, announcing himself as King of Naboo to help them embrace the future.[[77]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_4-77)

After deploying invasion forces to locations such as the city of [Spinnaker](/wiki/Spinnaker "Spinnaker"), Ren oversaw the invasions with Hux, who asked why Ren was invading the world and declaring himself its king. Ren simply stated that he was the Supreme Leader, meaning that he was already Naboo's king. Supplicant, Hux elaborated that there were other targets that would make better use of their military resources, such as [Corellia](/wiki/Corellia "Corellia"), which could serve as a much needed shipyard. At Ren's inquisition, Hux confirmed that the Naboo were not fighting back in any significant way, drawing his interest.[[78]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_5-78)

Ren traveled to the surface of Naboo to Spinnaker, disguised as an insurgent. Attacking a group of stormtroopers and an [Urban Assault Triped Transport](/wiki/Urban_Assault_Triped_Transport "Urban Assault Triped Transport"), Ren destroyed the entire force, leaving the citizens of Naboo dumbfounded. Ren offered to show them how he was able to accomplish such feats, leading them to an underground tunnel. There, he informed the citizens of recent First Order losses, though he dismissed claims of victory at the hands of Luke Skywalker and Leia Organa as propaganda, claiming that the Resistance was decimated and meaningless. Some of the citizens wondered if Kylo Ren might make a benign ruler, as Naboo survived occupation by the Empire, but the disguised Ren asserted that Kylo Ren would take everything they had.[[78]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_5-78)

Using his knowledge of the Rebellion, Ren would lead the citizens in a resistance effort against the First Order forces, which were unaccustomed to guerilla tactics. Ren would meet with Hux over hologram, who, not knowing of Ren's charade, bemoaned small pockets of resistance but dismissed them as of little concern, further emphasizing that Ren's personal oversight may expedite the occupation. Ren approved Hux's plan of using a Siege Dreadnought to destroy the city of Spinnaker. Claiming to have a source inside the First Order, Ren informed his resistance cell of the plan, quelling doubts about their actions and determined that the people of Naboo should act to defend their homeworld. Commanding the battle against the Dreadnought from the ground, Ren oversaw a struggle between the Dreadnought and a force of kitbashed ships sourced from [N-1 starfighters](/wiki/N-1_starfighter "N-1 starfighter"), [T-70 X-wing fighters](/wiki/T-70_X-wing_starfighter "T-70 X-wing starfighter"), [TIE Reapers](/wiki/TIE/rp_Reaper_attack_lander "TIE/rp Reaper attack lander") and [TIE/ln fighters](/wiki/TIE/ln_space_superiority_starfighter "TIE/ln space superiority starfighter"). Having observed Ren's charade quietly for some time, Vaneé asked why Ren was doing what he was doing. Ren claimed to want to have the people of Naboo to evolve, but Vaneé saw through Ren, recognizing a Vader-like streak of self hatred in Ren, interpreting the bizarre charade as a way of attacking himself. Angered by this accusation, Ren lifted Vaneé's droid chassis off of the ground, partially dismantling it. Questioning Vaneé's ultimate usefulness, Vaneé told Ren of a vault at Vader's castle on Mustafar full of power, but that it could only be opened when Ren was ready. Though Ren threatened Vaneé, demanding that he take him to the vault immediately, Vaneé refused, preferring to die than pass Vader's legacy to someone unworthy. Vaneé implored Ren to find somewhere true to put his hate other than himself: a worthy enemy. Processing Vaneé's proposal, Ren ordered Hux to withdraw the Dreadnought from Naboo, seconds before it would be ready to destroy the city.[[78]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_5-78)

Believing they had fought off the First Order, the resistance fighters of Naboo returned underground to celebrate and thank the disguised Ren for leading them. After killing all of the Naboo citizens in his company, Ren ordered Vaneé to find him a worthy enemy, of which Vaneé already had one in mind.[[78]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_5-78)

##### The shipyards of Corellia

Following Ren and Hux's previous discussion, the First Order brought its forces to bear on Corellia. Despite Hux's control over the battle so far, Ren took it upon himself to personally fly into the fray in his personal TIE silencer. Exhibiting phenomenal flying skills and executing exceptionally tight maneuvers, Ren cleared a path to the heavily defended command center. Though this defied Hux's plan for the battle, which called for a seige anchored by ground troops, Hux did not interfere with his Supreme Leader's strategy. Though his wingmates failed to provide Ren with adequate cover, Ren successfully arrived at the command center and secured a victory for the First Order.[[79]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_6-79)

Shortly after the victory at Corellia, Ren sat before a procession of First Order stormtroopers on his newly completed throne. As his followers chanted for their Supreme Leader, Ren regarded Hux, who stood beside him, telling his General that he knew the display made Hux feel small, and that it was not his role to feel large. Ren left his throne, ordering Hux to Ren's chambers for an after-action report and commending Hux for the throne. Hux reported that the invasion was a complete success, and that Corellia's shipyard were ready to begin shoring up losses from Starkiller Base, Crait and Naboo. Ren dismissed Hux, but the General remained, hoping to discuss another matter. Hux expressed his understanding that Ren used proactive and successful strategies that deviated from Hux's own, but made known his wish to be more informed of such surprise actions so as to be a more effective general. Shutting down Hux's concerns coldly, Ren simply dismissed Hux again. Picking up his commlink, Ren answered a call from Vaneé, who told Ren that he had found a Jedi, a worthy enemy for Ren, as promised.[[79]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_6-79)

##### The snows of Lahtee

Ren and Vaneé took Ren's Upsilon-class shuttle to Lahtee, a snowy world in the [Mid Rim](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories"). Ren believed that Vader had killed all of the Jedi, save for his uncle Luke Skywalker, the last Jedi. Vaneé reassured Ren that some few survived, but not for Vader's lack of trying; eventually, virtually no sightings or rumors of Jedi remained, and Vader's focus turned towards Skywalker. Vaneé's lead came from a report of a Jedi that came shortly before the end of the Empire and was never pursued, and the potential Jedi's name was unknown. Vaneé left Ren to his quest, hoping that a solitary quest would help Ren follow in Vader's footsteps.[[79]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_6-79)

Ren walked into the snowy forest alone and made his way to a bar in a settlement. Ordering [wine](/wiki/Wine "Wine") from the [Snivvian](/wiki/Snivvian "Snivvian") bartender, Ren asked if there was anyone unusual in the town. Quickly growing impatient, Ren attempted to perform a mind probe when his lightsaber flew from his belt and into the hands of a bar patron. An old [Theelin](/wiki/Theelin "Theelin") woman, [Grandea](/wiki/Grandea "Grandea"), the Jedi Ren was searching for, revealed herself, recognizing that the crystal in Ren's saber was cracked, and asked Ren to chat.[[79]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_6-79) Holding Ren at saber-point, the two walked outside.[[80]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_7-80)

With Ren surprised that Grandea knew his name without telling her, Grandea revealed that she could sense his name at the front of his mind, as if Ren wanted to drown out everything else by screaming, "I'm Kylo Ren." When asked why Ren was looking for Jedi, Ren simply replied that his reasons were his own. Grandea asserted that she was no longer a Jedi, telling Ren of her younger years, surviving [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66"), losing [her lightsaber](/wiki/Grandea%27s_lightsaber "Grandea's lightsaber"), going into hiding, and using a Jedi [mind trick](/wiki/Mind_trick "Mind trick") to evade the [Imperial Inquisitors](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius") and Vader. Still, Ren found her a suitable enemy. Briefly touching Ren's mind to uncover his intentions, Grandea pitied Ren, believing that he could have been so much more. Furious, Ren recovered and summoned his lightsaber, swinging it through Grandea's body. With Grandea lying at his feet, Ren muttered the name "Skywalker", now determined to erase him as well. Grandea, seemingly unharmed, told Ren that Luke Skywalker was dead. Now ghoulishly floating in the air, Grandea told a disbelieving Ren that she felt Skywalker's passing through the Force, and wondered how Ren, Skywalker's own student, did not. Repeatedly asking who Ren was, Ren struck her again with his lightsaber, after which the woman vanished. Confused and enraged, Ren shouted into the night.[[80]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_7-80)

##### The new Knight of Ren

After Ren's encounter with Grandea on Lahtee and the First Order's full subjugation of Corellia's shipyards, the *Finalizer* would be approached by the *[Night Buzzard](/wiki/Night_Buzzard "Night Buzzard")*, a ship that belonged to Ren's former allies, the Knights of Ren. Ren allowed the ship to board the *Finalizer* and was greeted by its sole occupant, a woman named [Tava Ren](/wiki/Tava_Ren "Tava Ren"), proclaiming herself to be a Knight of Ren and submitting herself to Ren's service.[[81]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_8-81) Ren ignited his lightsaber, quickly attempting to strike her down. Tava ignited her own lightsaber, engaging Ren in a fierce duel. Incurious about Tava, Ren deflected Tava's attempts at conversation but denied nearby stormtroopers the chance to take her down, wanting to deal with Tava himself. Asserting that the Knights of Ren no longer meant anything to him, Ren rebuffed Tava's goading and disarmed her, holding her neck between both lightsabers. Tava pled to Ren that she was the only one with which he could discuss the "Shadow", and Ren spared her life, taunting that Tava best remember how easy his victory was. Asking Ren for something to eat, the two warriors moved to a private dining chamber aboard the *Finalizer*.[[82]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_9-82)

As they ate, Ren asked Tava the whereabouts of the other Knights of Ren. Tava told Ren that though they were around, they did not want to come and meet Ren. Ren wondered how and why Tava took over the Knights of Ren, surprised that they were still alive after Ren abandoned them. Tava explained that she treated them like a prize while Ren treated them like garbage. Elaborating, Tava discussed her past as an enforcer for gang leader [Bedat](/wiki/Bedat "Bedat"), meeting the Knights after they were imprisoned by Bedat for botching a job. Tava asked to join their crew, which they allowed after Tava accomplished her "good death" by killing Bedat and all of his subordinates. Unsatisfied, Ren implored still why Tava came to him. Tava confirmed that her offer to serve Ren was a lie and that she had planned to kill Ren, which Ren did not believe would have worked. Having touched Ren's mind briefly with the Force, Tava claimed to see through Ren's facade, believing Ren to be a "wild man" not suited to the imposing and restrictive station of Supreme Leader. Though Ren warned Tava to be careful, Tava continued, suggesting that the Knights offered Ren the freedom to escape the life he built for himself within the First Order. Tava leaned over the table towards Ren, asking Ren who he wanted to be, and kissed him. Dismayed, Ren recoiled, and called over the *Finalizer's* comms for Tava to be executed by the ship's security forces. Still believing her assessment of Ren to be true, Tava retrieved her lightsaber and fled, fighting her way through hallways of First Order stormtroopers. Tava eventually reached the *Night Buzzard* and escaped the *Finalizer's* hangar, and though General Armitage Hux implored Ren on the *Finalizer's* bridge to order the ship shot down, Ren remained silent, allowing Tava to escape unharmed.[[82]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_9-82)

##### The pits of Mustafar

Ren would return to Fortress Vader on Mustafar, conferring with Vaneé to discuss Ren's uncle, Luke Skywalker, who Ren knew after his encounter with Grandea. Ren felt that he could still sense Skywalker through the Force, though not at the fortress. Ren did not fear Skywalker, but wanted him gone nonetheless. Asking Vaneé how Darth Vader might have accomplished forcing Skywalker to appear before him, Vaneé admitted that he did not know Vader's deepest secrets. Growing frustrated with Vaneé's apparently selective knowledge of Vader, Ren demanded that Vaneé show Ren's the vault hidden within the fortress and the power inside. Though Vaneé couldn't enter the vault himself, he led Ren to its entrance. Ren, confident in his not needing Vaneé's help, walked the corridor, eventually finding himself walking right back through the entrance from which he came. Believing Vaneé to be toying with him, Ren used the Force to knock over Vaneé's mechanical body. Vaneé, panicked, explained that the vault itself decided who entered but also told of another way for Ren to obtain Vader's power. Vaneé then led Ren to Vader's [meditation chamber](/wiki/Darth_Vader%27s_meditation_chamber "Darth Vader's meditation chamber"), hoping that Ren might find clarity inside as Vader had.[[48]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_10-48)

Ren, closing his eyes to meditate, implored his grandfather to bring him Skywalker. Falling into a Force vision, Ren found himself bound by the feet with many chains within a dark bog. Apparitions of people from his past, including his parents, fellow Jedi trainees, Lando Calrissian, Chewbacca, Rey, Snoke and Vader, appeared to Ren as withered skulls atop winding spinal columns. The apparations accused Ren with insults betraying his insecurities, such as "killer", "treacherous" and "disappointment". Ren, struggling to evade them, fell into the mud. Rejecting the apparitions, Ren summoned two spectral lightsabers, one appearing as the blue-bladed Skywalker lightsaber and another as his own. After cutting through the apparitions in a rage, Ren came to the conclusion that Skywalker would not be found in such a place, and reflected on his past memories to find him. After reflecting on his Jedi training with his uncle, Ren appeared within a brightly lit valley populated by glowing apparitions of Jedi. One figure approached Ren, wondering how Ren could have appeared there while the dark side of the Force burned within him. Ren attempted to slice through the figure with his blue-bladed spectral lightsaber, but the figure, unharmed, explained that the place would not allow that. Another figure approached Ren, materializing into the form of Skywalker, agreeing that Ren should not be there but confirming that he was all the same. Chiding that Ren missed him enough to follow him there, Skywalker asked Ren why he was there. Ren explained that though Skywalker was dead, he wanted to have killed Skywalker himself, and wanted to find who did kill Skywalker so he could learn how Skywalker suffered. Skywalker, bemused, told Ren that nobody killed him, that he sacrificed himself for others in the service of something greater. When Skywalker asked what Ren's life was for, Ren demanded that Skywalker stop trying to teach him, and Skywalker agreed that that time was over for the two of them. Ren then asked why Skywalker taught Rey, and Skywalker simply stated that she had wanted to learn. Telling Skywalker he hated him, Ren demanded that Skywalker stop following and watching Ren or be destroyed, asserting that Skywalker failed to turn Ren into him. Skywalker mused that Ren couldn't destroy him without destroying the Force, which would destroy Ren, further reflecting that it was meaningful that Ren had found himself at the Jedi's realm, and that he should ask himself how he managed it. As Ren faded from the realm, Skywalker told Ren that Kylo Ren meant nothing to him, but that he would always be there for Ben Solo.[[48]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_10-48)

Reappearing in the dark bog, Ren was approached by an enormous dark figure. The figure told Ren that he must be reminded of his pain after trying to return to the light and forget his pain and attacked Ren with a red-bladed lightsaber. Ren emerged from his vision and stumbled out of the meditation chamber, his body having manifested grievous real injuries. Vaneé cradled Ren, asking what he had done to himself and believing that his grandfather would be proud.[[48]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_10-48)

Vaneé placed Ren in Vader's bacta tank as Ren faded in and out of consciousness. Reciting Ren's recent journeys to him, Vaneé began to reveal his ultimate plan for Ren: Ren's "death" in the service of transforming him into a new Vader. For this to happen, Vaneé told Ren that he must "die", just as Anakin Skywalker had, to complete his journey and realize his full greatness. Vaneé injected Ren with a drug, causing Ren to lose consciousness, and moved Ren to a platform raised above a chamber of falling lava.[[83]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_11-83)

Ren regained consciousness just as one of [Vader's helmets](/wiki/Darth_Vader%27s_armor "Darth Vader's armor") descended onto his face, its three pieces fully assembling as Ren steadily descended into the lava. Vaneé, observing Ren from above, told Ren to breathe in the lava's fumes and allow them to settle into his mind. Using the Force, Ren dragged Vaneé to teeter over the lava, but released him after Vaneé revealed that only he could release Ren from the pit. As Vaneé elaborated on his vision, telling Ren that he would receive a brief immersion into the flames of Mustafar as Vader did, believing it to be a key step to Vader's ascendance to power. Regardless, Ren summoned the strength through the Force to free himself from his restraints and leap free from the lava pit. Removing Vader's helmet, Ren pursued Vaneé throughout the fortress. Ren made his way through multiple obstacles and traps involving hazards such as heights, flames, lava, laser bolts and arrows, and used his acrobatic and Force skills to complete them unscathed. All the while, Vaneé continued to speak to Ren through the fortress's comms, explaining his belief that the galaxy needed a Vader-like figure to induce order through absolute fear and that Vaneé hoped his legacy would be giving the chaotic galaxy such a figure. Ren came across a chamber that soon filled with derelict [DT-series sentry droids](/wiki/DT-series_sentry_droid "DT-series sentry droid") that he could not safely dispatch and fled them. Finding a display filled with lightsabers from long since fallen Jedi, Ren summoned one with a green blade, cutting down the sentry droids bleeding and cracking the weapon's exposed kyber crystal in his rage. Accepting his fate, Vaneé allowed Ren into his chamber. As a final request, Ren asked Vaneé whether Vader's vault was even real and contained real power, or whether it was merely a deception. When Vaneé admitted that he did not know, Ren told Vaneé that his gravest sin was wasting his time. As Ren held Vaneé over a chasm of lava with the Force, Vaneé accepted his death at the hands of one that was part of Vader's line. His head now severed from his mechanical body, Vaneé told Ren that everything he had done was in service to realizing Ren's potential, which only enraged Ren, who proclaimed that he was already everything he needed to be. Happy with Ren's self-acceptance, Vaneé fell to his death believing that Ren would honor his family's legacy.[[83]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_11-83)

##### Vader's vault

Finally rid of Vaneé, Ren once again approached the cavernous mouth of Vader's vault. After hearing a voice asking if he was afraid, Ren, unbowed, confidently strode through the entrance.[[83]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_11-83)

#### Campaign of terror

:   "*We have learned from the mistakes of the Empire—They were too* lenient*. The Resistance is looking to replenish their lost ships and weapons… It is imperative they find none. Make sure the word is spread from here—to the farthest corner of the galaxy.*"
