:   ―Kylo Ren[[84]](#cite_note-Allegiance_2-84)

In the aftermath of the Battle of Crait, word of the duel between Ren and Skywalker had spread across the galaxy, despite the First Order's efforts to suppress the rumors. Immersed in the dark side of the Force, Ren instituted a zero-tolerance policy against "subversive" worlds, directing his forces to hunt and destroy all dissidents who opposed his reign as the new Supreme Leader. Ren also kept his involvement in Snoke's death a secret, so that no one would doubt his claim to the leadership of the First Order. Although General Hux survived the regime change within the First Order, the new Supreme Leader was distrustful and refused to lower his guard around someone as devious as Hux.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5)

 [![The new Supreme Leader decreed that any form of contact with the Resistance was punishable by death.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/KyloRen-Allegiance2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210623055027) [![The new Supreme Leader decreed that any form of contact with the Resistance was punishable by death.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/KyloRen-Allegiance2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210623055027)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/KyloRen-Allegiance2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210623055027) 

The new Supreme Leader decreed that any form of contact with the Resistance was punishable by death.

 

Ren ensured that his one-time rival would have little independent authority without supervision, even giving assignments to the Knights of Ren before entrusting Hux with anything of importance.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) At some point during the war, Ren sought an update on the Order's stock of refueling stations, leading to a short notice meeting aboard the *[Titan](/wiki/Titan "Titan")* that Hux was made to attend. Prior to the meeting, when Stormtrooper Commander [Pyre](/wiki/Pyre "Pyre") complained about the short notice, Hux explained it was due to Ren's wishes.[[85]](#cite_note-Station_to_Station-85) Ren also kept Hux close by to countermand the general's orders when necessary; on one occasion, Hux dismissed a reported sighting of the Resistance operative Finn, believing it was a waste of the First Order's resources to follow up on every rumor regarding the Resistance. This led Ren to openly chastise Hux on the bridge of the *Finalizer*, ensuring the general understood that they would use every available asset to find and destroy the Resistance.[[86]](#cite_note-Allegiance_1-86)

Holding more power than he ever had in his life up to that point,[[87]](#cite_note-Rise_Article-87) the Supreme Leader made good on his vow to punish any world that showed anything less than absolute loyalty. Making his way to the neutral planet of [Fondor](/wiki/Fondor "Fondor"), Ren placed it under military occupation after learning that the Resistance had passed through its system. Although an [official](/wiki/Unidentified_human_male_(Fondor) "Unidentified human male (Fondor)") of Fondor swore that his government held no allegiance to the insurgents, having refused to assist them in any capacity, the mere contact with the enemies of the First Order provided Ren with his justification for seizing control of the [Fondor Shipyards](/wiki/Fondor_Shipyards "Fondor Shipyards"). Convinced the Old Empire had been too lenient, Ren adopted a zero-tolerance policy in regard to the Resistance, and as such, he personally decapitated the official. Ultimately, Fondor was made an example to the rest of the galaxy, warning them to stay away from the Resistance on pain of death. Such measures were intended by Ren to prevent the Resistance from replacing their lost resources.[[84]](#cite_note-Allegiance_2-84)

#### Supervising the advance

:   "*We can and will chase every rumor, every scrap, every vapor trail across the galaxy! We will mobilize every bounty hunter and informant and turn over every rock to find* all *of them…and wipe every one of them out of existence!*"
:   ―Kylo Ren, to Armitage Hux[[86]](#cite_note-Allegiance_1-86)

 [![With much of the galaxy conquered through sheer military might under Supreme Leader Kylo Ren, the First Order saw his reign as the dawn of a new era, with no system daring to oppose the Supreme Leader's wrath.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/KyloRen-GalaxysEdge5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210623054752) [![With much of the galaxy conquered through sheer military might under Supreme Leader Kylo Ren, the First Order saw his reign as the dawn of a new era, with no system daring to oppose the Supreme Leader's wrath.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/KyloRen-GalaxysEdge5.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210623054752)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/KyloRen-GalaxysEdge5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210623054752) 

With much of the galaxy conquered through sheer military might under Supreme Leader Kylo Ren, the First Order saw his reign as the dawn of a new era, with no system daring to oppose the Supreme Leader's wrath.

 

Under Ren's leadership and with its military spreading across the galaxy,[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) the First Order was confident that, under the new Supreme Leader, the galaxy was on the verge of achieving unprecedented harmony.[[88]](#cite_note-Galaxy's_Edge_5-88) A [stormtrooper sergeant](/wiki/Unidentified_First_Order_stormtrooper_sergeant "Unidentified First Order stormtrooper sergeant") in the [709th "Red Fury" Legion](/wiki/709th_Legion "709th Legion")[[89]](#cite_note-Galaxy's_Edge_1-89)—a formation of elite stormtroopers chosen by Ren himself[[90]](#cite_note-Black_Spire-90)—regarded his leader's regime as the harbinger of peace, establishing a new era in place of the fallen New Republic, which the [sergeant](/wiki/Sergeant "Sergeant") viewed as a turbulent period of chaos and corruption.[[88]](#cite_note-Galaxy's_Edge_5-88) The galaxy, which had largely demilitarized during the decades of peace, was unprepared to face the threat of the First Order, and many worlds capitulated to Ren's rule.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) However, the Supreme Leader lusted for even greater power.[[87]](#cite_note-Rise_Article-87) Eager to crush any who opposed him,[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) he continued the manhunt for the surviving members of the Resistance, deploying First Order forces to various locations across the galaxy,[[91]](#cite_note-Galaxy's_Edge-91) and began a quest to uncover the Force's darkest secrets, hoping to use that knowledge to cement himself as the supreme ruler of the galaxy.[[87]](#cite_note-Rise_Article-87)

To that end, Ren established an elite force of stormtroopers, the [First Order Raiders](/wiki/First_Order_Raider "First Order Raider"), to serve as extremely skilled relic hunters.[[92]](#cite_note-First_Order_Raiders_Databank-92) Ren dispatched his Raiders out into the galaxy with the mission of bringing him ancient relics,[[93]](#cite_note-Relic_Raiders-93) specifically those related to the Sith[[92]](#cite_note-First_Order_Raiders_Databank-92) because of their destructive potential and power.[[94]](#cite_note-Mika_Grey_Databank-94) During their hunts, the Raiders crossed paths with the treasure hunter [Mika Grey](/wiki/Mika_Grey "Mika Grey"), who learned of the troopers' personal allegiance to Ren[[93]](#cite_note-Relic_Raiders-93) and hoped to keep such artifacts out of the Supreme Leader's hands. In particular, she had spent over two years hunting a [Sith relic](/wiki/Unidentified_Sith_relic "Unidentified Sith relic") with life-ending power,[[94]](#cite_note-Mika_Grey_Databank-94) [finding](/wiki/Mission_to_Ashas_Ree "Mission to Ashas Ree") it before the First Order on the planet [Ashas Ree](/wiki/Ashas_Ree "Ashas Ree"). Ultimately, she turned its power against a group of Raiders under [Agent](/wiki/Agent "Agent") [Raith](/wiki/Raith "Raith"),[[93]](#cite_note-Relic_Raiders-93) destroying them and draining the relic's energy.[[95]](#cite_note-Relic_Episode_Guide_11-95)

#### The Batuu gambit

:   "*Enough! You will come to me! You cannot change what's happening, Rey. The past is dead. We, we can be the future! You and I can rule the galaxy, together.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren, to Rey[[52]](#cite_note-Galactic_Starcruiser-52)

 [![The hunt for Rey brought Kylo Ren to Batuu, where he sought to capture the scavenger who had evaded him.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/RenVsRey-SWGE.png/revision/latest?cb=20200405221928) [![The hunt for Rey brought Kylo Ren to Batuu, where he sought to capture the scavenger who had evaded him.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/RenVsRey-SWGE.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200405221928)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/RenVsRey-SWGE.png/revision/latest?cb=20200405221928) 

The hunt for Rey brought Kylo Ren to Batuu, where he sought to capture the scavenger who had evaded him.

 

After receiving word that Rey had apparently been sighted on Batuu, Ren personally oversaw the search for Resistance fugitives at the [Black Spire Outpost](/wiki/Black_Spire_Outpost "Black Spire Outpost") on [Batuu](/wiki/Batuu "Batuu"), having traveled to the remote installation via a [TIE/es assault shuttle](/wiki/TIE/es_assault_shuttle "TIE/es assault shuttle")[[91]](#cite_note-Galaxy's_Edge-91) along with[[89]](#cite_note-Galaxy's_Edge_1-89) his elite 709th Legion.[[90]](#cite_note-Black_Spire-90) Upon his arrival at [Docking Bay 9](/wiki/Docking_Bay_9_(Batuu) "Docking Bay 9 (Batuu)"), Ren was greeted by a First Order officer whom he deemed incompetent, and consequently strangled the officer by way of the Force.[[91]](#cite_note-Galaxy's_Edge-91) Ren's arrival on Batuu was supported by members of his Red Fury Legion, including stormtroopers [CF-8011](/wiki/CF-8011 "CF-8011") and [AD-2508](/wiki/AD-2508 "AD-2508"). In the presence of CF-8011, Ren repeatedly noted that he sensed disturbances in the Force. However, the reasoning for their deployment to Batuu and such statements from Ren were confusing to CF-8011, who asked AD-2508 what the dark warrior meant whenever he "sensed" something. Despite Ren's status as their Supreme Leader, AD-2508 mocked Ren as someone who needed to calm down.[[96]](#cite_note-Datapad-96) Other Red Fury stormtroopers, however, knew their deployment was because of Resistance activity on Batuu.[[89]](#cite_note-Galaxy's_Edge_1-89)

At one point during his time on Batuu, Ren confronted Resistance spy [Vi Moradi](/wiki/Vi_Moradi "Vi Moradi"), but she refused to give secrets to the Supreme Leader. Before Ren could strike Moradi down, Rey arrived, and the two Force-sensitives began a lightsaber duel. However, Ren was ultimately forced to leave when a stormtrooper informed him of an incident aboard their destroyer.[[97]](#cite_note-Kylo_vs_Rey_Galaxy's_Edge-97) Later, Ren was with Hux and in command of[[98]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Resistance-98) the *Finalizer*[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) when it [captured](/wiki/Battle_of_Batuu "Battle of Batuu") a Resistance [Intersystem Transport Ship](/wiki/Intersystem_Transport_Ship "Intersystem Transport Ship"). However, Poe Dameron managed to escape before returning with a sizable fleet that caught the First Order off guard. Ren, who commanded the First Order forces alongside General Hux, realized that the Resistance was using a hijacked [First Order Fleet Transport](/wiki/First_Order_Fleet_Transport "First Order Fleet Transport") and eventually engaged in a pursuit. Despite his efforts, the Resistance operatives escaped from the Star Destroyer using one of its [escape pods](/wiki/Escape_pod "Escape pod") to return to the ruins of Batuu.[[98]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Resistance-98)

 [![Kylo Ren dueled Rey aboard the Halcyon star cruiser and once again tried to tempt her to the dark side.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/Kylo-Rey-duel-GalacticStarcruiser.png/revision/latest?cb=20220911202223) [![Kylo Ren dueled Rey aboard the Halcyon star cruiser and once again tried to tempt her to the dark side.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/Kylo-Rey-duel-GalacticStarcruiser.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220911202223)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/Kylo-Rey-duel-GalacticStarcruiser.png/revision/latest?cb=20220911202223) 

Kylo Ren dueled Rey aboard the *Halcyon* star cruiser and once again tried to tempt her to the dark side.

 

When the First Order began to investigate the [MPO-1400 *Purgill*-class star cruiser](/wiki/MPO-1400_Purgill-class_star_cruiser "MPO-1400 Purgill-class star cruiser") *[Halcyon](/wiki/Halcyon "Halcyon")* for suspected Resistance activity, Ren personally arrived and threatened its current guests to try to find Rey. When she revealed herself, the two began a new duel as the crowd below watched, with Ren taking note of how her skills had grown. When Ren tried to talk down on the concept of the Resistance in a new attempt to convince her to join him, Rey rejected his offer, so Ren threw her against a railing and the wall, claiming the Skywalker lightsaber as his own from his injured enemy. After she avoided fire from the stormtroopers below, Ren managed to hold her in a Force grip, pulling her towards himself to demand that she join him while Chewbacca and other Resistance agents attacked.[[52]](#cite_note-Galactic_Starcruiser-52)

When Rey escaped and reclaimed her lightsaber, their duel continued until Yoda's holocron, the very same one Ren had assumed destroyed in the blaze of Skywalker's temple, played before them. Ren tried to claim the holocron for himself due to the knowledge it contained, but Rey stole it from him and escaped by Force pushing him back. Before chasing after her, Ren ordered Lieutenant [Harman Croy](/wiki/Harman_Croy "Harman Croy") to execute all of the guests below, whether or not they were loyal to the First Order, but the Resistance managed to overwhelm the stormtroopers after Ren left the room.[[52]](#cite_note-Galactic_Starcruiser-52)

#### Cementing his command

:   "*'*Supreme Leader.*' Not what I would have chosen for myself. 'Master of the dark side,' perhaps… 'Commander of the Knights of Ren'… But this is where I have landed. And now, it sounds… Right.* Just. *Head of the* First Order. *My word, unchallenged.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren[[99]](#cite_note-Follow_and_Lead-99)

Rebuilding his command in the wake of the *Supremacy*'s destruction, Ren brought [Allegiant General](/wiki/Allegiant_General "Allegiant General") [Enric Pryde](/wiki/Enric_Pryde "Enric Pryde") to the forefront of his operations after discovering the reserve forces under his command. He also transferred his command to Pryde's Star Destroyer [*Steadfast*](/wiki/Steadfast_(Resurgent-class) "Steadfast (Resurgent-class)"), bringing Hux with him after the *Finalizer* sustained significant damage from the run-in with Resistance forces over Batuu. Ren entrusted important jobs that could have otherwise gone to Hux to the Allegiant General: in effect, the years that Hux spent jockeying for power against Ren ultimately worked against the general, as his authority was superseded not only by Ren, but Pryde as well.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) As Supreme Leader, nevertheless, Ren formed a regime that was different from the one overseen by his predecessor. He sought to foster cooperation among the top First Order military leaders, and as such Ren formed the [Supreme Council](/wiki/First_Order_Supreme_Council "First Order Supreme Council"), a cabinet consisting of members of High Command, including Pryde, Hux, Admiral [Frantis Griss](/wiki/Frantis_Griss "Frantis Griss"), and generals [Amret Engell](/wiki/Amret_Engell "Amret Engell"), [Bellava Parnadee](/wiki/Bellava_Parnadee "Bellava Parnadee"), and [Domaric Quinn](/wiki/Domaric_Quinn "Domaric Quinn").[[100]](#cite_note-Supreme_Council_DB-100)

 [![As a head of state, Ren suppressed dissent through the threat and use of military force.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DarkOrder.png/revision/latest?cb=20230401004411) [![As a head of state, Ren suppressed dissent through the threat and use of military force.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DarkOrder.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20230401004411)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DarkOrder.png/revision/latest?cb=20230401004411) 

As a head of state, Ren suppressed dissent through the threat and use of military force.

 

They were all proud men and women who were unaccustomed to Ren's leadership, having risen through the ranks in a time when most high-ranking officers knew little of the First Order's goals and capabilities. Despite Ren's motivation for creating the Council, their meetings aboard the *Steadfast* became marred by sniping and turf wars.[[100]](#cite_note-Supreme_Council_DB-100) Meanwhile, however, the First Order's military might cowed many worlds into submission,[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) although some remained defiant despite the threat of annihilation. Ren, who came to see himself as ruler of the galaxy, toured the worlds that the First Order conquered in the name of their new Supreme Leader. [One of the worlds](/wiki/Unidentified_world_(Kylo_Ren) "Unidentified world (Kylo Ren)") that he visited was under military occupation; the officer who greeted him expressed how honored they were by his presence while [another](/wiki/Unidentified_First_Order_officer_(Kylo_Ren) "Unidentified First Order officer (Kylo Ren)") prepared his speech to the local population, which included metaphors and allusions of cultural relevance to the world that they occupied.[[99]](#cite_note-Follow_and_Lead-99)

As he stood on a balcony overlooking the crowd, he crushed the [datapad](/wiki/Datapad "Datapad") containing his speech, which was followed by the stormtroopers saluting. The civilians responded by kneeling before him with downcast eyes as the First Order soldiers shouted "all hail the Supreme Leader!" Ren visited another world that the First Order subjugated on his behalf. However, he was ambushed by a group of insurgents hiding within the crowd. Ren ordered his stormtroopers to stand their ground and fought beside them. During the battle, he targeted the [woman](/wiki/Unidentified_human_girl_(Kylo_Ren) "Unidentified human girl (Kylo Ren)") who led the insurgents, determined to make her an example to others who defied his authority. Interested in why she would attack him despite the consequences, he allowed her to declare that her people would rather die fighting for freedom than submit to Ren's [fascist](/wiki/Fascism "Fascism") rule. Ren's response was that he would make her people suffer for her actions, but the woman asserted that their sacrifice would not be in vain if it inspired further resistance against the First Order. Ren dismissed her as a fool, and said that she would regret her choice. As a result, her world was set aflame as Ren returned to the Star Destroyer in orbit.[[99]](#cite_note-Follow_and_Lead-99)

#### The *Colossus* cell

:   "*I will not suffer the existence of any Resistance cell. No matter how small.*"  
    "*We understand, Supreme Leader.*"  
    "*Do you?*"
:   ―Kylo Ren and Tierny[[101]](#cite_note-The_Escape-101)

In retaliation against the [Aeosians](/wiki/Aeosian "Aeosian") who supported the Resistance, a fleet of *Resurgent*-class Star Destroyers invaded their homeworld of [Aeos Prime](/wiki/Aeos_Prime "Aeos Prime") and [devastated](/wiki/Suppression_of_the_Aeos_system "Suppression of the Aeos system") it. After completing the [orbital bombardment](/wiki/Orbital_bombardment "Orbital bombardment"), First Order Security Bureau Agent [Tierny](/wiki/Tierny "Tierny") and Stormtrooper Commander Pyre reported their actions to General Hux but found Supreme Leader Kylo Ren waiting on the other side of the [holoprojector](/wiki/Holoprojector "Holoprojector").[[101]](#cite_note-The_Escape-101) Aware of Pyre and Tierny's failure to defeat the [*Colossus* resistance](/wiki/Team_Colossus "Team Colossus"),[[102]](#cite_note-Escape_1_EG-102) he declared that he would not tolerate the existence of any Resistance cell.[[101]](#cite_note-The_Escape-101) Reaching out through the Force, Ren influenced the two to stand and point their blasters at each other. He then severed the transmission, leaving his subordinates with an ominous warning about the price for failure.[[102]](#cite_note-Escape_1_EG-102)

 [![Ren would brook no failure, and so he unleashed his wrath on Agent Tierny as a demonstration of his power.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/NoMercyForTheWeak-TheEscape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200128081835) [![Ren would brook no failure, and so he unleashed his wrath on Agent Tierny as a demonstration of his power.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/NoMercyForTheWeak-TheEscape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200128081835)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/NoMercyForTheWeak-TheEscape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200128081835) 

Ren would brook no failure, and so he unleashed his wrath on Agent Tierny as a demonstration of his power.

 

Though they managed to locate the *Colossus* station in the [Barabesh system](/wiki/Barabesh_system "Barabesh system"), the [ensuing battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Barabesh "Battle of Barabesh") did not turn in the First Order's favor. Betrayed by the [TIE fighter pilot](/wiki/First_Order_TIE_fighter_pilot "First Order TIE fighter pilot") [DT-533](/wiki/Tamara_Ryvora "Tamara Ryvora"), the First Order failed to prevent the Resistance operatives Kazuda Xiono and [Jarek Yeager](/wiki/Jarek_Yeager "Jarek Yeager") from warning their allies of the impending attack. Rather than retreat, however, the citizenry of the *Colossus* held their ground against the forces of the First Order. While the [Ace Squadron](/wiki/Ace_Squadron "Ace Squadron") intensified their attack run on the [main Star Destroyer](/wiki/Thunderer "Thunderer"), Tierny received a transmission from Supreme Leader Ren. She beseeched him to send reinforcements, but Ren rejected her request and declared that the First Order had no tolerance for the weak. With that, Ren telekinetically choked the First Order agent with the Force,[[101]](#cite_note-The_Escape-101) unleashing his final punishment on Tierny.[[103]](#cite_note-Escape_2_EG-103)

#### Investigation on Vendaxa

:   "*If they are indeed hiding on Vendaxa, then we will pin them down, smother them with numbers, and the Resistan—*"
:   ―Armitage Hux[[104]](#cite_note-Loyalty_Test-104)

 [![Ren and Hux argued before being attacked by an Acklay.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7f/Kylo_and_Ren_argue.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200324010042) [![Ren and Hux argued before being attacked by an Acklay.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7f/Kylo_and_Ren_argue.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200324010042)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7f/Kylo_and_Ren_argue.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200324010042) 

Ren and Hux argued before being attacked by an Acklay.

 

During the hunt for the Resistance, General Hux announced to a squad of stormtroopers that the First Order had received word of the rebels operating in secret on the planet [Vendaxa](/wiki/Vendaxa "Vendaxa"). Supreme Leader Ren interrupted the general and dismissed the stormtroopers, intending to investigate the planet alone. However, Hux insisted on accompanying the Supreme Leader. They began their investigation upon arriving on Vendaxa, only to start bickering over their loyalties and sacrifices for the First Order. During their argument, an [acklay](/wiki/Acklay "Acklay") approached the pair, causing Hux to run for his life while Ren stood his ground. Ren was unafraid and fought against the creature, but Hux took the opportunity to shoot at the Acklay with his [SE-44C blaster pistol](/wiki/SE-44C_blaster_pistol "SE-44C blaster pistol"), causing it to run away. Ren and Hux ultimately returned to the First Order after confirming that there were no Resistance operatives on Vendaxa.[[104]](#cite_note-Loyalty_Test-104)

#### Ghost of Skywalker

:   "*Where are you? I can feel you! I know you're watching me! Show yourself, you coward! No more tricks, Skywalker...just the reckoning I deserve! You're a fool.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren, to Luke Skywalker[[105]](#cite_note-See_You_Around,_Kid-105)

 [![Feeling the presence of his Jedi Master, Ren hoped to lure him out by visiting familiar locations.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/KyloRenOnCrait-SeeYouAroundKid.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220720175017) [![Feeling the presence of his Jedi Master, Ren hoped to lure him out by visiting familiar locations.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/KyloRenOnCrait-SeeYouAroundKid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220720175017)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/KyloRenOnCrait-SeeYouAroundKid.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220720175017) 

Feeling the presence of his Jedi Master, Ren hoped to lure him out by visiting familiar locations.

 

Still sensing the presence of his Jedi Master Luke Skywalker, Kylo Ren attempted to have Skywalker show himself by visiting locations of their past, starting with Crait, the site of their final encounter. As the *Steadfast* neared the planet, Enric Pryde informed the Supreme Leader that they arrived at Crait, only for Ren to wrathfully order the preparation of his shuttle. Upon arriving on Crait, Ren began to violently swing his lightsaber near the location of his fateful duel with his former Jedi Master. The Supreme Leader and the Knights of Ren later traveled to the former Jedi outpost on Elphrona, where he and his master had their first encounter with the Knights.[[105]](#cite_note-See_You_Around,_Kid-105)

Ren commanded the Knights to remain vigilant for sightings of Skywalker's [ghost](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit"), to which the Knight [Vicrul](/wiki/Vicrul "Vicrul") replied that no such apparition was felt. Ren mocked him by saying that they were defeated in that outpost before claiming that he had one final place to look. Kylo Ren arrived on Ossus, where the Jedi Temple of his past lay in ruin. Ren desperately shouted for his Jedi Master to show himself, but received no answer. After making peace with his fruitless travels, Ren boarded his ship, ordering General Armitage Hux to bombard the location from orbit, as there was nothing left.[[105]](#cite_note-See_You_Around,_Kid-105)

### Dark legacies

#### The phantom Emperor

:   "*He's gone mad. Flames of rebellion burn across the galaxy and Ren chases a* ghost*.*"  
    "*No.* Someone *was behind that transmission. And Leader Ren will answer to no one.*"
:   ―Armitage Hux and Enric Pryde[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

Within a year of Kylo Ren's ascension to supreme power,[[2]](#cite_note-Timelines-2) a [mysterious transmission](/wiki/Palpatine%27s_broadcast "Palpatine's broadcast") broadcasting the voice of Darth Sidious—the long-dead Galactic Emperor and Dark Lord of the Sith—reached the far corners of the galaxy. Although Ren doubted that Sidious had returned, he was certain that others believed the message, so he was determined to [uncover the truth](/wiki/Search_for_Exegol "Search for Exegol") first to prevent any threats to his rule. As a result, he diverted his attention and the First Order's resources away from the Resistance to focus entirely on investigating the message.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) The broadcast bolstered the rumors that the Emperor lived but was in hiding, leading many within the First Order to believe that they should follow Sidious instead of Ren.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) While Pryde supported Ren's decision to investigate the mysterious message, Hux became convinced that the Supreme Leader had spiraled into insanity for committing the First Order's military towards what Hux considered as a hunt for a ghost while they faced rebellions across the galaxy.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

 [![Ren slaughtered the Alazmec of Winsit to acquire a Sith wayfinder on Mustafar.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/Malice-SWZ87_Chris_Bjors.png/revision/latest?cb=20240811152905) [![Ren slaughtered the Alazmec of Winsit to acquire a Sith wayfinder on Mustafar.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/Malice-SWZ87_Chris_Bjors.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20240811152905)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/Malice-SWZ87_Chris_Bjors.png/revision/latest?cb=20240811152905) 

Ren slaughtered the Alazmec of Winsit to acquire a Sith wayfinder on Mustafar.

 

In spite of the First Order's ongoing war against the Resistance and other dissidents, Ren's priorities changed after he learned that his late Master Snoke had not been the omnipotent ruler as he previously thought.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) Though he had doubts about the transmission's authenticity, Ren was determined to find the source of the message and discover the truth himself.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) To accomplish this, Ren sought a [Sith wayfinder](/wiki/Sith_wayfinder "Sith wayfinder") and undertook a [journey to Mustafar](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar_(First_Order) "Mission to Mustafar (First Order)"). Accompanied by Pryde, Hux and a stormtrooper escort, the Supreme Leader arrived in the Corvax Fen. His aim was to take possession of [Vader's wayfinder](/wiki/Vader%27s_wayfinder "Vader's wayfinder"), one of two [wayfinders](/wiki/Wayfinder "Wayfinder") made by the Sith.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Devoted to protecting the fen, the Alazmec of Winsit obstructed his path to the crumbling ruins of Vader's castle.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) Pryde and Hux watched from a safe distance as Ren slaughtered the cultists,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) outpacing his stormtrooper escort.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5)

At a small brackish lake, Ren encountered a [spider](/wiki/Spider "Spider")-like being that identified itself as the [Eye of Webbish Bog](/wiki/Eye_of_Webbish_Bog "Eye of Webbish Bog").[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Ren came close to killing the creature when it addressed him by his Skywalker heritage.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) Killing the cultists had not been a challenge for Ren; nevertheless the Eye deemed him worthy of claiming the wayfinder in accordance with Vader's wishes. The Eye assured Ren that the artifact would guide him to the hidden Sith world of [Exegol](/wiki/Exegol "Exegol"), through the Unknown Regions, but also warned him that his path would end with the discovery of his true self. After taking possession of the wayfinder, Ren returned to the *Steadfast* and proceeded into the Unknown Regions on his own.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

#### Heir to the new Sith Empire

:   "*Kill the girl. End the Jedi. And become what your grandfather Vader could not. You will rule all the galaxy as the new Emperor.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious, to Kylo Ren[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

 [![Ren's journey to Exegol revealed to him that the demise of the last Sith Lord had not ended the Sith religion.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/KyloRen-Exegol.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200202230109) [![Ren's journey to Exegol revealed to him that the demise of the last Sith Lord had not ended the Sith religion.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/KyloRen-Exegol.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200202230109)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/KyloRen-Exegol.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200202230109) 

Ren's journey to Exegol revealed to him that the demise of the last Sith Lord had not ended the Sith religion.

 

Ren used the onboard [navigation computer](/wiki/Navigation_computer "Navigation computer") of his [modified TIE whisper](/wiki/Kylo_Ren%27s_TIE_whisper "Kylo Ren's TIE whisper") to assimilate the data within Vader's wayfinder, which provided him with coordinates to navigate the anomalies of the Unknown Regions. After passing through the [Red Honeycomb Zone](/wiki/Red_Honeycomb_Zone "Red Honeycomb Zone"), he arrived directly at Exegol. There, he found an ancient [Sith Citadel](/wiki/Sith_Citadel "Sith Citadel").[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

Ren descended into the depths of the citadel with the intention of destroying the dark presence within and claiming its power for himself, which he believed was his birthright as the grandson of a Sith Lord. When a voice spoke telepathically to him, Ren instantly recognized it as both Darth Sidious and the voice he had heard in his mind throughout his childhood. Ren's suspicions of the Emperor's influence over his life[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) were further confirmed to him when Sidious morphed his voice into that of Snoke and Vader as he told Ren he'd been every voice Ren had heard inside his mind.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) Sidious approved of Ren's actions, including killing Snoke;[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) his followers had created Snoke to mold Ren into an heir of the Sith, and Ren had acted as a true Sith by killing his master.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) While searching for the Emperor, Ren saw a [vat](/wiki/Vat "Vat") containing multiple versions of Snoke's body,[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) a sign to Ren that Snoke was originally from Exegol. Ren had been unaware that Sidious was his true master in the ways of the dark side, whereas Snoke served as the Dark Lord's proxy.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

 [![Determined to destroy any threat to his reign, Ren sought to kill Darth Sidious.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/Kylo_Ren_confronts_Palpatine.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200418223214) [![Determined to destroy any threat to his reign, Ren sought to kill Darth Sidious.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/Kylo_Ren_confronts_Palpatine.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200418223214)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/Kylo_Ren_confronts_Palpatine.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200418223214) 

Determined to destroy any threat to his reign, Ren sought to kill Darth Sidious.

 

Ren found Sidious' physical form supported by a device that Ren recognized from his studies of the Clone Wars as an [Ommin harness](/wiki/Ommin_harness "Ommin harness"). The body within was a clone of the late Emperor and served as a host for his spirit, with the harness sustaining the cloned body as the dark side attached to the Emperor's soul caused rapid decay. Despite the frailty of the body, Ren could feel the undiminished strength of the dark side within.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

Sidious revealed to Ren the final stage of his long-gestating plan for vengeance: the [Final Order](/wiki/Final_Order "Final Order"). In a vision,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Ren witnessed more than a thousand [*Xyston*-class Star Destroyers](/wiki/Xyston-class_Star_Destroyer "Xyston-class Star Destroyer"), modeled after [*Imperial I*-class Star Destroyers](/wiki/Imperial_I-class_Star_Destroyer "Imperial I-class Star Destroyer"), each outfitted with [axial superlaser](/wiki/Axial_superlaser "Axial superlaser") [cannons](/wiki/Cannon "Cannon") that were capable of destroying entire planets. Once deployed, it would be the largest armada the galaxy had ever known. This confirmed the rumors that Ren had heard about Exegol, particularly the Sith Eternal cultists who secretly resided there and continued to worship the Sith despite the demise of the last Sith Lords.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) They were true believers in the dark side of the Force who had devoted their entire lives to creating a fleet that would annihilate the rebellion throughout the galaxy,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) and it was their intention that Ren should inherit the Sith legacy by leading their forces against the galaxy.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5)

 [![Ren discovered the Final Order, the largest fleet in galactic history, secretly constructed on Exegol.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/Unidentified_Star_Destroyer_fleet.png/revision/latest?cb=20190827043654) [![Ren discovered the Final Order, the largest fleet in galactic history, secretly constructed on Exegol.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/Unidentified_Star_Destroyer_fleet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190827043654)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/Unidentified_Star_Destroyer_fleet.png/revision/latest?cb=20190827043654) 

Ren discovered the Final Order, the largest fleet in galactic history, secretly constructed on Exegol.

 

Ren's desire to control both the fleet and the [army](/wiki/Sith_Eternal_army "Sith Eternal army") of [Sith troopers](/wiki/Sith_trooper "Sith trooper") delayed his plan for killing Sidious, who urged him to succeed where Vader failed by ruling the galaxy as the new [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") [Emperor](/wiki/Emperor "Emperor"). His only stipulation before ceding control of the fleet, otherwise known as the Final Order, was to prevent Rey from becoming a true Jedi by killing her.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) If she lived, Ren would die and the First Order would fall. Moreover, Sidious revealed her true heritage as his granddaughter. Ren realized he had incorrectly dismissed Rey's parents as a poor, frightened couple "living on the edge of desperation,"[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) when in truth they chose to live anonymously in order to protect their daughter from her grandfather.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

Though Sidious acknowledged Ren as a worthy apprentice who possessed the raw power of the Skywalker bloodline, he harbored doubts about Ren's commitment to the dark side due to his inner conflict. Sensing the last vestiges of the light within Ren, Sidious intended the task of killing Rey to serve as Ren's final test to prove his worth by ending the Jedi and leading the galaxy as its new master.[[36]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-36)

 [![Sidious urged Ren to kill the last Jedi and succeed him as the new Galactic Emperor.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a8/SidiousandKyloRen-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200401232210) [![Sidious urged Ren to kill the last Jedi and succeed him as the new Galactic Emperor.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a8/SidiousandKyloRen-TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200401232210)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a8/SidiousandKyloRen-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200401232210) 

Sidious urged Ren to kill the last Jedi and succeed him as the new Galactic Emperor.

 

Despite Sidious' ultimatum, Ren did not want to kill Rey; the full truth of her origins had renewed Ren's interest in turning her to the dark side to reign over the galaxy with him,[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) as he had tried without success during their last encounter,[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) believing they would be invincible together.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) After returning to his quarters on the *Steadfast*, Ren meditated using his grandfather's mask and sought Rey through their connection in the Force. At the time, she was running an obstacle course outside the [Resistance's new base](/wiki/Resistance_base_(Ajan_Kloss) "Resistance base (Ajan Kloss)") on [Ajan Kloss](/wiki/Ajan_Kloss "Ajan Kloss"). Their minds connected and began to flood with memories of past events. Rey struggled against the dark side within herself, but she eventually lashed out after losing control.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

#### Reforging the mask

:   **Kylo Ren**: "*I sense unease about my appearance, General Hux.*"
:   **Armitage Hux**: "*About the mask? No, sir. Well done.*"
:   **Bellava Parnadee**: "*I like it.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren, Armitage Hux, and Bellava Parnadee[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

Following his return from Exegol, Ren summoned his followers, the Knights to Ren, in order to utilize their tracking skills to locate Rey. As before, when he claimed the mantle of leadership, the Knights accepted Ren as their master without question, affirming that the results of his trial still stood. Recalling his Knights also motivated Ren to reforge his mask as a symbol of his place among their ranks. The work of rebuilding what Ren destroyed fell to [Albrekh](/wiki/Albrekh "Albrekh"), a Sith alchemist trained in classic metallurgy, capable of smithing feats that were unfamiliar to the modern galaxy. He was also the first [Symeong](/wiki/Symeong "Symeong") that Ren had ever encountered.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

 [![Kylo Ren watched as his new mask was forged from the shards of his first helmet by Albrekh, a Sith alchemist.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/RiseCollectorEdition-stare-at-helmet.png/revision/latest?cb=20220922025705) [![Kylo Ren watched as his new mask was forged from the shards of his first helmet by Albrekh, a Sith alchemist.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/RiseCollectorEdition-stare-at-helmet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20220922025705)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/RiseCollectorEdition-stare-at-helmet.png/revision/latest?cb=20220922025705) 

Kylo Ren watched as his new mask was forged from the shards of his first helmet by Albrekh, a Sith alchemist.

 

Ren gave the shards of his mask—all painstakingly scavenged from the wreckage of the *Supremacy*—to Albrekh, who used [Sarrassian iron](/wiki/Sarrassian_iron "Sarrassian iron") to fuse the pieces back together. Applying the iron into the cracks of the reformed helmet created a red adhesive stronger than steel. When the Symeong's work was finished, the mask was restored to its original shape, albeit with red fractures that Ren likened to crimson lightning. It was more than symbolic of his status as a Knight;[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) in Ren's mind, it reflected his own personal growth and evolution. He reaffirmed his affiliation with the Knights, but this time on his own terms.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) The reforged mask's crimson fractures also marked Ren's reign as the new Supreme Leader[[64]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-64) and his intent to follow in his grandfather's footsteps and become the Dark Lord of the Sith.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10)

Ren learned that a spy had been captured on the [Sinta Glacier Colony](/wiki/Sinta_Glacier_Colony "Sinta Glacier Colony") by the time he returned to the *Steadfast*. Enforcing a zero-tolerance policy on espionage and treason, Ren had the prisoner, the [Ovissian](/wiki/Ovissian "Ovissian") miner [Boolio](/wiki/Boolio "Boolio"), hauled before him to face summary execution by decapitation. After carrying out the deed himself, Ren joined the members of the Supreme Council in the High Command chamber where he slammed the spy's severed head on the conference table. While he acknowledged that there was another spy, one within their ranks, Ren was unconcerned with discovering their identity, feeling confident that the First Order would become a true Empire once it had assimilated the military assets he discovered on Exegol.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

Ren listened as the Council discussed their new strategy. Parnadee and Engell proposed increasing their recruitment quotas by conscripting more children into the military. Quinn was skeptical of their alliance with the Sith Eternal, disdaining the cultists and their beliefs. Pryde, however, supported integration between the two forces, arguing that the Sith fleet would increase the First Order's range in power by ten-thousand fold, replacing the losses they suffered with the destruction of Starkiller Base, which he held Hux responsible for. Unlike the other officers, the Allegiant General did not fear Ren, who had considered liquidating Pryde but ultimately found him too competent to replace.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

 [![The discovery of new warships and soldiers bolstered the Supreme Council's confidence in the young Supreme Leader.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/First-Order-Supreme_Council.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200313073650) [![The discovery of new warships and soldiers bolstered the Supreme Council's confidence in the young Supreme Leader.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/First-Order-Supreme_Council.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20200313073650)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/First-Order-Supreme_Council.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200313073650) 

The discovery of new warships and soldiers bolstered the Supreme Council's confidence in the young Supreme Leader.

 

Ren moved to silence Quinn when the general began inquiring about the specific terms of his agreement with Sidious, preventing the Council from learning of the Emperor's interest in Rey. Using his anger and impatience to fuel his connection to the dark side, he threw Quinn up to the ceiling, causing his body to fracture upon impact. The Council watched silently as their colleague remained suspended above them, slowly choking to death while Ren informed the remaining members of his intention to personally oversee the hunt for Rey with the support of his Knights. Meanwhile, the Council was instructed to maintain order in the galaxy by suppressing any worlds exhibiting signs of dissent.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Though they preferred conquering the galaxy through orthodox tactics and strategies rather than relying on Ren's total devotion to the dark side of the Force, their confidence in his leadership had increased with his promise of the Sith armada.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5)

#### Hunting Rey on Pasaana

:   "*I offered you my hand once. You wanted to take it. Why didn't you?*"  
    "*You could have killed me. Why didn't you?*"  
    "*You can't hide, Rey. Not from me.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren and Rey[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

 [![Ren used his bond with Rey to find her, and also to warn her that Sidious wanted him to kill her.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/12/ReyOnPasana-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200306003418) [![Ren used his bond with Rey to find her, and also to warn her that Sidious wanted him to kill her.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/12/ReyOnPasana-TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200306003418)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/12/ReyOnPasana-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200306003418) 

Ren used his bond with Rey to find her, and also to warn her that Sidious wanted him to kill her.

 

Allegiant General Pryde reported to Ren that the First Order had been unsuccessful in their search for the scavenger, and Hux offered to personally lead the kill squads against her. Ren ordered Pryde to target ships in the same class as the *Millennium Falcon*, and informed Hux that the search for Rey was too important to risk error; as such, the Knights of Ren would lead the mission instead.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

In his private quarters on the *Steadfast*, Ren used his bond with Rey to initiate a connection. Unbeknownst to Ren, she was in the [Forbidden Valley](/wiki/Forbidden_Valley "Forbidden Valley") of [Pasaana](/wiki/Pasaana "Pasaana") during the [Festival of the Ancestors](/wiki/Festival_of_the_Ancestors "Festival of the Ancestors"), [seeking the way to Exegol](/wiki/Mission_to_Pasaana_(Resistance) "Mission to Pasaana (Resistance)"). It was their most powerful connection yet, showing them each other as if physically present in each other's locations without any other sounds or beings there.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) He told her that the Emperor desired her death, but that he had no intention of serving another master and followed his own plan instead. Ren asked her why she had rejected his offer on the *Supremacy*, knowing that she wanted to accept it. Rey avoided the question and asked why he had not taken the opportunity to kill her when he had the chance. He responded that she could not hide from him.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

 [![The Knights of Ren journeyed to Pasaana with the intention of capturing the scavenger who vexed their dark master.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/KnightsOfRen-DB.png/revision/latest?cb=20220509230610) [![The Knights of Ren journeyed to Pasaana with the intention of capturing the scavenger who vexed their dark master.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/KnightsOfRen-DB.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220509230610)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/KnightsOfRen-DB.png/revision/latest?cb=20220509230610) 

The Knights of Ren journeyed to Pasaana with the intention of capturing the scavenger who vexed their dark master.

 

Ren's thoughts betrayed that he was still affected by killing his father, and when Rey threw into his mind the image of him killing Han, he confronted her with her own memory of counting the days since her parents left her.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Ren claimed that his mother and Rey's friends did not recognize the dark side in her as he did. He said that he could sense her anger and pain and stated that he did not want to have to kill her, but he would find her and turn her to the dark side. Before their connection ended, he ripped the [husk necklace](/wiki/Husk_necklace "Husk necklace") from her neck which physically transported it from Rey's location to Ren's hand.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

Ren informed Pryde that he had found Rey through the Force, and [intelligence officer](/wiki/Intelligence_officer "Intelligence officer") [Tishra Kandia](/wiki/Tishra_Kandia "Tishra Kandia") returned with her analysis of the necklace; it was made in the [Middian system](/wiki/Middian_system "Middian system"), specifically the Forbidden Valley. Ren ordered Pryde to immediately deploy a division of local troops and to prepare his ship for departure.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) While Ren was unaware of the purpose of Rey's presence on Pasaana, he had hope that he would soon find her.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

Shortly after Ren's arrival on Pasaana, the *Millennium Falcon* was found by the Knights of Ren and their stormtrooper escorts. The Supreme Leader ordered them to confiscate and scan the ship before finally destroying it. Meanwhile, Rey sensed Ren's presence in the Force as his ship drew closer to her location.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) As Ren prepared to confront her, he realized that killing his father had not eliminated his pull to the light because Rey remained as his light. Until Ren killed her or the light inside her, he could not fully claim the darkness.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

 [![Ren confronted Rey in the Pasaana desert, determined to confirm what he had learned about her origins.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/KyloRen-PasaanaDesert.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200728054525) [![Ren confronted Rey in the Pasaana desert, determined to confirm what he had learned about her origins.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/KyloRen-PasaanaDesert.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200728054525)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/KyloRen-PasaanaDesert.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200728054525) 

Ren confronted Rey in the Pasaana desert, determined to confirm what he had learned about her origins.

 

Ren increased the speed of his TIE whisper, flying it directly towards Rey with the intention of killing her.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Rey used her training under Organa and the Force augmenting her abilities to flip backwards over his ship, cutting the support pylon of his left wing with her lightsaber. Ren attempted to compensate, but lost control of the starfighter as it tumbled and ripped apart.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

Despite the violent crash, Ren emerged from the burning wreckage unharmed. By then, Rey was straining with the Force to stop a First Order transport from leaving the planet, believing that Chewbacca had been taken aboard as a prisoner of the First Order. Ren reached out towards the vessel using his own powers trying to pull the transport out of Rey's grip.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) He wanted to provoke her anger to gauge her true potential and determine the truth of her connection to the Emperor.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) A tug of war ensued over the shuttle, causing Rey to give into her feelings and unwittingly channel the power of the dark side until Force lightning emanated from her fingertips. The transport to exploded to Rey's horror and Ren's astonishment. He watched from a distance as a [derelict freighter](/wiki/Bestoon_Legacy "Bestoon Legacy") took off, leaving Pasaana with Rey and her companions aboard it.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) To Ren, this was confirmation that she was close to turning to the dark side and joining him in seizing the Sith throne and fleet.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

#### Confronting Rey with the truth

:   "*My mother was the daughter of Vader. Your father was the son of the Emperor. What Palpatine doesn't know is that we're a dyad in the Force, Rey. Two that are one.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren, to Rey[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

 [![Ren ordered his forces on Kijimi to hunt down Rey and her companions.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/KijimiGarrison-TROSVD.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200118043255) [![Ren ordered his forces on Kijimi to hunt down Rey and her companions.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/KijimiGarrison-TROSVD.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200118043255)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3e/KijimiGarrison-TROSVD.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200118043255) 

Ren ordered his forces on Kijimi to hunt down Rey and her companions.

 

When Ren returned to the *Steadfast*, Pryde and Hux presented him with the First Order's newest prisoner, Chewbacca; he had been on a second transport, not the one that Rey destroyed.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) Ren taunted Chewbacca before interrogating his mind with the Force to discover the purpose of Rey's visit to Pasaana. Ren sifted through Chewbacca's memories of both Han and Ben Solo, including "Uncle Chewie" teaching young Ben to shoot a blaster and fly a speeder. Though Ren discovered the information he sought, he struggled to center his thoughts after the interrogation was complete. He ordered his officers to have Chewbacca's belongings brought to his quarters.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

Pryde and Griss informed Ren that his Knights had tracked Rey to a [settlement](/wiki/Kijimi_City "Kijimi City") on the [occupied world](/wiki/Occupation_of_Kijimi "Occupation of Kijimi") of [Kijimi](/wiki/Kijimi "Kijimi"). Ren rejected Hux's proposal to destroy the city as Ren wanted Rey captured alive. The local [First Order garrison](/wiki/Kijimi_garrison "Kijimi garrison") unsuccessfully searched for Rey's team. Unknown to Ren, the arrival of the *Steadfast* at Kijimi allowed Rey to sense Ren's conflicted mind and realize that Chewbacca was still alive. Her team infiltrated the *Steadfast* to rescue him.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) Ren arrived in Kijimi City afterward, and overcome by frustration, he used his lightsaber to destroy several inanimate objects before ordering a lockdown on the city.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

 [![The bond between Ren and Rey was stronger than ever before, allowing them to exist within each other's minds and spaces.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5f/Force-bond_battle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200110053029) [![The bond between Ren and Rey was stronger than ever before, allowing them to exist within each other's minds and spaces.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5f/Force-bond_battle.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20200110053029)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5f/Force-bond_battle.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200110053029) 

The bond between Ren and Rey was stronger than ever before, allowing them to exist within each other's minds and spaces.

 

After Rey entered Ren's quarters, she touched the [Blade of Ochi of Bestoon](/wiki/Blade_of_Ochi_of_Bestoon "Blade of Ochi of Bestoon") which triggered memories of her parents. Her vision changed into a Force connection with Ren. They were in each other's minds and spaces, and were physically together, yet still separate at the same time. Ren told Rey that he had gained knowledge about her past and disputed her accusation that he was a liar. Ren stated that he never lied to her.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) While she believed him, she knew that he used the truth for his dishonest intentions.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Ignoring that she repeatedly told him to stop and that she did not want this, he forced her to remember what she had suppressed and listen to what he had learned; her [father](/wiki/Dathan "Dathan") and [mother](/wiki/Miramir "Miramir") chose to be "no one" in order to keep their daughter safe as Sidious' assassin [Ochi](/wiki/Ochi "Ochi") hunted her family. Rey saw a vision of Ochi killing her parents.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

During this confrontation, they engaged in a lightsaber duel and caused damage to each other's surroundings. Red berries from Kijimi spilled across the floor of Ren's quarters on the *Steadfast*, and their blades slashed through the obsidian pedestal supporting Vader's mask. The mask was transported to Ren, which revealed Rey's location to him before the connection ended.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) He ordered his troops to lock down the Star Destroyer to prevent Rey's escape so he could reveal her origins to her in person.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

 [![Ren revealed to Rey their nature as a dyad in the Force, a phenomenon which he explained as "two that were one](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6d/Dyad.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20211012225649) [![Ren revealed to Rey their nature as a dyad in the Force, a phenomenon which he explained as "two that were one](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6d/Dyad.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20211012225649)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6d/Dyad.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20211012225649) 

Ren revealed to Rey their nature as a dyad in the Force, a phenomenon which he explained as "two that were one."

 

Rey sensed Ren's presence upon his return to the *Steadfast* and decided to confront him while her friends escaped from the warship, not wanting them to risk their lives against the dark side warrior. A contingent of stormtroopers also arrived as Ren disembarked from his TIE whisper and cornered Rey at the hangar entrance. When Rey asked Ren why Sidious had tried to kill her when she was a child, the Supreme Leader revealed that Rey had inherited her powers from her paternal grandfather, the Emperor. In addition to the revelation of Rey's secret connection to the [Palpatine bloodline](/wiki/Palpatine_family "Palpatine family"), Ren disclosed his discovery of their shared nature as a dyad, making them one presence in the Force. The true extent of their connection was a secret that Ren kept from Sidious, whose death he plotted in order to claim the [Throne of the Sith](/wiki/Throne_of_the_Sith "Throne of the Sith") with Rey.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

 [![Ren removed his helmet, allowing Rey to see his face as he invited her to join him against her grandfather, the Emperor.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/Ben_Solo_or_Kylo_Ren_IX_TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191222114716) [![Ren removed his helmet, allowing Rey to see his face as he invited her to join him against her grandfather, the Emperor.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/Ben_Solo_or_Kylo_Ren_IX_TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191222114716)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/Ben_Solo_or_Kylo_Ren_IX_TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191222114716) 

Ren removed his helmet, allowing Rey to see his face as he invited her to join him against her grandfather, the Emperor.

 

As a sign of trust Ren removed his mask, allowing Rey to see his face along with the scar that she had given him in their first battle.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Ren, who was convinced that he had eradicated the last trace of his former persona, also wanted Rey to realize that he was fully committed to the ways of the dark side.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) Ren's invitation to join him reminded Rey of the offer that he made to her in Snoke's throne room. While their victory over Snoke compelled Rey to acknowledge the potential of their combined power, she remained committed to the Resistance's cause.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Following a moment of indecision,[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) Rey chose to reject Ren once more when the *Millennium Falcon* arrived at the hangar entrance. The starship's engines forced the stormtroopers back, though Ren braced himself with the Force, watching Rey as she boarded his late father's ship.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

Ren knew from the analysis of Ochi's dagger that Rey would next travel to [Kef Bir](/wiki/Kef_Bir "Kef Bir"), an ocean moon located in the [Endor system](/wiki/Endor_system "Endor system"). While en route to the system, Sidious contacted Ren through the Force. His cloned body had further deteriorated, yet Ren was impressed by Sidious' ability to commune with another being across light-years. Sidious threatened to turn his fleet against Ren if he did not kill Rey. While mentally shielding his true intentions, Ren assured Sidious that he knew where Rey had gone and declared that he would not allow her to become a Jedi.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

Despite the escape of the *Millennium Falcon*'s crew, the incident aboard the *Steadfast* revealed Hux's efforts to undermine Ren. Hux failed to convince Pryde that the Resistance used coercion to enlist his aid; consequently, the general was executed for committing espionage against the First Order. Pryde then instructed his subordinates to inform the Supreme Leader that they had found the Resistance's spy.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

#### The last duel

:   "*You were right. I did want to take your hand.* Ben's *hand.*"
:   ―Rey, to Kylo Ren[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

 [![Ren cornered Rey in the ruins of the second Death Star, where their respective grandfathers met their demise.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ab/A_Dyad_in_the_Force.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20230129161947) [![Ren cornered Rey in the ruins of the second Death Star, where their respective grandfathers met their demise.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ab/A_Dyad_in_the_Force.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20230129161947)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ab/A_Dyad_in_the_Force.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20230129161947) 

Ren cornered Rey in the ruins of the second Death Star, where their respective grandfathers met their demise.

 

Ren [confronted](/wiki/Mission_to_Kef_Bir "Mission to Kef Bir") Rey within the wreckage of the [Emperor's Throne Room](/wiki/Emperor%27s_Throne_Room "Emperor's Throne Room") in the [ruins](/wiki/Death_Star_ruins "Death Star ruins") of the second [Death Star](/wiki/Death_Star "Death Star"). After Rey found the [Emperor's wayfinder](/wiki/Emperor%27s_wayfinder "Emperor's wayfinder"), she retreated from the dark side vision of her mirror-self and dropped the wayfinder. To her horror, Ren picked it up.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) His appearance there felt like both her worst nightmare and destiny.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) As she demanded the wayfinder, Ren claimed she had proven she was not a Jedi, and like him, could never return to Leia Organa. He urged her to surrender to the dark side, and declared that she would never find her way to Exegol without his help. He crushed the wayfinder in his hand.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

 [![The Supreme Leader and the former scavenger fought amidst the Death Star ruins as well as the raging ocean waves of Kef Bir.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/KyloReyKefBirDuel-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200623143830) [![The Supreme Leader and the former scavenger fought amidst the Death Star ruins as well as the raging ocean waves of Kef Bir.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/KyloReyKefBirDuel-TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20200623143830)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/KyloReyKefBirDuel-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200623143830) 

The Supreme Leader and the former scavenger fought amidst the Death Star ruins as well as the raging ocean waves of Kef Bir.

 

Rey immediately attacked Ren,[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) drawing on her anger to amplify her power as she sought to kill him.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) He initially evaded her lightsaber before defending himself with his own. They dueled through the Death Star wreckage and outside onto a bridge-like hunk of metal while the ocean raged around them. During the fight, Finn approached them and Rey instinctively pushed him away with the Force to protect him. She leapt to another section of the ruins to avoid the massive waves and Ren followed her across to continue the fight.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) As they fought, Ren communicated with Rey through telepathy, insisting that he knew her despite her words to the contrary. Ren's guard remained unbroken despite how her anger flooded her with additional Force energy. He was physically stronger, and though she was a little faster, she was tiring and slowing due to lack of sleep and not recovering from healing the [vexis](/wiki/Vexis "Vexis") on Pasaana.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Ren, however, withstood a colossal wave and continued to advance.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

 [![During the duel, Ren withstood a colossal wave to show Rey that he could withstand anything.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6c/Kylo_Ren_IX_TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250210210134) [![During the duel, Ren withstood a colossal wave to show Rey that he could withstand anything.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6c/Kylo_Ren_IX_TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250210210134)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6c/Kylo_Ren_IX_TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250210210134) 

During the duel, Ren withstood a colossal wave to show Rey that he could withstand anything.

 

Ren's anger and hatred fueled his attacks[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) as he drove the exhausted Rey back and knocked her off her feet, which caused her to lose her grip on her lightsaber.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) As he raised his lightsaber above her, she believed she was about to die.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10)

Then Ren stopped; from across the galaxy, he sensed his mother use her remaining reserves of strength to send him her love, forgiveness, and hope as she called him to the light.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) He dropped his lightsaber as he felt her death.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) Exulting at the prospect of victory,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Rey caught his lightsaber and moved to kill him[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) by running his abdomen through with his own blade.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

 [![When the duel ended, Rey healed Kylo Ren's wound and confessed that she wanted to take Ben Solo's hand.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/Rey_heals_Kylo_Ren.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200410013209) [![When the duel ended, Rey healed Kylo Ren's wound and confessed that she wanted to take Ben Solo's hand.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/Rey_heals_Kylo_Ren.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20200410013209)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/Rey_heals_Kylo_Ren.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200410013209) 

When the duel ended, Rey healed Kylo Ren's wound and confessed that she wanted to take Ben Solo's hand.

 

Ren collapsed to the ground in physical and emotional agony as Rey sensed Organa's death through the Force.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) Sharing Ren's grief for Organa and no longer wishing to see him die,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Rey reached out to the wound that would have meant his certain death.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) She transferred much of her life force to his body to repair his wound, even mending the scar that she had inflicted on his face in their first duel[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) and making whole again his burned flesh and damaged organs, clearing his mind as well.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7) Ren was astonished by her actions and her demonstration of a power that he had not known existed.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Before leaving him on Kef Bir, Rey admitted that he had been correct about her wanting to take his hand, but not Kylo Ren's; she had wanted to take Ben Solo's hand.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

### The return of Ben Solo

#### The death of Kylo Ren

:   "*I miss you, son.*"  
    "*Your son is dead.*"  
    "*No. Kylo Ren is dead. My son is alive.*"  
    "*You're just a memory.*"  
    "*Your memory.* "
:   ―Han Solo (memory) and Ben Solo[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

 [![The memory of Han Solo helped his son, Ben Solo, overcome the dark persona of Kylo Ren.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/BenSoloandHanSolo-TROS.png/revision/latest?cb=20230129165834) [![The memory of Han Solo helped his son, Ben Solo, overcome the dark persona of Kylo Ren.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/BenSoloandHanSolo-TROS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20230129165834)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/BenSoloandHanSolo-TROS.png/revision/latest?cb=20230129165834) 

The memory of Han Solo helped his son, Ben Solo, overcome the dark persona of Kylo Ren.

 

The actions of his mother and Rey threw Ren's mind into turmoil as he sought to understand their reasons. He stood on the wreckage of the battle station while thinking of the voices in his mind and how they convinced him that his family never loved him. He also thought of his old master, Supreme Leader Snoke, who conditioned Ren to believe what the voices said to him. However, as a result of his mother's effort to reach him at the cost of her life, Ren found himself questioning everything he had been led to believe about the dark side, his family, and himself. In addition, he tried to understand Rey's reason for healing him.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

His deep contemplation gave way to the memory of his late father, Han Solo, who manifested before Ren as a vision. Though the voices in his mind convinced Ren that it was too late for repentance, the vision of Han told him that he missed his son and it was not too late to fight for his mother's legacy. Ren was overcome by the emotions drawn out of him by his father's memory, and though he still questioned his resolve, uncertain if he was strong enough to do what he believed needed to be done, his father reassured him that he was strong. Ren ultimately made his choice by throwing his lightsaber into the sea. In that moment, he ceased to be Kylo Ren and became Ben Solo once again.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

#### Battle of Exegol

:   "*As once I fell, so falls the last Skywalker.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious, to Ben Solo[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

 [![Claiming the lightsaber of Anakin Skywalker as his own, Ben Solo destroyed the Knights of Ren during the Battle of Exegol.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f3/KyloFacesTheKnightsOfRen.png/revision/latest?cb=20200325083206) [![Claiming the lightsaber of Anakin Skywalker as his own, Ben Solo destroyed the Knights of Ren during the Battle of Exegol.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f3/KyloFacesTheKnightsOfRen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20200325083206)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f3/KyloFacesTheKnightsOfRen.png/revision/latest?cb=20200325083206) 

Claiming the lightsaber of Anakin Skywalker as his own, Ben Solo destroyed the Knights of Ren during the Battle of Exegol.

 

Stranded on Kef Bir, Solo climbed through the ruins of the Death Star in search of a hangar bay. He eventually found and repaired an old [TIE scout](/wiki/TIE_scout "TIE scout"). After leaving the ocean moon, Solo followed Rey's transmitted tracking markers towards Exegol, but the scout's navicomputers malfunctioned and threw its pilot off course. Solo, however, used all of his concentration to correct his course, thereby preventing his starfighter from becoming lost in unknown space.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

The [Battle of Exegol](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol") was under way by the time of Solo's arrival. The Sith fleet was in the process of launching its warships when the Resistance attacked Exegol, attempting to stop the fleet's deployment across the galaxy. Solo landed his TIE scout next to Rey's starfighter, an old Rebellion [T-65B X-wing starfighter](/wiki/T-65B_X-wing_starfighter "T-65B X-wing starfighter") that had once [belonged to Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Red_Five_(T-65B_X-wing_starfighter) "Red Five (T-65B X-wing starfighter)"). Sensing Rey's presence emanating from the Sith Citadel, he sprinted for the monolith and descended to the lower levels to find her. Armed only with a blaster pistol and his own conviction, Solo charged through the cavernous cathedral beneath the citadel, shooting his way through the Sith cultists and [elite guards](/wiki/Sovereign_Protector "Sovereign Protector") who obstructed his path. As he drew closer to the [throne room](/wiki/Amphitheater_of_the_Sith_Eternal "Amphitheater of the Sith Eternal"), the Knights of Ren appeared before him. Their hatred pulsated like waves through the Force, and Solo realized that they had traveled to Exegol to fight for Sidious, their true master.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

 [![Standing together as a true dyad, Ben Solo and Rey confronted the clone remnant of Darth Sidious.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/Ben-and-Rey-on-Exegol.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200826185249) [![Standing together as a true dyad, Ben Solo and Rey confronted the clone remnant of Darth Sidious.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/Ben-and-Rey-on-Exegol.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20200826185249)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/Ben-and-Rey-on-Exegol.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200826185249) 

Standing together as a true dyad, Ben Solo and Rey confronted the clone remnant of Darth Sidious.

 

The six Force-sensitive warriors initially held the upper hand, as their numbers, weapons and training worked to their advantage against their former leader. Solo sustained blunt force trauma to his abdomen and the back of his skull, being hit several times by his opponents' melee weapons. The Knights refrained from killing him outright, as they were confident in their ability to defeat a single opponent who appeared defenseless before them. They circled for another attack, but to their surprise, Solo revealed a blue-bladed lightsaber in his palm. It was the lightsaber that once belonged to his grandfather and uncle, in turn, and had been carried by Rey until she passed it to Solo through their bond as a dyad. He instantly recognized it as his lightsaber, as it had become an extension of his own self.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

Thinking of what his father would say in this moment,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Solo simply shrugged his shoulders at the Knights, knowing now that the odds were in his favor.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) Armed with the blade of the Chosen One himself, Solo immediately pressed the attack with all the focus of a Jedi,[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) killing Cardo and Kuruk with a single swing of the saber to their chests.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) Simultaneously, Rey ignited her spare weapon, [Leia Organa's lightsaber](/wiki/Leia%27s_lightsaber "Leia's lightsaber"), as several of the Emperor's guards surrounded her. As before on Pasaana and Kijimi, Solo and Rey were separate and together at the same time, with Rey battling the crimson-robed guards and Solo confronting his former comrades. This time, however, they were drawing on each other for strength, becoming even more powerful as one instead of two. Though he destroyed the Knights of Ren,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Solo did so without feelings of hatred or anger towards them, electing to give them the quick deaths that they had denied to those they had killed.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10)
