 [![Having discovered that Solo and Rey were a dyad, Sidious drained them of their essences in order to regain his unlimited power.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Force_drained_by_Sidious.png/revision/latest?cb=20200410073238) [![Having discovered that Solo and Rey were a dyad, Sidious drained them of their essences in order to regain his unlimited power.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Force_drained_by_Sidious.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20200410073238)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Force_drained_by_Sidious.png/revision/latest?cb=20200410073238) 

Having discovered that Solo and Rey were a dyad, Sidious drained them of their essences in order to regain his unlimited power.

 

Arriving in the throne room, Solo used the Force to incapacitate the last guardsman and approached Rey. They turned towards the Emperor, standing side-by-side with their lightsabers raised, to which Sidious exclaimed that they would die together. Despite their combined strength, the two Force users were overpowered by Sidious' attack through the Force. As a side effect, however, part of their life force transferred to the Emperor and began healing his cloned body. Sidious was astonished, realizing that his granddaughter and Vader's grandson were a dyad in the Force, and therefore, possessed a power equivalent to life itself.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

Neither Solo nor Rey were able to prevent the Emperor from draining them of more Force energy. They became weaker as Sidious completely restored the vessel that carried his spirit. Their near lifeless bodies lay on the floor while the Emperor reveled in his restoration. In retaliation for his own death at Vader's hand,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Sidious scornfully proclaimed to Solo that he would fall as the last Skywalker, hurling the young Jedi into a nearby chasm.[[54]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_Bio_Gallery-54)

#### Redemption and sacrifice

:   "*Ben…*"
:   ―Rey, to Ben Solo[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

 [![Ben Solo sacrificed himself for the love of another, as Anakin Skywalker once had, restoring Rey to life.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/Compassion-SWZ87_Chris_Bjors.png/revision/latest?cb=20240811031838) [![Ben Solo sacrificed himself for the love of another, as Anakin Skywalker once had, restoring Rey to life.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/Compassion-SWZ87_Chris_Bjors.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20240811031838)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/Compassion-SWZ87_Chris_Bjors.png/revision/latest?cb=20240811031838) 

Ben Solo sacrificed himself for the love of another, as Anakin Skywalker once had, restoring Rey to life.

 

Solo survived due to his body being caught on a jagged outcropping. Despite breaking his ribs and twisting his ankle in the fall, he began climbing his way out of the chasm through perseverance. At the same time, Rey succeeded in destroying her grandfather with the help of the spirits of the Jedi,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) although the monumental effort left her dead.[[67]](#cite_note-Rey_Bio_Gallery-67) She reached out with the Force, trying to find Solo through their bond as her remaining life force faded from her body.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

After returning to the surface, Solo took Rey's body in his arms and, realizing that she was dead, began to despair. However, he sensed a spark of her essence and realized that the Force had not yet claimed her. Recalling the way she used the Force to heal him on Kef Bir, Solo applied the same technique on Rey, willing her to return to life.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) He took the life energy that she had given to him and returned it to its original source along with all that remained of his own essence.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) In the process he found "reservoirs of power" that he did not know he possessed, yet devoted all of it in his efforts to revive Rey.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

 [![Rey kissed Solo during his final moments, acknowledging their bond as a dyad for the first time.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/BenandReyKiss-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200329212013) [![Rey kissed Solo during his final moments, acknowledging their bond as a dyad for the first time.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/BenandReyKiss-TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200329212013)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/BenandReyKiss-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200329212013) 

Rey kissed Solo during his final moments, acknowledging their bond as a dyad for the first time.

 

Solo ultimately succeeded in bringing Rey back to life, though the effort would cost him his own life. During his final moments, Solo was surprised to see that Rey was glad to be with him. He believed that he did not deserve acknowledgement or gratitude from her, but to his astonishment Rey kissed him, acknowledging their bond as a dyad for the first time. His final awareness was of Rey holding his hand as the Force beckoned him, reaching for Solo in welcome. He died peacefully,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) having felt no hesitation about sacrificing his life for Rey.[[1]](#cite_note-TSWB-1)

### Afterlife

:   "*I will always be with you.*"  
    "*No one's ever really gone.*"
:   ―Ben Solo's final words and Rey's response[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

Death reunited Ben Solo with his mother, Organa, who did not pass into the Force until she was joined by her son.[[1]](#cite_note-TSWB-1) Their corporeal forms vanished simultaneously,[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) allowing mother and son to rest in peace together, becoming one with the [Cosmic Force](/wiki/Cosmic_Force "Cosmic Force").[[1]](#cite_note-TSWB-1)

Rey felt despair as she watched Solo's body disappear until he called out to her from beyond death, promising that he would always be with her. She took comfort in hearing his voice as it reassured her that no one who died was truly gone.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

### Legacy

:   "*And when you called yourself by that new name, you saw your* truth*. It represents what you want to do on a deep level. The part of yourself you want to cut away. The part you want to* kill*. Perhaps someday you will do it. The galaxy will hear that name and* see you*.*"
:   ―Snoke, to Ben Solo[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25)

 [![The reign of Kylo Ren ended with the redemption of Ben Solo and the fall of the First Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/Uprising_on_Cloud_City.png/revision/latest?cb=20200315163622) [![The reign of Kylo Ren ended with the redemption of Ben Solo and the fall of the First Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/Uprising_on_Cloud_City.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200315163622)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/Uprising_on_Cloud_City.png/revision/latest?cb=20200315163622) 

The reign of Kylo Ren ended with the redemption of Ben Solo and the fall of the First Order.

 

Following the deaths of Kylo Ren, Enric Pryde, and Darth Sidious, a popular [uprising against the First Order](/wiki/Uprising_against_the_First_Order "Uprising against the First Order") commenced as a consequence of the Sith fleet's destruction on Exegol. The First Order subsequently lost its control over[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) the empire that it fought to create through conquest during Ren's reign as Supreme Leader,[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) losing worlds, such as [Corellia](/wiki/Uprising_on_Corellia "Uprising on Corellia"), [Coruscant](/wiki/Uprising_on_Coruscant "Uprising on Coruscant"), [Lothal](/wiki/Uprising_on_Lothal "Uprising on Lothal"), [Naboo](/wiki/Uprising_on_Naboo_(First_Order) "Uprising on Naboo (First Order)"), and [Thyferra](/wiki/Uprising_on_Thyferra "Uprising on Thyferra").[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) Other revolts against the First Order occurred on [Endor](/wiki/Uprising_on_Endor "Uprising on Endor"), [Bespin](/wiki/Uprising_on_Cloud_City "Uprising on Cloud City"), and [Jakku](/wiki/Uprising_on_Jakku "Uprising on Jakku"), where *Resurgent*-class Star Destroyers sustained significant damage as a result of the uprisings, causing the warships to fall out of orbit. News of the uprisings reached the generals Poe Dameron and Finn by the time the Resistance returned to Ajan Kloss to celebrate their victory against the Emperor and his followers.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) Rey, having been revived through Ben Solo's sacrifice,[[1]](#cite_note-TSWB-1) had also returned to the Resistance's secret base where she embraced her friends.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

 [![Though redeemed as Ben Solo, Kylo Ren left a legacy of death and destruction that rivaled Darth Vader.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fe/Kneelren.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20201222195819) [![Though redeemed as Ben Solo, Kylo Ren left a legacy of death and destruction that rivaled Darth Vader.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fe/Kneelren.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201222195819)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fe/Kneelren.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20201222195819) 

Though redeemed as Ben Solo, Kylo Ren left a legacy of death and destruction that rivaled Darth Vader.

 

Despite Kylo Ren's efforts to live up to the memory of Darth Vader, in the end Ben Solo emulated Anakin Skywalker by sacrificing his life "for the love of another." He achieved redemption with his final act,[[54]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_Bio_Gallery-54) returning to the light side[[1]](#cite_note-TSWB-1) and passing into the Force[[54]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_Bio_Gallery-54) as a Jedi.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7) Rey mourned the death of Ben Solo while rejecting his dark-side persona as Kylo Ren.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) The amount of death and destruction caused by Ren rivaled the legacy of his grandfather, Darth Vader.[[1]](#cite_note-TSWB-1) Nevertheless, Rey chose to remember him as Ben Solo rather than Kylo Ren. Following the Emperor's destruction, Rey acknowledged Solo as the reason for her success in resisting the dark side's temptations in addition to other influences such as her friends and the legacy of the Jedi Order. While she took comfort in the knowledge that Solo remained with her in spirit, she expressed a sense of loss and disappointment about[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) his passing into the Force,[[54]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_Bio_Gallery-54) having lost the opportunity to know Ben Solo as the person he was before he became Kylo Ren.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

The other individuals who remembered Solo were his father's friends, Chewbacca and Lando Calrissian,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) both of whom Solo had considered his "uncles" during his childhood.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7) Ren had become the focus of Chewbacca's fury for the killing of Han Solo; however, the Wookiee retained joyful memories of his relationship with the Solo family, which included the time he spent helping to raise Ben. Among Chewbacca's possessions was a [hologram disc](/wiki/Hologram_disc "Hologram disc") that contained a picture of the Wookiee holding Ben Solo as an infant. The disc was hidden in a secret compartment beside Chewbacca's bunk on the *Millennium Falcon*; Calrissian discovered the disc prior to the Battle of Exegol and could not bear to look at an image of Han's son, [his own child](/wiki/Kadara_Calrissian "Kadara Calrissian") having been abducted by the First Order.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

 [![Ben Solo's death marked the end of the Skywalker bloodline.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/05/The_Skywalkers.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220502025527) [![Ben Solo's death marked the end of the Skywalker bloodline.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/05/The_Skywalkers.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220502025527)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/05/The_Skywalkers.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220502025527) 

Ben Solo's death marked the end of the Skywalker bloodline.

 

In the aftermath of Solo's death, Rey visited Tatooine where she buried the Skywalker lightsabers in the [childhood home](/wiki/Lars_homestead "Lars homestead") of her first master, Luke Skywalker. Her mind dwelt on Solo as she looked over the horizon at the planet's [twin](/wiki/Tatoo_I "Tatoo I") [suns](/wiki/Tatoo_II "Tatoo II"), reflecting on how he helped her to defeat Darth Sidious.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) The Skywalker bloodline ended with Ben Solo, but its legacy was preserved by Rey, who chose "Skywalker" as her surname to honor the family that accepted her[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) in spite of her secret heritage as a Palpatine.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

## Personality and traits

### The Skywalker heir

:   "*Alas, you're no Vader. You're just a child in a mask.*"
:   ―Snoke[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

 [![Ben Solo was a scion of the Skywalker family who shared similar traits with his forebears.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/BenSolo-SWTLC.png/revision/latest?cb=20230401012208) [![Ben Solo was a scion of the Skywalker family who shared similar traits with his forebears.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/BenSolo-SWTLC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230401012208)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/BenSolo-SWTLC.png/revision/latest?cb=20230401012208) 

Ben Solo was a scion of the Skywalker family who shared similar traits with his forebears.

 

Ben Solo was a [human](/wiki/Human "Human") [male](/wiki/Gender "Gender")[[4]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_DB-4) who stood at 1.89 meters[[106]](#cite_note-CEUE-106) and weighed 89 [kilograms](/wiki/Kilogram "Kilogram").[[6]](#cite_note-TFA_head_to_head-6) He had dark brown hair, light skin, and brown eyes[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) that appeared ancient to his father when Solo was a child.[[30]](#cite_note-Last_Shot-30) There was a strong family resemblance between Solo and his parents; he had his father's long face and posture,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) as well as his pronounced [nose](/wiki/Nose "Nose") and lopsided smile.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7) He also had his mother's warm,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) piercing brown eyes, a feature Organa was sure was inherited from her own birth mother, Padmé Amidala.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7) He also mirrored his parents in personality, whether as Kylo Ren[[62]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Hux-62) or Ben Solo.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) He was very much like his mother, as observed by General Armitage Hux, who believed that Ren would have denied the comparison.[[62]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Hux-62) He also had his father's sarcastic sense of humor,[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) which sometimes emerged in serious or violent situations.[[63]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Kylo-63)[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) However, Solo was also similar to his grandfather, to the dismay of his parents who saw "too much of Vader" within their son.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

Possessing an inquisitive mind, Solo endeavored to gain greater knowledge of the Force[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) and the Jedi ways[[43]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-43) during his apprenticeship under Skywalker.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) Solo was particularly interested in ancient Jedi weapons; on one occasion, he marveled at a lightsaber rifle.[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25) He practiced the art of fancy [handwriting](/wiki/Writing "Writing") or "calligraphy,"[[43]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-43) an art that had fallen into disuse as almost no one wrote by hand during the era of the New Republic.[[11]](#cite_note-Bloodline-11) He recorded his handwritten insights into the Jedi on parchment scrolls which he kept next to his calligraphy set.[[43]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-43) His interests included dark aspects of the Force not taught by Skywalker.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) After Solo became Kylo Ren, he studied both Jedi and arcane dark side lore, using these contradictory teachings for greater power.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50)

 [![Solo's skills as a Jedi under Luke Skywalker grew to a point where he surpassed multiple students put together.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7a/TalkingBehindLukesBack-TheRiseOfKyloRen2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200217034613) [![Solo's skills as a Jedi under Luke Skywalker grew to a point where he surpassed multiple students put together.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7a/TalkingBehindLukesBack-TheRiseOfKyloRen2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200217034613)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7a/TalkingBehindLukesBack-TheRiseOfKyloRen2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200217034613) 

Solo's skills as a Jedi under Luke Skywalker grew to a point where he surpassed multiple students put together.

 

When Skywalker's attention was divided by teaching multiple students, Solo turned to the dark voice he knew as Snoke. Solo struggled with the expectations of his family legacy;[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) he was descended from some of the most powerful Jedi and Sith in galactic [history](/wiki/Timeline_of_galactic_history "Timeline of galactic history"). Supreme Leader Snoke considered Ren a focal point between the dark side and the light,[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) a balance that made him a target of Snoke so Ren's powers could be used to further the ambitions of the First Order. His fall to the dark side suppressed the boy who had once been named Ben Solo.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) Solo burned and destroyed the Jedi temple[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) while furious that his uncle had apparently tried to kill him. He was immediately horrified and tried in vain to help his fellow students. He surveyed the fiery ruins and the bodies scattered around him in a state of shock, expressing how he never wanted this outcome. He warned his peers who survived the temple's destruction that he did not want to fight them, and fled to join Snoke and the Knights of Ren.[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47) His turn to the dark side was marked by killing the Knights' leader and murdering Voe, a fellow Padawan.[[9]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_4-9)

When Solo turned away from the Jedi path, he no longer felt obliged to hold back his power. He embraced his conviction that he was more powerful than any of Skywalker's other apprentices, individually or collectively, and even Skywalker himself. As far as he was concerned, the notion that the others were his equal was a lie.[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47) Solo hated his full name; he felt as though everyone wanted him to be like his namesake he had never met, Obi-Wan "Ben" Kenobi, and that inheriting his father's invented surname represented how everything was a lie. Snoke told Solo to become his true self by adopting a new name, and encouraged him to take the name that Solo had invented as a child.[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25)

 [![Ren was known for losing control of his temper and the destructive outbursts that ensued.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/48/Kylo_loses_his_temper.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200201150214) [![Ren was known for losing control of his temper and the destructive outbursts that ensued.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/48/Kylo_loses_his_temper.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200201150214)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/48/Kylo_loses_his_temper.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200201150214) 

Ren was known for losing control of his temper and the destructive outbursts that ensued.

 

As Kylo Ren, he was known for expressing himself with his lightsaber, and did so often enough that nearby stormtroopers avoided the area he was currently destroying.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) He also used the Force to strangle, telekinetically throw, or kill subordinates who challenged him.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) He reveled in the fury of battle and killing his enemies.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) In addition to his temperament, Ren was known for his lack of patience,[[56]](#cite_note-Phasma-56) especially for those who failed him.[[64]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-64) While Ren was not born into the First Order, he was convinced that they were on the right side of history.[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39) Ren fought alongside his stormtroopers on the front lines of the battlefield. Although he would ignore the counsel of his advisors, favoring brute force over negotiation, he earned fear and respect through his ferocity as a warrior.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)[[63]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Kylo-63)

Having honed his fighting skills on the battlefield, Ren had little respect for his rival, General Hux, as a warrior.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) He regarded the general with disdain and saw Hux as neither brave nor trustworthy.[[62]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Hux-62) Ren embodied conflict,[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) having learned the arts of the Force through Jedi and Sith teachings.[[4]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_DB-4) He sought to bury his past as Ben Solo, yet channeled painful experiences and emotions from his youth to further his own power. He hoped to become immune to the light and avoid Darth Vader's sentimentality so he could succeed where Vader had failed.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50)

 [![Ren was the embodiment of the conflict between the dark side and the light.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/Take_that_ridiculous_thing_off.png/revision/latest?cb=20180106201918) [![Ren was the embodiment of the conflict between the dark side and the light.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/Take_that_ridiculous_thing_off.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20180106201918)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/Take_that_ridiculous_thing_off.png/revision/latest?cb=20180106201918) 

Ren was the embodiment of the conflict between the dark side and the light.

 

Despite Ren's willingness to extinguish the light within himself by any means necessary,[[1]](#cite_note-TSWB-1) his attempt to break his connection with the past and surrender entirely to the dark side by killing his father not only failed, but also marked him physically[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) and psychologically.[[4]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_DB-4) Murdering his father imbalanced his mind and led to his defeat by Rey, who marked his face with a scar that became a reminder of his failure. Snoke, having observed that Ren remained at war with himself, derided Han's murder as an act of petulance instead of strength.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

Ren accepted the idea that he was a monster with cold reservation[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) and believed the dark side was in his nature.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) His failed attempts to contact his grandfather through the Force caused him to believe that hope, which he equated to a false prophet, only led to severe disappointment. Ren did not believe in the existence of an afterlife until his mother and Rey saved him from certain death, causing him to reconsider his outlook on life and death.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10)

 [![Ren saw himself as a monster and believed that the dark side was in his nature.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/aa/Kylo_connecting_with_Rey.png/revision/latest?cb=20190519080841) [![Ren saw himself as a monster and believed that the dark side was in his nature.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/aa/Kylo_connecting_with_Rey.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190519080841)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/aa/Kylo_connecting_with_Rey.png/revision/latest?cb=20190519080841) 

Ren saw himself as a monster and believed that the dark side was in his nature.

 

Ren's desperation to prove himself as a worthy apprentice[[54]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_Bio_Gallery-54) was ultimately replaced by the desire to free himself from his Master, having spent much of his life as a student of Skywalker and Snoke in turn. He soon grew resentful of his status as Snoke's apprentice, believing he would always be kept subservient as long as his Master was alive. Ren felt liberated by Snoke's death because it granted him the power and independence he had long coveted. He had no intention of ever serving another master and was, therefore, fiercely protective of his new rank.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) Like Vader before him, Ren believed it was his destiny to rule over the weaker beings of the galaxy.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) He dreamed of conquering the galaxy with Rey at his side.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

If Ren had chosen his own title, it would have been "Master of the Dark Side" or "Commander of the Knights of Ren" rather than "Supreme Leader;" however, he considered the title right and just for himself as the head of the First Order. Embracing an authoritarian style of leadership, he believed that all people and their worlds must bend to his will. He was determined to show the First Order's true power to the galaxy and expected it to be met with gratitude. Ren enjoyed the simplicity of fascism. Wielding absolute power reminded him of his grandfather, Ren, like Vader, was a leader who expected total obedience from his followers[[99]](#cite_note-Follow_and_Lead-99) and punished those who failed him. Relic hunter Mika Grey once taunted Agent Raith with such knowledge, remarking that Ren would surely punish the First Order Raider if he returned without any artifacts to show for himself.[[93]](#cite_note-Relic_Raiders-93)

 [![Ren reveled in the power of his position as Supreme Leader, believing that the galaxy had to follow wherever he led.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/Kylo-stands-tall.png/revision/latest?cb=20250526114120) [![Ren reveled in the power of his position as Supreme Leader, believing that the galaxy had to follow wherever he led.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/Kylo-stands-tall.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250526114120)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f1/Kylo-stands-tall.png/revision/latest?cb=20250526114120) 

Ren reveled in the power of his position as Supreme Leader, believing that the galaxy had to follow wherever he led.

 

Ren had little tolerance for those who defied him to his face, especially after he became the Supreme Leader. Defiance against the First Order, which he considered the greatest regime in the galaxy, perplexed him. Ren did not understand why a person would reject a life of security under his rule, risking one's life just to show their contempt for the First Order. However, he was interested in understanding the views of those who opposed him, though he considered them "radicals" for doing so. Regardless of their reasons, he still intended to punish an entire world and its population if they resisted his authority. Ultimately, Ren believed that resistance was futile, and that it was his right to lead the galaxy as the Supreme Leader of the First Order.[[99]](#cite_note-Follow_and_Lead-99)

Ren was also distrustful of others; having isolated himself from his family and friends, the only people in Ren's life were subordinates and a master that he hated. Gaining the title of Supreme Leader only made Ren more suspicious of the individuals around him, particularly Hux,[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) but also Pryde and Darth Sidious. After the duel with Rey on Kef Bir, Ren questioned his beliefs and regretted the choices he made. His parents' love for him and Rey's compassion brought him back to the light, destroying the persona of Kylo Ren. Although he still carried feelings of guilt and self-doubt within him, he later recognized them as remnants of Snoke's conditioning that led Solo to become Kylo Ren. Having reconciled with his father in spirit, Solo hoped that one day he would come to forgive himself.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

 [![Renouncing the dark side destroyed the persona of Kylo Ren and restored that of Ben Solo.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/BenSoloRestored-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200327024359) [![Renouncing the dark side destroyed the persona of Kylo Ren and restored that of Ben Solo.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/BenSoloRestored-TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20200327024359)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/BenSoloRestored-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200327024359) 

Renouncing the dark side destroyed the persona of Kylo Ren and restored that of Ben Solo.

 

Solo's personality and his former persona as Ren were different in several ways, as observed by both himself and Rey. Unlike Ren, Solo neither derived pleasure from killing nor reveled in the fury of battle.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) He was relieved that the weapon he used to kill his father would never kill again after he discarded it.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) He confronted his enemies with a Jedi's focus instead of enjoyment or anger. Unlike Ren, who had shown mercy to no one,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Solo avoided prolonging his opponent's suffering by giving them the mercy of a quick death.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10)

Although he no longer counted himself among the ranks of the Knights of Ren, he still regarded them as his brothers-in-arms until their reunion on Exegol. Sensing their hatred for him,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Solo knew that they would no longer obey his orders as their true allegiance belonged to Darth Sidious.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) He felt betrayed, but resolved to fight them out of determination to help Rey.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Mirroring Darth Vader's death as Anakin Skywalker, Solo sacrificed his life out of love and died following this redemptive act.[[54]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_Bio_Gallery-54) He did not hesitate to do so,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) and he likened the experience to returning home.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10)

### Son of heroes

:   "*Kid's gonna get in trouble one day. Every kid does, but with the blood of a scoundrel and a princess in his veins, his defiance will shake the stars.*"
:   ―Lando Calrissian[[3]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-3)

 [![Ben Solo was loved by his parents, but their absence in his life fostered feelings of abandonment in him.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8e/Han_Leia_and_Ben.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161210085037) [![Ben Solo was loved by his parents, but their absence in his life fostered feelings of abandonment in him.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8e/Han_Leia_and_Ben.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161210085037)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8e/Han_Leia_and_Ben.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161210085037) 

Ben Solo was loved by his parents, but their absence in his life fostered feelings of abandonment in him.

 

Ben Solo meant everything to his parents, Han Solo and Leia Organa, and he was happy in his childhood.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) He grew to believe that his parents thought he was disturbed, having overheard their conversations about him and his lack of control over his innate Force abilities.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) His parents' busy professional lives and their decision to send him to be trained by his uncle left him feeling abandoned.[[38]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-38) He did not realize at the time that his fears about his family were influenced by Darth Sidious.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

Despite his feelings of neglect and abandonment, Ren did not hate his parents.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) During his trial on Dagobah, he could not bring himself to attack the vision of his parents, even as Snoke urged him to kill the source of his conflict.[[58]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Snoke-58) Although he was adamant that Han Solo meant nothing to him,[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) Ren struggled with uncertainty when his father confronted him.[[107]](#cite_note-Han_Solo_Bio_Gallery-107) His decision to kill Han was motivated by his desperation to escape his past[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) by freeing himself from his attachments. However, his connection to the dark side did not grow stronger after committing patricide. Instead, the act of killing his own father caused Ren to feel weaker,[[54]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_Bio_Gallery-54) affecting his very spirit and leaving him feeling more lost than ever.[[4]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_DB-4) When faced with the chance to kill his mother, Ren was surprised to sense her concern for him, having anticipated anger at the death of her husband. In the end, Ren could not bring himself to fire on her.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

As Leia Organa died, she reached out through the Force to send her hope and love to her son, calling him back to the light.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Listening to the voice of his father and seeing pride and joy in Han's eyes ultimately caused the last vestiges of the persona of Kylo Ren to fade from the mind of Ben Solo.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10)

### Nephew of a legend

:   "*At least he could have let me fly the ship. Would give me something to* do*. He's a great teacher, very strong. I've learned so much from him… But he never seems to want me to* use *any of it.*"
:   ―Ben Solo, on his apprenticeship under Luke Skywalker[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25)

 [![Solo idolized his uncle, Luke Skywalker, when he was a child.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/72/MyMasterIsALegend-TheRiseOfKyloRen2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200131031818) [![Solo idolized his uncle, Luke Skywalker, when he was a child.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/72/MyMasterIsALegend-TheRiseOfKyloRen2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20200131031818)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/72/MyMasterIsALegend-TheRiseOfKyloRen2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200131031818) 

Solo idolized his uncle, Luke Skywalker, when he was a child.

 

Ben Solo regarded his uncle and mentor, Luke Skywalker, with great esteem. Though he had misgivings about Skywalker's teaching methods, Solo saw his uncle as an amazing teacher and a legendary Jedi Master. He recognized his master's strength and knowledge with the Force, and learned much under Skywalker's tutelage. Despite the boredom that Solo tried to cope with on some of their missions together, he shared his uncle's enthusiasm for discovering ancient Jedi relics. In private, he lamented how Skywalker hoarded such treasures by storing them away in his temple, never to be used.[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25)

As a Skywalker and a Jedi-in-training, Solo felt as though he was being judged against his legendary uncle and, by extension, the Jedi Masters who trained him. While such comparisons motivated Solo to excel at his Jedi training, they also contributed to his insecurities. His ambition was to become more powerful and accomplished than the generations of Jedi who preceded him, including the "old guard" of Jedi Masters like Obi-Wan Kenobi and Yoda whose legacies influenced the Skywalker family for two generations. Having never known the Jedi who died before his birth, Solo likened his competition with deceased Jedi Masters to playing a game of [sabaac](/wiki/Sabacc "Sabacc") with "ghosts." Though jealous of his predecessors, Solo grew to respect the skills of the most legendary Jedi who were revered by his uncle. In contrast to his views of the old Jedi, Solo did not consider his fellow students as rivals.[[7]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-7)

 [![Convinced that his uncle tried to murder him, Solo gave into his anger and the power of the dark side.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/BenSoloNeedsVisine-TheRiseOfKyloRen1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210316061759) [![Convinced that his uncle tried to murder him, Solo gave into his anger and the power of the dark side.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/BenSoloNeedsVisine-TheRiseOfKyloRen1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210316061759)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/BenSoloNeedsVisine-TheRiseOfKyloRen1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210316061759) 

Convinced that his uncle tried to murder him, Solo gave into his anger and the power of the dark side.

 

Seeing his uncle standing over him with an ignited lightsaber had a profound impact on Solo's psyche. Solo saw this as a betrayal that confirmed his worst fears about his family.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) Overcome with anger and confusion, he believed his uncle would have murdered him in his sleep. The experience also left him disillusioned with the Jedi way, which Solo now viewed as a lie that his life had been wasted on.[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47)

In contrast to the enduring sentiment that he harbored for his mother and father,[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) Kylo Ren never forgave Skywalker[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) for what he believed was an intention to kill him in his sleep.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) Snoke tasked Ren with destroying any remnants of the Jedi, including his own uncle, whose attempt to restore the Jedi Order was thwarted when Ren betrayed him and the other Jedi students.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) Ren struck down a vision of Skywalker on Dagobah without hesitation or regret.[[58]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Snoke-58) When confronted by his uncle on Crait, Ren's hatred intensified,[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) and he overlooked inconsistencies in Skywalker's illusionary appearance while the Resistance fled.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5)

### Serving a dark master

:   "*I have never had a student with such promise. Before you.*"
:   ―Snoke, to Kylo Ren[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39)

 [![With Snoke as his master, Ren trained to rid himself of all traces of his former persona.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/TrainingOnDagobah-AORSnoke1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200217034214) [![With Snoke as his master, Ren trained to rid himself of all traces of his former persona.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/TrainingOnDagobah-AORSnoke1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200217034214)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/TrainingOnDagobah-AORSnoke1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200217034214) 

With Snoke as his master, Ren trained to rid himself of all traces of his former persona.

 

Ben Solo was drawn towards the dark side by Snoke beginning in his childhood.[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39) Through telepathic contact, Snoke acted as a confidant while sowing doubt.[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25) After destroying the Jedi temple, Solo sought out Snoke, whom he regarded as the only friend he had left. Snoke, in turn, used the situation to further discredit Skywalker in Solo's eyes, convincing the boy that his youth had been wasted learning the ways of the Jedi.[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47) Encouraged by Snoke, Solo sought the Knights of Ren,[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25) and became their leader when he killed their master and turned to the dark side.[[9]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_4-9)

Snoke promised Ren a future in which he was "heir to the Force" with no Jedi to oppose him.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) Ren's inner conflict grew as his Master encouraged him to use the heritage of both the light and the dark,[[106]](#cite_note-CEUE-106) honing Ren into a weapon of the First Order and the archetype of a new kind of dark side user that filled the void left behind when the Sith were destroyed during the Battle of Endor.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50)

 [![Disillusioned with his role as an apprentice, Ren sought to take control of his life by destroying his master.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Episode_VIII_Snoke_and_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20180727071207) [![Disillusioned with his role as an apprentice, Ren sought to take control of his life by destroying his master.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Episode_VIII_Snoke_and_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180727071207)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Episode_VIII_Snoke_and_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20180727071207) 

Disillusioned with his role as an apprentice, Ren sought to take control of his life by destroying his master.

 

After his defeat at Starkiller Base, Ren was furious and resentful[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) when his Master derided him as a failed apprentice[[54]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_Bio_Gallery-54) and "a child in a mask."[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) Snoke regarded Ren's imbalance after killing his father as proof that Ren was too weak and sentimental to be worthy of his grandfather's legacy.[[54]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_Bio_Gallery-54) Ren's pain caused him to explore the connection he and Rey shared and question his loyalty to Snoke. In addition, his father's warning that the Supreme Leader was only using him for his power echoed in his mind. Ren was plotting his future through uncertain times and, with dark side-fueled ambition, prioritized his survival and ultimate ascension.[[108]](#cite_note-CVD-108)

At first, Ren continued to think of Snoke as his esteemed mentor for guiding him on the path to the power of the dark side. However, the revelation of Darth Sidious' revival alarmed Ren as it fueled his suspicion that the Master he respected had been subservient to a greater power. Learning the truth about Snoke's origins shattered the respect that Ren held for the former Supreme Leader,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) but it also reinforced Ren's belief that he had made the right decision to seize power from his predecessor.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) Whereas Ren once regarded Snoke as the wise leader of the First Order,[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) he now saw his old Master as nothing more than an expendable "vat-grown organism."[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10)

### Heir of Darth Vader

:   "*Young Ben Solo possessed what all masters live to see: raw, untamed power. But a great conflict raged within the boy as well. Not only did his inner turmoil make him heir apparent to his grandfather, Lord Vader, it also made him the perfect pawn.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious[[36]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-36)

 [![Kylo Ren saw himself as the rightful heir to the legacy of his grandfather, Darth Vader.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/InTheShadowOfVader-SWTheDarkSide.png/revision/latest?cb=20220627042114) [![Kylo Ren saw himself as the rightful heir to the legacy of his grandfather, Darth Vader.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/InTheShadowOfVader-SWTheDarkSide.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/226?cb=20220627042114)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/InTheShadowOfVader-SWTheDarkSide.png/revision/latest?cb=20220627042114) 

Kylo Ren saw himself as the rightful heir to the legacy of his grandfather, Darth Vader.

 

Like his grandfather, Anakin Skywalker, Ben Solo felt the need to prove himself because of the great power that he was born with.[[1]](#cite_note-TSWB-1) As Kylo Ren he saw himself carrying on the tradition embodied by Darth Vader, the dark side version of his grandfather[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) and Ren's personal hero.[[109]](#cite_note-Splash_Screen_Fun_Fact_#2-109) However, Ren's understanding of Skywalker's history was twisted by Snoke.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) Ren, like Snoke, attributed the Galactic Empire's downfall not to ineffective strategy but to Vader's sentimentality for his son, Luke Skywalker. Ren considered it a foolish error in judgment and a momentary lapse in an otherwise great life. He believed that if Vader had not succumbed to the light, the Empire would have prevailed.[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39)

Ren idolized his grandfather—the darkness that was Vader, not the light of Skywalker.[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39) He would have given anything to meet Vader in person, but rejected the memory of Skywalker and believed that version of his grandfather to be nothing more than a coward and a traitor, not his true grandfather.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) Although Ren admired Vader, he remained torn by his conflict and was afraid of never attaining the strength his grandfather possessed.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) He kept a shrine to Vader in his personal chambers aboard the *Finalizer*, with the charred remains of the Sith Lord's helmet that had been recovered from his [funeral pyre](/wiki/Funeral_of_Anakin_Skywalker "Funeral of Anakin Skywalker") on Endor.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) Sitting atop a ceremonial plate that Ren covered with the ashes of fallen foes,[[110]](#cite_note-Helmet_Collection_21-110) the site was both a monument to the dark side's powers and its weakness.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) Ren's efforts to make contact with Vader were motivated by his desire to feel his grandfather was proud of him. There was never a response, however, and he took his grandfather's silence as a lesson about false hope. As a result, Ren came to believe that there was nothing after death.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10)

 [![Ren idolized his grandfather, whose helmet he kept as a reminder of the dark side's power and weakness.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/79/Kylo_Ren_Vader_Helmet_Chamber.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160420020932) [![Ren idolized his grandfather, whose helmet he kept as a reminder of the dark side's power and weakness.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/79/Kylo_Ren_Vader_Helmet_Chamber.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160420020932)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/79/Kylo_Ren_Vader_Helmet_Chamber.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160420020932) 

Ren idolized his grandfather, whose helmet he kept as a reminder of the dark side's power and weakness.

 

He chose to leave his grandfather's mask aboard the *Finalizer* before transferring to Snoke's flagship, the *Supremacy*, unable to face the charred helmet until he recovered from his loss against Rey.[[43]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-43) He still treated Vader's mask with reverence after his ascension as Supreme Leader, placing the Sith relic atop a pedestal made of Mustafarian [obsidian](/wiki/Obsidian "Obsidian"). During the final months of the war, the helmet was carefully preserved in a climate-controlled reliquary aboard the *Steadfast*; he went to great lengths to ensure the preservation of this artifact by storing it in a custom collector's case built by First Order technicians. As with Ren's quarters, the case was made for the purpose of preserving Vader's helmet, possessing temperature control systems. It also shielded its contents from radiation and sensor scans, its [obviribdum](/wiki/Obviribdum "Obviribdum") outer shell designed to be impervious to blaster fire at considerable expense. The entire box was [magnetically](/wiki/Magnet "Magnet") sealed and could only be opened by its built-in access keypad.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5)

Ultimately, the charred helm continued to serve as an instrument in Ren's meditations, despite his failed attempts to commune with the spirit of his ancestor who once wore it. It also served a symbolic purpose, representing the power embodied by Ren's grandfather, yet also "weakness and dependency" as Vader could not live outside of the mask.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5)

### A rival for power

:   "*Someone in your army tried to kill you. Clearly, you've managed to inspire a lot of loyalty, Hux.*"  
    "*Oh, please. I thought you could read minds, Ren. You honestly believe people hate* me *more than they hate* you*? With your petulant tantrums and your…*"  
    "*And my what?*"
:   ― Kylo Ren and Armitage Hux[[62]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Hux-62)

 [![Kylo Ren's rise to power brought him into conflict with General Armitage Hux.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a2/Armitage_Hux_and_Kylo_Ren-TFA.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200830053200) [![Kylo Ren's rise to power brought him into conflict with General Armitage Hux.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a2/Armitage_Hux_and_Kylo_Ren-TFA.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20200830053200)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a2/Armitage_Hux_and_Kylo_Ren-TFA.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200830053200) 

Kylo Ren's rise to power brought him into conflict with General Armitage Hux.

 

Despite Kylo Ren's status as the champion of the First Order,[[4]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_DB-4) his rise within the organization attracted the hostility of General Armitage Hux. A rivalry developed between the two as they both sought the approval of Supreme Leader Snoke.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) Whereas Hux resented the mystical aspects of the First Order embodied by his rival,[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) Ren considered the general untrustworthy and cowardly.[[62]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Hux-62) Ren, who prided himself on his fighting skills, was unimpressed by Hux as a soldier.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) His low opinion of Hux was such that he could not fathom why the Supreme Leader favored a general who wanted to usurp his throne.[[62]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Hux-62) Even as Ren held Hux in great contempt, he did share at least one commonality with the general: they preferred to keep their appearances and individual quarters simple.[[56]](#cite_note-Phasma-56)

As someone who was used to flattery throughout his life,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Ren was unaccustomed to directness, and when Hux confronted Ren about his insecurities about his heritage, the dark warrior came close to killing his adversary. Only the threat of Snoke's reprisal for killing his favorite officer prevented Ren from ending Hux's life. Shortly afterward, however, Ren made an effort to protect Hux when the two were attacked by a norwood, and was surprised to find that Hux had fled in the opposite direction, leaving Ren to fight the creature on his own. This incident reinforced Ren's views of Hux as a coward.[[62]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Hux-62)

 [![Ren was often tempted to kill Hux who he had disdained as a coward.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/13/StruckANerve-AORHux1.png/revision/latest?cb=20211126194315) [![Ren was often tempted to kill Hux who he had disdained as a coward.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/13/StruckANerve-AORHux1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20211126194315)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/13/StruckANerve-AORHux1.png/revision/latest?cb=20211126194315) 

Ren was often tempted to kill Hux who he had disdained as a coward.

 

The rivalry between Ren and Hux grew only stronger after Starkiller Base's destruction, with Ren increasingly irritated by Hux,[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) who enjoyed knowing that his rival needed to be rescued after his defeat at the hands of a scavenger.[[43]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-43) Hux's confidence increased as Ren fell out of favor with Snoke, to the extent that he began patronizing Ren during the attack on the Resistance fleet. Ren swore to make the general pay for speaking to him like a child.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

Their rivalry ended when Ren usurped his master's throne, killing Snoke to become the new Supreme Leader. Ren did not hesitate to put Hux in his place by way of the dark side, and threatened to asphyxiate the general until he recognized Ren's claim. The new Supreme Leader decided on keeping Hux alive but close by;[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) having never trusted the man whose ambitions were well known to Ren,[[62]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Hux-62) he was certain that Hux would betray him at the earliest opportunity.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

 [![As the new Supreme Leader, Ren took several opportunities to reduce Hux's status in the First Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4e/Hux_Databank_IX_TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200106052527) [![As the new Supreme Leader, Ren took several opportunities to reduce Hux's status in the First Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4e/Hux_Databank_IX_TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20200106052527)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4e/Hux_Databank_IX_TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200106052527) 

As the new Supreme Leader, Ren took several opportunities to reduce Hux's status in the First Order.

 

Ren would remain suspicious of Hux throughout his reign. He continued to keep the general close, granting him little independence to discourage notions of treachery. He also took steps to diminish Hux's influence, such as favoring Allegiant General Enric Pryde with greater authority.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) Although Ren saw his actions towards Hux as petty, he still enjoyed exerting power at the expense of his former rival. During the last days of their conflict with the Resistance, Ren all but ignored Hux despite forcing him to remain part of his entourage, which included Pryde.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

For all of the actions that Ren took to neutralize Hux as a threat to his power,[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) he never suspected that Hux was the informant who leaked classified information about the discovery on Exegol to the Resistance. When considering the possible identity of the spy in their ranks, Ren immediately dismissed Hux as a suspect. While his loyalty to Ren had always been in doubt, Ren never questioned Hux's allegiance to the First Order, and as such, he did not believe the general would do anything that could undermine the First Order's ability to win the war.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10)

### A dyad in the Force

:   "*You come from nothing. You're nothing. But not to me. Join me. Please.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren, to Rey[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

 [![Ren felt an innate connection to Rey from the moment he met her, unaware that they formed a dyad in the Force.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/db/KyloRenandRey-KyloDB.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200401153800) [![Ren felt an innate connection to Rey from the moment he met her, unaware that they formed a dyad in the Force.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/db/KyloRenandRey-KyloDB.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20200401153800)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/db/KyloRenandRey-KyloDB.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200401153800) 

Ren felt an innate connection to Rey from the moment he met her, unaware that they formed a dyad in the Force.

 

Ren was puzzled by the strange connection he felt with Rey during their first encounter. He was also astonished by her ability to read his mind while he probed hers, which allowed her to sense Ren's thoughts as well as his inner conflict and doubts.[[54]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_Bio_Gallery-54) To Ren's surprise, Rey evoked feelings of compassion within him, according to Snoke, who decried his apprentice's sentimentality as a form of weakness. Ren denied his Master's accusations, unable to comprehend how he could feel anything except hatred for an enemy of the First Order.[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39) Nevertheless, he offered to make Rey his apprentice after gauging her raw strength in the Force.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) Even though she defeated him, Ren had sensed that their destinies were somehow intertwined.[[54]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_Bio_Gallery-54) He plotted his own path to regain the power and status he lost to her blade. Rey's fate was inextricably tied to his own, and he was unable to deny their Force-bond.[[108]](#cite_note-CVD-108) Henceforth, Ren's churning emotions were as much about Rey as they were himself.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

A lifetime of conflict and loneliness caused Ren to find solace in his connection with Rey, and he developed an "insatiable" fascination with her.[[1]](#cite_note-TSWB-1) His emotional state became even more intense as their Force-bond grew stronger;[[54]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_Bio_Gallery-54) to Rey's surprise, Ren no longer bothered trying to hide his pain and misery from her.[[67]](#cite_note-Rey_Bio_Gallery-67) Despite lowering his mental barriers, Ren was still guarded with his feelings as Rey attempted to learn more about his fall to the dark side and specifically his actions in regard to Han Solo. While her inquisitive nature amused Ren, he would raise his guard by using deflection and derision to avoid Rey's questions about his conflict and his father. Ren treated Rey as though they were master and student, keeping her at bay and off balance by his questions. His facade, however, broke when Rey called him by the name he had been born with. In that moment, he looked lost.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

 [![Ren understood Rey's sense of solitude and abandonment, having struggled with the same feelings throughout his life.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/Force-bond.png/revision/latest?cb=20180417032028) [![Ren understood Rey's sense of solitude and abandonment, having struggled with the same feelings throughout his life.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/Force-bond.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20180417032028)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/Force-bond.png/revision/latest?cb=20180417032028) 

Ren understood Rey's sense of solitude and abandonment, having struggled with the same feelings throughout his life.

 

Ren understood Rey's feelings of solitude and abandonment; having experienced such emotions as well, he was all too familiar with the psychological effect they had on a person in the long term.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) He allowed Rey to confide in him and insisted that she was not alone. When Snoke ordered his apprentice to complete his training by killing Rey, Ren knew what he had to do.[[54]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_Bio_Gallery-54) In that moment, the oft-conflicted apprentice's fears and doubts gave way to a newfound sense of purpose and determination that surprised his own Master. He did not hesitate to kill the one he considered his true enemy, who turned out to be Snoke instead of Rey.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

Ren wanted Rey to join him,[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) as he had when they first dueled on Starkiller Base,[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) by forming a co-regency between themselves as rulers of the galaxy.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) Rey sensed that there was no threat in Ren's intentions toward her; he wanted Rey to overcome her past, and as such he told Rey that her parents were no one, believing that revelation would make her embrace the dark side as he did.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) Ren wanted Rey to be like him,[[73]](#cite_note-Resistance_Reborn-73) yet his brutal honesty gave way to a softer approach when he beseeched her to join him, telling Rey that while she was no one, she was still important to him.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

 [![Ren felt compassion for Rey, who cared about him as well.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/Rey_and_Ben_Solo.png/revision/latest?cb=20180711044728) [![Ren felt compassion for Rey, who cared about him as well.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/Rey_and_Ben_Solo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20180711044728)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/16/Rey_and_Ben_Solo.png/revision/latest?cb=20180711044728) 

Ren felt compassion for Rey, who cared about him as well.

 

Rey's refusal to join Ren left the dark warrior feeling betrayed. He wondered why Rey had not taken the opportunity to kill him while he was unconscious, and for a moment he contemplated the possibility that Rey actually cared for him. He pushed such thoughts aside, however, convinced that Rey's feelings made her foolish and sentimental, and would be the death of her.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) Ren vowed to destroy Rey along with everyone else who opposed him, but upon seeing her again through their bond,[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) he was left with a feeling of emptiness despite his recent accomplishments, which included his ascension as the new Supreme Leader.[[54]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_Bio_Gallery-54)

 [![Ren continued to pursue Rey, determined to prevent the apprentice from becoming a true Jedi.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/Dyad_in_the_Force.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200922194001) [![Ren continued to pursue Rey, determined to prevent the apprentice from becoming a true Jedi.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/Dyad_in_the_Force.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20200922194001)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/25/Dyad_in_the_Force.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200922194001) 

Ren continued to pursue Rey, determined to prevent the apprentice from becoming a true Jedi.

 

Despite his complete submission to the dark side of the Force,[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) Ren's conflict remained and he was still tempted by the light side. He had thought that his father's death would bring an end to the agony within, only to realize, in time, that Han Solo represented his past, whereas Rey personified what he felt as the pull to the light. Though he was bidden to kill the scavenger by the clone of Darth Sidious, Ren feigned compliance. The discovery of her full origins reignited his desire to turn her to the dark side, yet he was also conflicted over whether it was worth the risk, now that he knew his struggle against the light was directly tied to Rey. His uncertainty was compounded by feelings of anger and resentment over her rejection of his first offer, which confounded Ren.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

Ren sensed the terror that Rey felt whenever he was near her, and found it intoxicating, though her determination to resist him infuriated the Supreme Leader. The thought that she had dared to reject him fueled his rage, causing Ren to lose himself to his anger and hatred, forgetting for a moment about his plans to overthrow the Emperor and take control of the Star Destroyer fleet. Blinded by overwhelming rage and desperate to end his pain, he succumbed to the temptation of killing her. When the attempt failed, Ren chided himself for allowing Rey to use his anger against him, though he was even more stunned by the realization that he was relieved he had not killed her.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

 [![Ren's deepest desire was to rule the galaxy with Rey by his side.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/DyadofKyloRenandRey-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200624095615) [![Ren's deepest desire was to rule the galaxy with Rey by his side.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/DyadofKyloRenandRey-TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/260?cb=20200624095615)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/DyadofKyloRenandRey-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200624095615) 

Ren's deepest desire was to rule the galaxy with Rey by his side.

 

Snoke had trained Ren to channel the dark side by acting on his impulses, but now the impulse to kill Rey could not be reconciled with his deepest desire, for the thing he wanted most was Rey herself. He found the effort of tempting Rey difficult, yet worthwhile, and with each encounter between them, he felt increasingly closer to achieving his goal with her. Ren also came to understand that his plans for her required planning and patience, but he was well aware of his impatience and temper. As a result, he found inspiration in Rey's grandfather Sidious, wanting to be able to embrace a plan so long suffering and painstakingly careful, and being able to do it without feeling tempted by the light. Ren knew that he did not have the Emperor's patience, but in his desire to convert Rey, he was willing to learn it.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

Ren, whose mercurial nature inspired fear amongst his subordinates, maintained his composure around Rey. Her presence had a calming effect on him, although Rey found his calm irritating as she struggled to control her anger and frustration toward him. Following their confrontation on the *Steadfast*, Ren found himself enjoying the experience of seeing Rey in person again, taking little notice of the dead and the injured around him. For Ren, any loss was a small price to pay to be with Rey. He delighted in provoking her rage; he wanted her to know that they were a dyad in the Force; and he enjoyed seeing the look on her face, which he regarded as beautiful, when he finally told her.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

 [![Rey's compassion played a part in the return of Ben Solo, who stood with her as a true dyad against Darth Sidious.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/71/TheDyadVsTheEmperor-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250415052905) [![Rey's compassion played a part in the return of Ben Solo, who stood with her as a true dyad against Darth Sidious.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/71/TheDyadVsTheEmperor-TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250415052905)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/71/TheDyadVsTheEmperor-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250415052905) 

Rey's compassion played a part in the return of Ben Solo, who stood with her as a true dyad against Darth Sidious.

 

After discarding the persona of Ren, Solo developed a new sense of purpose, which was to protect Rey. The need that he felt to stand at her side determined his actions for the remainder of his life, including his decision to die for her. Solo's return to the light also had an effect on his connection to Rey, changing the way the bond felt between them. Unlike with Ren, when the two halves of the dyad fought on opposite sides of the Force, the connection with Solo felt right to Rey. The differences between the personalities of Solo and Ren, as well as the way they fought as one on the side of the light, convinced Rey that this was how the bond between them was always meant to be. By standing together against Sidious, Solo and Rey achieved their true potential as a dyad in the Force, making their combined strength an equivalent to the power of life.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

## Powers and abilities

### Lightsaber abilities

:   "*He really* was *the prize student.*"
:   ―Voe, on Ben Solo's overall ability as a Jedi[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47)

 [![Ren's extraordinary powers were complemented by his skills as a lightsaber swordmaster.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/68/KyloHachette.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210906220308) [![Ren's extraordinary powers were complemented by his skills as a lightsaber swordmaster.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/68/KyloHachette.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/190?cb=20210906220308)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/68/KyloHachette.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210906220308) 

Ren's extraordinary powers were complemented by his skills as a lightsaber swordmaster.

 

Out of the many apprentices his uncle trained, Ben Solo was the most talented and skilled with a lightsaber, although he was never able to surpass his uncle's skill in lightsaber combat.[[38]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-38) Kylo Ren, Solo's dark side persona, was a ruthless and efficient combatant on the battlefield,[[1]](#cite_note-TSWB-1) as well as master swordsman by the time of his apprenticeship to Snoke.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) Ren, who pulled from the teachings of the light and the dark to hone his power, possessed superb skills in lightsaber combat. The destruction of Skywalker's new generation of Jedi earned him the nickname of "Jedi Killer" amongst the First Order ranks, and his abilities with a lightsaber were what ultimately prevented the art of lightsaber combat from returning to prominence as he eliminated the remnants of the Jedi.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) In combat Ren typically utilized his lightsaber in the standard grip form, but he was also proficient in the unorthodox reverse grip.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

With his proficiency in the art of lightsaber combat, Ren could fight outnumbered and prevail against multiple adversaries. Back when he was still Ben Solo, he fought off three of his fellow students on Elphrona.[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13) He fought alongside Rey against the Elite Praetorian Guard until they were separated, forcing Ren to fight four guardsmen on his own. He killed two Praetorians with his crossguard lightsaber and, using a dead guard's [vibro-voulge](/wiki/Vibro-voulge "Vibro-voulge") as an improvised weapon in conjunction with his saber, demonstrated his ability in the art of [Jar'Kai](/wiki/Jar%27Kai "Jar'Kai") while defeating a third guard. Though he was outmaneuvered by the fourth and final Praetorian, Ren survived by stabbing the guardsman through the face with Rey's lightsaber.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) After reclaiming his identity as Ben Solo, although he was briefly outmatched by the Knights of Ren as he was outnumbered by his former subordinates, once armed with his grandfather's lightsaber, Solo[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) reminded them why he had been their master[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) and swiftly bested all six Knights on his own.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

 [![Ren's swordsmanship extended to the use of Jar'Kai.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/KyloRenElitePraetorianGuardJarKai-TLJ.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180505211236) [![Ren's swordsmanship extended to the use of Jar'Kai.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/KyloRenElitePraetorianGuardJarKai-TLJ.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180505211236)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/KyloRenElitePraetorianGuardJarKai-TLJ.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180505211236) 

Ren's swordsmanship extended to the use of Jar'Kai.

 

Ren's loss to Rey—a girl unfamiliar with the lightsaber—was an isolated case according to his master Snoke, who believed his apprentice lost because he was unbalanced by the murder of his father.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) Ren, however, held that he would have defeated Rey if not for the physical wound that he sustained from Chewbacca's bowcaster, preventing him from fighting at full strength.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) Despite her victory, Rey knew that Ren was strong with the dark side, and would only grow more powerful with time.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) Luke Skywalker even regarded his nephew Ren as a strong adversary who was far more powerful than Rey.[[111]](#cite_note-TLJ_Adaptation_4-111) During the battle against the Praetorian Guards, neither emotional conflict nor physical injuries hindered Ren's fighting ability. Rey observed Ren during the battle, and compared him to a caged beast as he unleashed his fury, engaging several elite guardsmen who were felled by the dark warrior despite holding a numerical advantage.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34)

 [![During their final duel, Ren unleashed a series of powerful lightsaber strikes that drove Rey to her knees.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7b/KyloRenvsReyDS2-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200405114454) [![During their final duel, Ren unleashed a series of powerful lightsaber strikes that drove Rey to her knees.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7b/KyloRenvsReyDS2-TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200405114454)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7b/KyloRenvsReyDS2-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200405114454) 

During their final duel, Ren unleashed a series of powerful lightsaber strikes that drove Rey to her knees.

 

Ren was highly accomplished in both an acrobatic and offensive form of lightsaber combat as well as the art of defense. As such, he was adept at evading close-quarter attacks while unarmed, sidestepping Rey's blade several times before activating his own lightsaber.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) He was also skilled in hand-to-hand combat, seamlessly incorporating martial arts strikes into his lightsaber sequence, which he utilized against Finn[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) and the Praetorian Guards.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) Even in his injured state, he deflected all but one of Finn's attacks that injured him in the shoulder,[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) and returned with his own fierce blows that overwhelmed Finn before disarming and severely injuring the stormtrooper.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) He maintained a fierce offense on Rey before she tapped into the Force to overwhelm him and managed to parry some of her blows afterward despite ultimately losing the duel.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

While Rey had improved her skills in lightsaber combat with a year's worth of training, she failed to break through Ren's guard in both of their later engagements. Ren found her attacks easy to dodge and block, even as her powers grew with her anger. During their final duel, it became clear to Rey that Ren was physically stronger than her. His ability to dodge and parry all of her attacks angered Rey, who grew increasingly frustrated by her failure to outfight Ren. After defending himself for a time, Ren seized the offensive with a series of swift and powerful strikes. The combination of his strength and skill ultimately overwhelmed Rey, causing Rey to lose her footing and to fall to her knees, completely exposed and defenseless. However, Ren was beckoned by his mother through the Force, sensed her death from afar, and dropped his lightsaber, leading Rey to capitalize on his distraction by usurping Ren's weapon and impaling him with it.[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29)

### Force powers

:   "*I've seen this raw strength only once before in Ben Solo. It didn't scare me enough then. It does now.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

 [![Like his grandfather, Ren was strong with the dark side of the Force and possessed great skill with telekinetic abilities.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/Force_Stop_SWD.png/revision/latest?cb=20171120071521) [![Like his grandfather, Ren was strong with the dark side of the Force and possessed great skill with telekinetic abilities.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/Force_Stop_SWD.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20171120071521)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/Force_Stop_SWD.png/revision/latest?cb=20171120071521) 

Like his grandfather, Ren was strong with the dark side of the Force and possessed great skill with telekinetic abilities.

 

The heir to the Skywalker bloodline,[[40]](#cite_note-Snoke_Bio_Gallery-40) Ben Solo was gifted with extraordinary strength in the Force,[[112]](#cite_note-The_Force_DB-112) though it was raw and untamed, a fact which did not go unnoticed by Luke Skywalker, Snoke,[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) or Darth Sidious.[[36]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-36) Skywalker recognized that his young nephew possessed Force powers that were already immense, and accepted Solo as his student.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) Snoke was intrigued by Solo's potential for limitless power, and conspired to bring that power into his service[[40]](#cite_note-Snoke_Bio_Gallery-40) at the expense of the resurgent Jedi Order.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) After surviving his confrontation with Skywalker, Solo believed that he had killed his Master, a feat which caused his confidence to grow and led him to seek Snoke's guidance.[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47)

After he became Kylo Ren, he wanted to be as powerful as Darth Vader, but was afraid he would not be as strong as the Sith Lord once was. Though not yet at the heights of his grandfather's[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) or his uncle's power,[[58]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Snoke-58) Ren's raw strength still gave him powerful abilities with the Force and in combat.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) Armitage Hux described Ren as a "one-man Starkiller;" by wielding the power of the dark side, Ren inspired fear across the galaxy not unlike the superweapon[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) that destroyed Hosnian Prime.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) Sidious credited himself with shaping Ren into a worthy apprentice, one that was just as powerful with the dark side of the Force as a true Sith.[[36]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-36)
