 [![Through the dark side, Ren gained greater power by focusing his rage.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1c/Focused_rage.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20211020174731) [![Through the dark side, Ren gained greater power by focusing his rage.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1c/Focused_rage.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20211020174731)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1c/Focused_rage.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20211020174731) 

Through the dark side, Ren gained greater power by focusing his rage.

 

The dark side that flowed through Ren made him a nearly unstoppable force, manifested in the potent [focused rage](/wiki/Focused_rage "Focused rage") that he drew from his inner conflict,[[113]](#cite_note-SWFA-113) and he was exceptionally skilled in telekinetic attacks and defenses[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) even before adopting the persona of Kylo Ren.[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47) When defending himself from Skywalker the night his Master came close to murdering him, Ben Solo was able to telekinetically collapse an entire hut on Skywalker without harming himself while they simultaneously clashed blades.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) Solo was capable of using his mind to control both objects and other people; in the wake of burning the temple, he used his telekinetic abilities to attack three Jedi apprentices, hurling numerous pieces of fiery debris in their direction.[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47) After he was tracked to Elphrona by the same students who confronted him at the temple, Solo telekinetically lifted both Tai and Voe, tossing them into the abandoned Jedi outpost. Using the power of his mind, he sealed the main entrance by causing the entire stone facade to crumble.[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13) He was able to create an explosion through the Force, causing the annihilation of the entire Cave of Evil, of which he managed to survive, unharmed.[[58]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Snoke-58)

He was also able to alter the weather by creating a lightning storm, what he did during the destruction of Luke's Jedi temple. His pupils constricted in his [red](/wiki/Color "Color")-clouded [eyes](/wiki/Eye "Eye") as matching red storm clouds appeared above the temple. Becoming aware of the clouds, he questioned their appearance just before they erupted with lightning. The storm he had created set fire to the dwellings and razed the temple, killing most of his fellow students.[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47)

Whether as Solo[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13) or Ren, his ability to effectively use the Force was dependent on his concentration and state of mind.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) Though he could still use his telekinetic powers under mental duress, he nonetheless experienced greater difficulty controlling the Force when his focus was interrupted. During the duel on Elphrona, Solo managed to catch Voe in the air after pushing her over a cliff. Unlike before, he struggled to maintain his hold on her through the Force. Hennix's interference broke Solo's concentration completely, causing him to lose his grip on Voe.[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13) On Starkiller Base, Ren found himself struggling to summon his grandfather's lightsaber to his hand, having sustained physical and emotional wounds in the wake of killing his own father.[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39)

 [![Ren had the power to immobilize his targets, using the Force to make their bodies respond to his commands rather than their own.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3b/A_Mysterious_Connection.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191229144018) [![Ren had the power to immobilize his targets, using the Force to make their bodies respond to his commands rather than their own.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3b/A_Mysterious_Connection.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191229144018)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3b/A_Mysterious_Connection.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191229144018) 

Ren had the power to immobilize his targets, using the Force to make their bodies respond to his commands rather than their own.

 

Ren used his telekinetic skills to [Force push](/wiki/Force_push "Force push") Rey, sending her flying against a tree. He also pulled Dopheld Mitaka by the neck to his hand, as well as to hold him up with one hand while still pulling them with the Force.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) Ren was proficient in the use of Force Stasis, enough to use such telekinetic halts in combat, which allowed him to freeze the motion of a target, immobilize and restrain people, hold a blaster bolt midair for over a minute,[[6]](#cite_note-TFA_head_to_head-6) and block a lightsaber blade with the Force.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) He was also able to manipulate the movements of living beings, which allowed him to force Rey to point her blaster at the ground as he simultaneously froze her in place.[[6]](#cite_note-TFA_head_to_head-6) By the time he arrived on Batuu, Ren's proficiency in telekinesis allowed him to crush a person's larynx—an ability used by his grandfather before him—as he demonstrated on a subordinate at the Black Spire Outpost.[[91]](#cite_note-Galaxy's_Edge-91)

 [![Ren could telekinetically control the actions of others regardless of the actual space between them and himself.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f2/DoYouUnderstand-TheEscape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200128073002) [![Ren could telekinetically control the actions of others regardless of the actual space between them and himself.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f2/DoYouUnderstand-TheEscape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200128073002)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f2/DoYouUnderstand-TheEscape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200128073002) 

Ren could telekinetically control the actions of others regardless of the actual space between them and himself.

 

By the time he ascended to the rank of Supreme Leader, Ren's telekinetic abilities allowed him to influence the actions of others across the galaxy. He demonstrated the range of his Force powers by controlling Agent Tierney and Commander Pyre while speaking to them through a hologram, forcing them to stand and aim their weapons at each other. When Tierny failed him again, Ren sent the agent another transmission and began choking her by way of the Force.[[101]](#cite_note-The_Escape-101)

Ren was also powerful in using the Force to strengthen his body, becoming sufficiently durable and resilient to having survived a long ranged blast from [Chewbacca's bowcaster](/wiki/Chewbacca%27s_bowcaster "Chewbacca's bowcaster") while only briefly doubling over in pain despite the severe injury even though the weapon could instantly kill armored stormtroopers on impact.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) His natural ability with the Force allowed him to contain the blast and minimize the damage it caused, thereby preventing the resultant wound from being fatal.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) He could also cut ahead of Rey and Finn in this state, demonstrating remarkable speed. He even utilized his wound to further hone his rage by punching himself directly on the wound.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) Additionally, Ren was capable of exerting enough strength to crush the Emperor's wayfinder with his bare hands and was able to [leap across great distances](/wiki/Force_jump "Force jump") to an even greater extent than Rey[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) and Voe.[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13)

 [![Ren interrogated his prisoners by invading their minds through the Force.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/01/RenMindprobesPoe-TGGH.png/revision/latest?cb=20220502033226) [![Ren interrogated his prisoners by invading their minds through the Force.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/01/RenMindprobesPoe-TGGH.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220502033226)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/01/RenMindprobesPoe-TGGH.png/revision/latest?cb=20220502033226) 

Ren interrogated his prisoners by invading their minds through the Force.

 

Ren excelled in interrogation, as he could [telepathically](/wiki/Telepathy "Telepathy") invade the minds of his prisoners and psychologically torture them into revealing withheld information. His abilities also allowed him to render opponents unconscious without harming them, as he did to Rey on Takodana, causing her to fall asleep with a wave of his hand so he could capture her without resistance.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) Although Snoke was capable of probing his apprentice's mind, Ren was able to deceive his Master into believing that he intended to kill Rey when his actual target was Snoke himself.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) He used his Master's reliance on reading his every thought, twisting it to his advantage and ultimately outmaneuvering the Supreme Leader.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5)

Snoke considered Ren and Rey equals in the Force[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) after realizing that their bond was uniquely powerful, making them a dyad in the Force.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) After Snoke's demise, both sides of the dyad exerted equal control over the Skywalker lightsaber, which caused the weapon to break into two separate pieces.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) However, Ren ultimately proved stronger with the Force during their tug-of-war over a transport on Pasaana, in spite of all of Rey's exertion to stop the vessel from being pulled away from her.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10)

### Other abilities

:   "*He took out our main engines. One shot. If he was even the* tiniest *bit off, we'd be hot vapor right now.*"
:   ―Voe, on Ben Solo's piloting skills[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47)

 [![Hailing from a family of expert pilots, Ren inherited the flying skills of his father and maternal grandfather.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f4/Predictive_Shot_SWZ.png/revision/latest?cb=20190618000702) [![Hailing from a family of expert pilots, Ren inherited the flying skills of his father and maternal grandfather.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f4/Predictive_Shot_SWZ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190618000702)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f4/Predictive_Shot_SWZ.png/revision/latest?cb=20190618000702) 

Hailing from a family of expert pilots, Ren inherited the flying skills of his father and maternal grandfather.

 

Ben Solo's inherent Force ability came from his mother, whereas he gained his amazing reflexes and piloting skills from his father Han Solo.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) He was an excellent pilot[[114]](#cite_note-TIE_silencer_DB-114)—both as Ben Solo[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47) and Kylo Ren[[114]](#cite_note-TIE_silencer_DB-114)—hailing from a bloodline of expert pilots that included not only his father, but also his grandfather Anakin Skywalker.[[115]](#cite_note-TLJ:ICS-115)

After he destroyed Skywalker's temple, Solo fled from the scene in his starship, the *Grimtaash*. Pursued by his fellow Jedi students, Solo made an attack run on their vessel, the *Verity*. Knowing that Solo's father and uncle were both accomplished pilots in their own right, Tai was convinced that Voe's attempt at evasive action would fail. Indeed, they did not succeed in evading Solo. With one shot, he rendered the *Verity*'s main engine inoperable. Taking note of Solo's accuracy, Voe mentioned that the slightest imprecision would have destroyed the *Verity*, yet Solo had only disabled the ship instead of destroying it outright.[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47)

Kylo Ren exercised little restraint against his enemies until faced with the decision on whether to fire on his mother.[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) Utilizing his personal fighter, Ren led the First Order's initial attack on the Resistance fleet. He was able to evade the *Raddus*' defenses and destroy the vessel's starfighter hangar,[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) owing to his own talents as a pilot.[[114]](#cite_note-TIE_silencer_DB-114) Ren was never satisfied with the speed and responsiveness of his craft and pushed the First Order engineers to outdo their best efforts. He modified his TIE whisper's astrogational systems to accept Darth Vader's wayfinder as a signal source, and the ancient device sent out binary signals that the ship's hyperdrive interpreted as jump coordinates.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) Having important members of the Rebellion as family members, Ren learned the tactics of rebellion as he grew up, which made him a skilled strategist. He used this knowledge to guide the people of [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo") with great skill against the First Order invasion, which he himself caused.[[78]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_5-78)

## Equipment

### Weapons

#### Ben Solo/Kylo Ren's lightsaber

:   "*He was dressed in black, carried a '*laser sword*' like in the old Jedi stories.*"
:   ―Eila, on Kylo Ren[[60]](#cite_note-The_Children_from_Tehar-60)

 [![Ben Solo's Jedi lightsaber produced a blue plasma blade.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b0/BenSoloLightsaber2-SWTLC.png/revision/latest?cb=20200930223831) [![Ben Solo's Jedi lightsaber produced a blue plasma blade.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b0/BenSoloLightsaber2-SWTLC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200930223831)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b0/BenSoloLightsaber2-SWTLC.png/revision/latest?cb=20200930223831) 

Ben Solo's Jedi lightsaber produced a blue plasma blade.

 

As was the tradition of the Jedi Order,[[116]](#cite_note-A_Test_of_Strength-116) Ben Solo constructed his lightsaber at some point between 15 ABY and around 19 ABY[[117]](#cite_note-Creation_date-117) while being trained as a Jedi Padawan under his uncle, and Jedi Master, Luke Skywalker.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) His innate strength in the Force and natural talent meant he excelled over his peers in skill with the lightsaber.[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13)

 [![Kylo Ren's lightsaber was an ancient design that recalled weapons used in the Great Scourge of Malachor.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/Kylo_Ren_confronts_Rey_and_Finn.png/revision/latest?cb=20160122052345) [![Kylo Ren's lightsaber was an ancient design that recalled weapons used in the Great Scourge of Malachor.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/Kylo_Ren_confronts_Rey_and_Finn.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160122052345)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/Kylo_Ren_confronts_Rey_and_Finn.png/revision/latest?cb=20160122052345) 

Kylo Ren's lightsaber was an ancient design that recalled weapons used in the Great Scourge of Malachor.

 

Kylo Ren repurposed the kyber crystal and lightsaber hilt formerly used as Ben Solo to create his new[[9]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_4-9) [Sith lightsaber](/wiki/Sith_lightsaber "Sith lightsaber").[[4]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_DB-4) First, he used the dark side to bleed the crystal; it cracked in its master's grip with a surge of fiery energy. Its hue was thus changed[[9]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_4-9) to red-yellow.[[118]](#cite_note-SWL:AGtWotF-118) In order to channel dangerous amounts of power through this broken crystal,[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) he added vents on either side to divert the excess heat and produce quillon blades.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50)

The crude design was an ancient one, dating back thousands of years[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) to a [battle](/wiki/Great_Scourge_of_Malachor "Great Scourge of Malachor") between the Jedi and Sith on the planet [Malachor](/wiki/Malachor "Malachor").[[119]](#cite_note-Twilight_of_the_Apprentice-119) Even with these adaptations, the kyber crystal within could barely contain the weapon's power, and the broken crystal gave the red blade an unstable and fiery, flickering appearance. While its crude appearance suggested construction by an inexperienced hand,[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50) Ren preferred his lightsaber's volatile nature and chose to not repair it.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) Its partially exposed inner workings allowed for easy modifications and upkeep.[[43]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-43)

#### The Skywalker lightsaber

:   "*That lightsaber. It belongs to me.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8)

 [![During the Battle of Exegol, Ben Solo wielded the lightsaber that once belonged to his grandfather, Anakin Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0a/Death_of_Trudgen.png/revision/latest?cb=20210915004530) [![During the Battle of Exegol, Ben Solo wielded the lightsaber that once belonged to his grandfather, Anakin Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0a/Death_of_Trudgen.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210915004530)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0a/Death_of_Trudgen.png/revision/latest?cb=20210915004530) 

During the Battle of Exegol, Ben Solo wielded the lightsaber that once belonged to his grandfather, Anakin Skywalker.

 

The Skywalker lightsaber was a Jedi weapon constructed by Ben Solo's grandfather, Anakin Skywalker, in the early days of the Clone Wars.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5) An admirer of Darth Vader, Kylo Ren despised the lightsaber that once belonged to Vader's former self, a Jedi Knight, as well as Ren's uncle, Luke Skywalker.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) Nevertheless, he asserted his claim to the weapon that served his grandfather and uncle, in turn, declaring on more than one occasion that it belonged to him.[[39]](#cite_note-TFA_novel-39)[[34]](#cite_note-TLJ_EE-34) Ultimately, however, Ren sought to destroy the Skywalker lightsaber that represented the family heritage he rejected.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10)

His desire for its destruction ended when Ren renounced the dark side of the Force, becoming Ben Solo once more. During the Battle of Exegol, the blade passed from Rey to Solo by way of their bond as a Force dyad,[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10) restoring the Skywalker lightsaber to the possession of a Skywalker.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) Solo claimed his family's lightsaber as his own, knowing that it belonged to him the moment he felt it in his hand. He relished the feel of the lightsaber as it became an extension of his own being,[[29]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-29) although he experienced neither anger nor pleasure while using it in battle. He wielded it only with the discipline of a trained Jedi.[[10]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-10)

#### Blasters

 [![Ben Solo's DL-44](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/67/BenSolosDL44-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.png/revision/latest?cb=20250306233059) [![Ben Solo's DL-44](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/67/BenSolosDL44-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20250306233059)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/67/BenSolosDL44-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.png/revision/latest?cb=20250306233059) 

Ben Solo's DL-44

 

When he first joined the Knights of Ren, Ben Solo was given a [DL-44 heavy blaster pistol](/wiki/DL-44_heavy_blaster_pistol "DL-44 heavy blaster pistol") similar to his [father's](/wiki/Han%27s_heavy_blaster_pistol "Han's heavy blaster pistol") in a [holster](/wiki/Holster "Holster") on the side of his leg, but he eventually discarded it.[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13) When he returned to the light side and decided to help Rey on Exegol, Solo utilized another [blaster pistol](/wiki/Blaster_pistol "Blaster pistol") of an unidentified model. He later was disarmed of this weapon when he was surrounded and overwhelmed in combat by the Knights of Ren, before Rey gave him the Skywalker lightsaber through their bond.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12)

### Vehicles

:   "*Prepare my ship.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37)

As a Jedi Padawan, Ben Solo possessed a starship named the *Grimtaash*.[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47)
As Kylo Ren, he flew in a [*Upsilon*-class command shuttle](/wiki/Upsilon-class_command_shuttle "Upsilon-class command shuttle") which was present during the [subjugation of Tuanul](/wiki/Attack_on_Tuanul "Attack on Tuanul") and the [Battle of Takodana](/wiki/Battle_of_Takodana "Battle of Takodana"), where it landed at the remains of [Takodana Castle](/wiki/Takodana_Castle "Takodana Castle").[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-8) At the time of the Battle of Crait, Kylo Ren flew his personal TIE silencer, a [TIE/vn space superiority fighter](/wiki/TIE/vn_space_superiority_fighter "TIE/vn space superiority fighter").[[115]](#cite_note-TLJ:ICS-115) When he sought the location of Exegol, he used his customized TIE whisper, a [TIE/wi modified interceptor](/wiki/TIE/wi_modified_interceptor "TIE/wi modified interceptor").[[120]](#cite_note-TIE_whisper-120)

### Outfits

:   "*Vader wore his mask because he couldn't breathe without it. But you…you just dress-up to hide the faces of your rebel scum parents—*"
:   ―Armitage Hux, to Kylo Ren[[62]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Hux-62)

 [![Ren wore a mask to hide his former identity and project a more intimidating persona.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/KyloRen-SWBC4cvr.png/revision/latest?cb=20231229032418) [![Ren wore a mask to hide his former identity and project a more intimidating persona.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/KyloRen-SWBC4cvr.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20231229032418)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/KyloRen-SWBC4cvr.png/revision/latest?cb=20231229032418) 

Ren wore a mask to hide his former identity and project a more intimidating persona.

 

Kylo Ren often kept his face covered with his mask which was modeled on the battle gear of the Knights of Ren. [His mask](/wiki/Kylo_Ren%27s_helmet "Kylo Ren's helmet") projected and amplified his voice in a deeper way. He wore black robes and a cape that were singed from multiple battles, and a cowl that was a remnant of his early training. The combination of these elements made Ren an intimidating presence, particularly on the battlefield where he exuded confidence in his powers and his purpose.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50)

However, Ren had deeply rooted insecurities that he attempted to conceal by wearing his mask and acting like Vader.[[58]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Snoke-58) Additionally, he sought to hide his face as it reminded him of his former self[[64]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-64) as well as his mother and father.[[62]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Hux-62)

After usurping the title of Supreme Leader, Ren had his helmet reforged by a [Sith alchemist](/wiki/Sith_alchemist "Sith alchemist"). He considered it a mark of his role in the Knights of Ren, and a symbol of his own identity being broken and rebuilt.[[5]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-5)

## Behind the scenes

### Creation and development

:   "*I've written four* Star Wars *movies now, and there's never been a character quite like the one that Adam [Driver] plays. I think you're going to see something that's brand new to the saga… He's full of emotion. No matter how we express ourselves in the world, whether we hide it and act very calm or whether we're very out there and demonstrative, everybody's roiling with emotion. And you want your characters to be that way, too. Then they have to deal with their emotions as best they can, with what they are.*"
:   ―*The Force Awakens* co-writer Lawrence Kasdan, on Kylo Ren[[121]](#cite_note-EW_Kylo_Ren-121)

 [![Several unused helmet designs were considered for the "Jedi Killer," the character who became Kylo Ren.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a8/Kylo_Ren_Helmet.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160414173517) [![Several unused helmet designs were considered for the "Jedi Killer," the character who became Kylo Ren.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a8/Kylo_Ren_Helmet.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/242?cb=20160414173517)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a8/Kylo_Ren_Helmet.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160414173517) 

Several unused helmet designs were considered for the "Jedi Killer," the character who became Kylo Ren.

 

On [October 30](/wiki/October_30 "October 30"), [2012](/wiki/2012 "2012"), [The Walt Disney Company](/wiki/The_Walt_Disney_Company "The Walt Disney Company") purchased [Lucasfilm](/wiki/Lucasfilm "Lucasfilm") from [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas"), the creator of *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")*, and announced that they would be making the long-awaited *Star Wars* [sequel trilogy](/wiki/Sequel_trilogy "Sequel trilogy"), beginning with [*Star Wars*: Episode VII](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VII_The_Force_Awakens "Star Wars: Episode VII The Force Awakens") in [2015](/wiki/2015 "2015"). In the months prior, as Lucasfilm co-chair (and eventual president) [Kathleen Kennedy](/wiki/Kathleen_Kennedy "Kathleen Kennedy") began the work to produce the new slate of films, it became clear to the creative team that the story could not just rely on characters from the previous films but would have to introduce new characters to carry the franchise forward.[[122]](#cite_note-Art_of_TFA-122)

Since George Lucas' earliest versions of the film's story, a son of Han Solo and Leia Organa struggling with the dark side of the Force was always in the mix. In some of these versions, the son's name was "Skyler" and he was corrupted to the dark side by [Darth Talon](/wiki/Darth_Talon "Darth Talon"), a character originally created for the [Dark Horse Comics](/wiki/Dark_Horse_Comics "Dark Horse Comics")' *[Star Wars: Legacy](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Legacy "Star Wars: Legacy")* [comic book](/wiki/Star_Wars_comic_books "Star Wars comic books") series set over a century after the films.[[123]](#cite_note-George's_Original_Plans-123) Talon's role was then morphed into that of the "Jedi Killer," the initial name of the character who evolved into Kylo Ren, which was used throughout the film's pre-production before the director and co-writer [J.J. Abrams](/wiki/J.J._Abrams "J.J. Abrams") and his team settled on a name for the character. The character's design went through a number of iterations before the final design was approved on [March 11](/wiki/March_11 "March 11"), [2014](/wiki/2014 "2014"). One design made him look similar to Darth Vader. According to concept artist [Christian Alzmann](/wiki/Christian_Alzmann "Christian Alzmann"), the idea behind the similarity was that Darth Vader, as a Lord of the Sith, was not a "one-off" look. Instead, "he has a specific title and a specific look that goes with that title. Even though the mask was helping him breathe, there was still a certain look to it." Concept artist [Glyn Dillon](/wiki/Glyn_Dillon "Glyn Dillon"), who designed the final look of the character, said that the design of the Jedi Killer was like "trying to land a helicopter on a penny. We couldn't be too Vader-ish, but we couldn't reference something else too heavily, either."[[122]](#cite_note-Art_of_TFA-122)

 [![Kylo Ren's "Jedi Killer" concept art inspired the design of the Guavian security soldiers.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/Kylo_Ren_concept_art_Guavian.png/revision/latest?cb=20160321131812) [![Kylo Ren's "Jedi Killer" concept art inspired the design of the Guavian security soldiers.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/Kylo_Ren_concept_art_Guavian.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/229?cb=20160321131812)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/Kylo_Ren_concept_art_Guavian.png/revision/latest?cb=20160321131812) 

Kylo Ren's "Jedi Killer" concept art inspired the design of the Guavian security soldiers.

 

Additional design concepts showed the Jedi Killer as someone who ate matter from stars. He would be in a meditation chamber, where energies from a sun could come into the room and he would consume whatever power was within it. Another piece of art showed him with a more robotic look, holding the mask of Darth Vader; at one point, the mask of Darth Vader was a central element to the film, before becoming part of the shrine that Kylo Ren had in the final story. One rejected piece of concept art showed the Jedi Killer with a red and black mask with a circular pattern in the center. This design later inspired the appearance of the [Guavian security soldiers](/wiki/Guavian_security_soldier "Guavian security soldier"), the cybernetically enhanced security soldiers of the [Guavian Death Gang](/wiki/Guavian_Death_Gang "Guavian Death Gang").[[122]](#cite_note-Art_of_TFA-122)

Other designs the crew worked on included a fortress for the Jedi Killer. Concept artist [Doug Chiang](/wiki/Doug_Chiang "Doug Chiang") took "iconic shapes that we know from *Star Wars*" but put "different material on them—in this case turning them into concrete instead of that slick painted metal." The crew also considered giving the Jedi Killer his own droid, such as a torture droid or something else that looked ominous.[[122]](#cite_note-Art_of_TFA-122) The idea of the Jedi Killer having an interrogation droid ultimately made it into the film, with Kylo Ren using interrogation droids and other torture techniques to break his prisoners.[[50]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-50)

The final design was meant to be memorable, much like Darth Vader's mask—upon which Ren's look was intentionally based. Costumer designer [Michael Kaplan](/wiki/Michael_Kaplan "Michael Kaplan") said that Abrams wanted the look to be memorable for kids, and that Abrams loved the final design when it was presented. In developing the character, original screenwriter [Michael Arndt](/wiki/Michael_Arndt "Michael Arndt"), whose screenwriting duties were taken over by Abrams and co-writer [Lawrence Kasdan](/wiki/Lawrence_Kasdan "Lawrence Kasdan") when Arndt departed the project, said the character's backstory came about because the writers needed a rationale for the heroes of the [original trilogy](/wiki/Original_trilogy "Original trilogy") to have separated after the events of the [1983](/wiki/1983 "1983") film [*Star Wars*: Episode VI *Return of the Jedi*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VI_Return_of_the_Jedi "Star Wars: Episode VI Return of the Jedi"). Abrams wanted Episode VII, which came to be named *The Force Awakens*, to tap into parental fears of a child gone wrong through Kylo Ren.[[124]](#cite_note-EW_Kylo_Shock-124) He also wanted the film to tell the story of someone who was still becoming a villain, saying that the only reason Ren had "any hope of being a worthy successor" to the iconic Darth Vader was because he kills Han Solo. "There's nothing I could think of that is more hideous than patricide," Abrams said, "especially when it comes to Han Solo."[[125]](#cite_note-Abrams_on_Kylo-125) At [Rian Johnson](/wiki/Rian_Johnson "Rian Johnson")'s request, the position of the character's facial scar was moved slightly for *The Last Jedi*.[[126]](#cite_note-Rian_tweet-126)

Ren's parentage was initially to have been revealed earlier in *The Force Awakens*, when Ren speaks to Darth Vader's helmet. Ren calling Vader his grandfather would have been the reveal, and the scene was written to take place shortly after Finn and Dameron escaped from the *Finalizer*. Ren would have blamed himself for not having done anything about Finn's change of heart regarding the First Order, and he would have sought the counsel of his grandfather for guidance. Eventually, the film's editors, [Mary Jo Markey](/wiki/Mary_Jo_Markey "Mary Jo Markey") and [Maryann Brandon](/wiki/Maryann_Brandon "Maryann Brandon"), felt that the revelation came too early and it was a waste of a good moment. Instead of its original placement, they moved the scene later in the film to foreshadow Han Solo's death.[[127]](#cite_note-Vader_Scene_Edit-127) The moment when Ren first removes and places his mask on a table of ashes was originally filmed for the scene when he spoke to Vader's helmet; it was reshot with his mask on, but they wanted to keep that shot and moved it to his interrogation of Rey. Abrams described the table's contents as ashes of the enemies that Ren killed.[[128]](#cite_note-JJ_Abrams_Kylo_Ren_Ashes-128) This fact was later mentioned in the [twenty-first](/wiki/Star_Wars_Helmet_Collection_21 "Star Wars Helmet Collection 21") issue of [*Star Wars* Helmet Collection](/wiki/Star_Wars_Helmet_Collection "Star Wars Helmet Collection").[[110]](#cite_note-Helmet_Collection_21-110)

For the film's [soundtrack](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens_(soundtrack) "Star Wars: The Force Awakens (soundtrack)"), composer [John Williams](/wiki/John_Williams "John Williams") wrote a theme for Kylo Ren that first appears in the track "[Main Title and The Attack on the Jakku Village](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens_(soundtrack) "Star Wars: The Force Awakens (soundtrack)")." It is reprised throughout the film, including in "Kylo Ren Arrives at the Battle."[[129]](#cite_note-Soundtrack-129) In composing the theme, Williams approached it as an extension of Darth Vader and "[The Imperial March](/wiki/The_Imperial_March "The Imperial March")," without it being too similar. He wanted the theme to convey Ren's great and evil power and strength, as well as the threat he posed. These elements came together to create a theme that could be instantly accessible to the audience.[[130]](#cite_note-Sound_of_a_Galaxy-130)

### Casting and portrayal

:   "*When they think of their actions as morally justified, it makes them dangerous and unpredictable. There's no level they won't go to to accomplish what they're after. I never thought of the character as an evil person.*"
:   ―Adam Driver on Kylo Ren[[131]](#cite_note-Empire_Kylo-131)

 [![Kylo Ren is played by Adam Driver, whom J.J. Abrams said brings a "wonderful ferocity" to the role.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/AdamDriver-IMDB.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180430012723) [![Kylo Ren is played by Adam Driver, whom J.J. Abrams said brings a "wonderful ferocity" to the role.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/AdamDriver-IMDB.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/237?cb=20180430012723)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/AdamDriver-IMDB.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180430012723) 

Kylo Ren is played by Adam Driver, whom J.J. Abrams said brings a "wonderful ferocity" to the role.

 

Kylo Ren was portrayed by [Adam Driver](/wiki/Adam_Driver "Adam Driver") in *The Force Awakens*, a role he reprised in the [2017](/wiki/2017 "2017") sequel [*Star Wars*: Episode VIII *The Last Jedi*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VIII_The_Last_Jedi "Star Wars: Episode VIII The Last Jedi")[[132]](#cite_note-VIII_Filming-132) and the [2019](/wiki/2019 "2019") finale to the sequel trilogy, [*Star Wars*: Episode IX *The Rise of Skywalker*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IX_The_Rise_of_Skywalker "Star Wars: Episode IX The Rise of Skywalker").[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) Abrams originally saw other actors for the role, including [Eddie Redmayne](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eddie_Redmayne "wikipedia:Eddie Redmayne"), who had been cast in other films by casting director [Nina Gold](/wiki/Nina_Gold "Nina Gold"), but all of them lost out to Driver.[[133]](#cite_note-Kylo_Redmayne-133) Driver didn't need to audition for the role, however, and instead had a meet and greet with Abrams where the director wanted to get a look at the actor. Just as Abrams had to consider whether to cast Driver, the actor had to decide whether he wanted to take the part.[[134]](#cite_note-Howard_Stern-134) Abrams described Driver has having a "wonderful ferocity that was perfect for this character."[[135]](#cite_note-EW_Abrams_Driver-135)

Driver does not see Ren as a villain, a stance he took in order to get into the head of the character and portray him as well as possible. Rather, Driver sees him as a religious fanatic who sees his actions as morally justified. This makes Ren more dangerous and unpredictable for the actor, as there is no level that Ren will not go to in order to accomplish his objectives.[[131]](#cite_note-Empire_Kylo-131) Getting into Ren's head was one part of Driver's method-acting approach. On set, Driver often stayed in character, keeping his helmet on to do so. Co-star [John Boyega](/wiki/John_Boyega "John Boyega"), who plays Finn, recalled that acting with Driver was intense because Driver wanted to forget he was in *Star Wars* and take the role as seriously as any other role he had ever played.[[136]](#cite_note-Driver_Method-136) The process of getting into Ren's costume provided an extra motivation for the actor; Driver said that by the time he was in the costume and ready to shoot, the "cumbersome and difficult" process left him feeling "so pissed by the time we were ready to start shooting that I felt totally ready."[[137]](#cite_note-Secrets_SXSW-137)

In previous roles, Driver did not watch his performance because he preferred to not see himself on screen. He comes from a theater background, where actors never saw their own performances, and always hated noticing mistakes that he could not correct. He made an exception for *The Force Awakens*, however, and watched the film in a private screening with just his co-stars [Daisy Ridley](/wiki/Daisy_Ridley "Daisy Ridley") and [Carrie Fisher](/wiki/Carrie_Fisher "Carrie Fisher"), who played Rey and Leia Organa respectively. He felt comfortable sitting through the film and watching it with them because of how much time and effort he and his co-stars put into the film.[[134]](#cite_note-Howard_Stern-134)

### *The Last Jedi* and *The Rise of Skywalker*

It is requested that this article section [be expanded](/wiki/Special:EditPage/:Ben_Solo "Special:EditPage/:Ben Solo"). *Please improve it in any way that you see fit, and remove this notice once the article section is more complete.*

Rian Johnson, writer-director of *Star Wars*: Episode VIII *The Last Jedi*, stated that he felt the most interesting option for Kylo Ren would be to take out the character's shaky foundation at the start of the film. Johnson stated that, by the end of *The Last Jedi*, Ren is no longer a Darth Vader copy, and he is now his own complex villain taking control. He also felt it was good setup for the ninth film in the [Skywalker saga](/wiki/Star_Wars_saga "Star Wars saga"),[[138]](#cite_note-Johnson_discusses_Snoke-138) which was eventually titled *Star Wars*: Episode IX *The Rise of Skywalker* and firected by Abrams. *The Rise of Skywalker* ends with Ben Solo returning to the light side of the Force, forsaking the name "Kylo Ren" and fighting as a Jedi until his sacrifice to save Rey.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-12) However, according to Driver, the original "overall arc" for Ren—which he states was supported by Abrams—was to have him end without being redeemed as an intentional inversion of Darth Vader's arc. Whereas Vader began the [original trilogy](/wiki/Original_trilogy "Original trilogy") committed to the dark side and ended it, in Driver's words, "vulnerable and weak," Ren was supposed to begin the sequel trilogy in that state of confusion and then end it more committed to the dark side than ever. However, Driver stated that this plan changed while shooting. Nonetheless, he claimed he kept his mind focused on that plan regardless of what was filmed.[[139]](#cite_note-Variety_Adam-139)

In [2024](/wiki/2024 "2024"), Driver stated that, as Solo is dead, he has no intentions of returning to the *Star Wars* universe. Furthermore, he admitted that he made the filming process "way more exhausting for" himself than it needed to be because, while he was working on *Star Wars*, he "hadn't quite figured out the momentum of a set that was that big."[[139]](#cite_note-Variety_Adam-139) Meanwhile, [Daisy Ridley](/wiki/Daisy_Ridley "Daisy Ridley")—who portrayed Rey in the sequel trilogy and is set to return in a [forthcoming film](/wiki/Untitled_Star_Wars_film_(Sharmeen_Obaid-Chinoy) "Untitled Star Wars film (Sharmeen Obaid-Chinoy)")—did not confirm nor deny if Solo would ever return to *Star Wars* because she did not have any information to that affect. When asked if Driver or her other sequel co-stars could return, she simply said she not know "what or who is who" in the upcoming film.[[140]](#cite_note-Variety_Interview-140) Later, she repeated that she had no idea if Solo was set to make some kind of posthumous appearance.[[141]](#cite_note-Deadline_03-10-24-141)

### Further appearances

:   "*What a gift that character is. Everything he does is driven by self-hatred and self-love in equal measure. A rich stew.*"
:   ―Charles Soule, on Kylo Ren[[142]](#cite_note-Soule_7-142)

In addition to being portrayed by Driver in the films, Ren had two voice actors in *[Star Wars Battlefront II](/wiki/Star_Wars_Battlefront_II "Star Wars Battlefront II")*, one for while he wore the mask, and the other for when he had the mask removed. The former was voiced by [Lucasfilm](/wiki/Lucasfilm "Lucasfilm") sound editor [Matthew Wood](/wiki/Matthew_Wood "Matthew Wood"), who previously voiced General [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous") in various *Star Wars* media, while the latter was voiced by [Roger Craig Smith](/wiki/Roger_Craig_Smith "Roger Craig Smith").[[64]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-64) Wood continued the voice role in the [2020](/wiki/2020 "2020") animated movie *[The LEGO Star Wars Holiday Special](/wiki/The_LEGO_Star_Wars_Holiday_Special "The LEGO Star Wars Holiday Special")*.[[143]](#cite_note-Holiday_Special-143)

Kylo Ren was introduced as a playable character of the same name in the 2015 mobile game *Star Wars: Galaxy of Heroes*, which features characters and ships from both the canon and Legends continuities. He has been released 4 times, in 2015 as Kylo Ren, 2017 as Kylo Ren (Unmasked) 2020 as Supreme Leader Kylo Ren, and 2022 as Ben Solo.[[144]](#cite_note-GoH-144) Kylo Ren was confirmed to appear at [*Star Wars*: Galaxy's Edge](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galaxy%27s_Edge "Star Wars: Galaxy's Edge") in one of several promotional trading cards for Rise of the Resistance that were handed out during the [December 16](/wiki/December_16 "December 16"), 2017 "Galactic Nights" event. The card in question, called "RESISTANCE RECRUITS FACE KYLO REN'S INTERROGATION," showed a Resistance soldier being lifted telekinetically by the Knight of Ren.[[145]](#cite_note-WDWNewsToday-145)

The story of Ben Solo's fall to darkness and transformation into Kylo Ren was told in the comic miniseries *[Star Wars: The Rise of Kylo Ren](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Kylo_Ren "Star Wars: The Rise of Kylo Ren")* by [Charles Soule](/wiki/Charles_Soule "Charles Soule"),[[9]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_4-9) who pitched the series with a poetic, thematic reference[[146]](#cite_note-SouleThematic-146) and promised fans it was the story about Ren and his Knights that they had all wanted to see.[[147]](#cite_note-SouleLimitedSeries-147) Soule later returned to the character with the ongoing comic *[Star Wars: Legacy of Vader](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Legacy_of_Vader "Star Wars: Legacy of Vader")*. As regarded by Soule, Ren is a rich character whose every action is driven by an equal mixture of self-love and self-hatred.[[142]](#cite_note-Soule_7-142)

### *The Hunt for Ben Solo*

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [The Hunt for Ben Solo](/wiki/The_Hunt_for_Ben_Solo "The Hunt for Ben Solo")

:   "*I always was interested in doing another* Star Wars*. I had been talking about doing another one since 2021. Kathleen* [Kennedy] *had reached out. I always said: With a great director and a great story, I'd be there in a second. I loved that character and loved playing him.*"
:   ―Adam Driver[[148]](#cite_note-2025AP-148)

Despite his public rejection of returning to *Star Wars* in 2024[[139]](#cite_note-Variety_Adam-139) and Solo's death in *The Rise of Skywalker*, Adam Driver revealed in [2025](/wiki/2025 "2025") that he had always been interested in returning to the franchise and had been in talks about returning as Solo since [2021](/wiki/2021 "2021"); in that year, Lucasfilm President [Kathleen Kennedy](/wiki/Kathleen_Kennedy "Kathleen Kennedy") had reached out to him about possibly returning to the franchise, to which Driver said he would if they could find a director and story good enough enough to warrant his return. Ultimately, Driver partnered with director [Steven Soderbergh](/wiki/Steven_Soderbergh "Steven Soderbergh") for two years to create a pitch that culminated in the possible film *[The Hunt for Ben Solo](/wiki/The_Hunt_for_Ben_Solo "The Hunt for Ben Solo")*. The story would have been set after *The Rise of Skywalker* and featured a surviving Solo, who Driver believed had unfinished business he wanted to explore. Joined by Rebecca Blunt, Soderbergh and Driver created a story pitch that they presented to Lucasfilm higherups Kennedy, [Carrie Beck](/wiki/Carrie_Beck "Carrie Beck"), and [Dave Filoni](/wiki/Dave_Filoni "Dave Filoni"), all of whom were interested.[[148]](#cite_note-2025AP-148)

With Lucasfilm's interest secured, Driver and company recruited filmmaker Scott Z. Burns to create a script that Driver was amazed by, calling it "one of the coolest" scripts he had ever been involved with. Lucasfilm loved the script and understood the plan the team had for the film, but [Bob Iger](/wiki/Bob_Iger "Bob Iger") and Alan Bergman of The Walt Disney Company did not understand how Solo had survived so vetoed the project. In 2025, Driver said he could finally talk about the film in an interview with AP News and promised it would have been "really cool." Soderbergh concurred; in a statement to AP News, he said he "really enjoyed making the movie in my head" and apologized to fans that they would never be able to see it.[[148]](#cite_note-2025AP-148)

### Continuity

#### Connections and similarities

 [![Kylo Ren shares some similarities with Jacen Solo, the son of Leia and Han in Star Wars Legends, who became the Sith Lord Darth Caedus.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fd/C-GA_War.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080419002117) [![Kylo Ren shares some similarities with Jacen Solo, the son of Leia and Han in Star Wars Legends, who became the Sith Lord Darth Caedus.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fd/C-GA_War.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/214?cb=20080419002117)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fd/C-GA_War.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080419002117) 

Kylo Ren shares some similarities with Jacen Solo, the son of Leia and Han in *Star Wars* Legends, who became the Sith Lord Darth Caedus.

 

Kylo Ren shares some similarities with [Jacen Solo](/wiki/Darth_Caedus "Darth Caedus"),[[149]](#cite_note-CBR-149) the son of [Leia Organa Solo](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo") and [Han Solo](/wiki/Han_Solo/Legends "Han Solo/Legends") in the now non-[canonical](/wiki/Canon "Canon") [*Star Wars* Legends](/wiki/Star_Wars_Legends "Star Wars Legends") storyline. Jacen, the twin brother of [Jaina Solo Fel](/wiki/Jaina_Solo_Fel "Jaina Solo Fel"), was a [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight/Legends "Jedi Knight/Legends") who ultimately turned to the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force/Legends "Dark side of the Force/Legends") and became the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord/Legends "Sith Lord/Legends") Darth Caedus under the guidance of the Sith Lady [Lumiya](/wiki/Lumiya "Lumiya"). It was Jacen's hope to lead the [Galactic Alliance](/wiki/Galactic_Federation_of_Free_Alliances "Galactic Federation of Free Alliances"), once the New Republic, in bringing order to [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy/Legends "The galaxy/Legends") after the horrors of the [Yuuzhan Vong War](/wiki/Yuuzhan_Vong_War "Yuuzhan Vong War"). He killed his aunt [Mara Jade Skywalker](/wiki/Mara_Jade_Skywalker "Mara Jade Skywalker"),[[150]](#cite_note-LOTF_Sacrifice-150) and committed atrocities across the galaxy before he was finally killed by his sister at the end of the [Second Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Second_Galactic_Civil_War "Second Galactic Civil War").[[151]](#cite_note-LOTF_Invincible-151)

Ren shares a similar name to that of *Legends* character [Kybo Ren](/wiki/Gir_Kybo_Ren-Cha "Gir Kybo Ren-Cha"), a space pirate from the *Legends* animated series *[Star Wars: Droids: The Adventures of R2-D2 and C-3PO](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Droids:_The_Adventures_of_R2-D2_and_C-3PO "Star Wars: Droids: The Adventures of R2-D2 and C-3PO")*.[[152]](#cite_note-The_Pirates_of_Tarnoonga-152)

#### Canon contradictions

The *[Star Wars: The Force Awakens—The Official Visual Story Guide](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Force_Awakens%E2%80%94The_Official_Visual_Story_Guide "Star Wars: The Force Awakens—The Official Visual Story Guide")* magazine from [March 20](/wiki/March_20 "March 20"), [2016](/wiki/2016 "2016"),[[153]](#cite_note-AmazonMagazine-153) claims that Kylo Ren founded the Knights of Ren on page sixty-four. Earlier in its text, on page eight, however, the magazine states that Ren had simply joined the group.[[154]](#cite_note-OfficialMagazineGuide-154) In 2019[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47) and 2020,[[25]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-25) the *Rise of Kylo Ren* comic series would confirm that the Knights were,[[47]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_1-47) as suggested by page eight of the prior guide,[[154]](#cite_note-OfficialMagazineGuide-154) a pre-existing organization that Ren had joined the ranks of[[13]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_3-13) before arising to a position of leadership over its members.[[9]](#cite_note-Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_4-9)

### In popular culture

#### Matt the Radar Technician

 [![On Saturday Night Live, Adam Driver played Kylo Ren as taking on the role of "Matt the Radar Technician" to better understand the personnel under his command](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1c/Matt_the_Radar_Technician.png/revision/latest?cb=20160206214938) [![On Saturday Night Live, Adam Driver played Kylo Ren as taking on the role of "Matt the Radar Technician" to better understand the personnel under his command](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1c/Matt_the_Radar_Technician.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20160206214938)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1c/Matt_the_Radar_Technician.png/revision/latest?cb=20160206214938) 

On *Saturday Night Live*, Adam Driver played Kylo Ren as taking on the role of "Matt the Radar Technician" to better understand the personnel under his command

 

On [January 17](/wiki/January_17 "January 17"), 2016, Driver hosted the popular sketch comedy show *[Saturday Night Live](/wiki/Saturday_Night_Live "Saturday Night Live")* and filmed a sketch called "Undercover Boss: Starkiller Base." Parodying the show [*Undercover Boss*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Undercover_Boss "wikipedia:Undercover Boss"), Kylo Ren disguises himself as a radar technician named Matt and mingles with the crew of Starkiller Base—including a stormtrooper played by future *[Star Wars Resistance](/wiki/Star_Wars_Resistance "Star Wars Resistance")* voice actor [Bobby Moynihan](/wiki/Bobby_Moynihan "Bobby Moynihan")—to learn more about what it is like to work on the base. Throughout the sketch, in which he becomes friends with a Lieutenant Colonel named Zack ([Taran Killam](/wiki/Taran_Killam "Taran Killam")), whose son he killed months earlier, Ren displays his fiery temper on numerous occasions, particularly when crew members criticized Ren without knowing who they were speaking to. In the end, Ren says that he feels he understands the crew of Starkiller Base better and that he is ready to show everyone a brand new Kylo Ren—as Zack's lifeless body sits in the background.[[155]](#cite_note-Undercover_Starkiller-155) Driver again appeared on the show on [January 25](/wiki/January_25 "January 25"), 2020, appearing in a follow-up skit in which he goes undercover as "Randy the Intern."[[156]](#cite_note-Adam_SNL-156)

#### Ben Swolo

 [!["Ben Swolo," as described by fans](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f7/Ben_Swolo.png/revision/latest?cb=20191226024035) [!["Ben Swolo," as described by fans](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f7/Ben_Swolo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20191226024035)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f7/Ben_Swolo.png/revision/latest?cb=20191226024035) 

"Ben Swolo," as described by fans

 

In *The Last Jedi*, Kylo Ren is briefly featured shirtless in one of his conversations with Rey via their Force bond.[[37]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-37) A screenshot of Ren's muscular body quickly spread around the internet as a meme, which dubbed the character "Ben Swolo" or simply "Shirtless Kylo Ren" while in that form.[[157]](#cite_note-Ben_Swolo-157) The original *Undercover Boss* skit had also featured "Matt" comment to a group of stormtroopers that a friend told him that he saw Kylo Ren in the [shower](/wiki/Shower "Shower") and that Ren "had an eight-pack" and was "shredded." These lines proved a source of retroactive amusement when *The Last Jedi* indeed featured Ren's shirtless appearance. In response to the online discussion around the scene, Director Rian Johnson explained that the scene was not merely gratuitous, but was intended to establish that through their Force-bond, Rey could actually see his body and not simply hear his voice or see just his face and eyes.[[158]](#cite_note-shirtless-158) Ren's shirtless appearance was later parodied in the *[The LEGO Star Wars Holiday Special](/wiki/The_LEGO_Star_Wars_Holiday_Special "The LEGO Star Wars Holiday Special")*.[[159]](#cite_note-HS-159)

[31.3](#cite_ref-Star_Wars_50_31-3) [31.4](#cite_ref-Star_Wars_50_31-4) [*Star Wars* (2020) 50](/wiki/Star_Wars_(2020)_50 "Star Wars (2020) 50") 32. [↑](#cite_ref-AhsokaDate_32-0) [SWInsider](/wiki/Star_Wars_Insider "Star Wars Insider") "[A Certain Point of View](/wiki/A_Certain_Point_of_View_(department) "A Certain Point of View (department)")" — [*Star Wars Insider* 228](/wiki/Star_Wars_Insider_228 "Star Wars Insider 228") dates the events of "[Part Seven: Dreams and Madness](/wiki/Part_Seven:_Dreams_and_Madness "Part Seven: Dreams and Madness")" to nine [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") after [*Star Wars*: Episode IV *A New Hope*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope"), which corresponds to [9 ABY](/wiki/9_ABY "9 ABY") per *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")*. Preceding episodes, also take place in that year, since they take place after *[Star Wars: The Book of Boba Fett](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Book_of_Boba_Fett "Star Wars: The Book of Boba Fett")*, which is dated to 9 [ABY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system") according to *Timelines*. As "[Part Eight: The Jedi, the Witch, and the Warlord](/wiki/Part_Eight:_The_Jedi,_the_Witch,_and_the_Warlord "Part Eight: The Jedi, the Witch, and the Warlord")" takes place shortly after Part Seven, the events of [*Ahsoka*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Ahsoka "Star Wars: Ahsoka") as a whole must all take place within the same year. 33. [↑](#cite_ref-Creation_date_117-0) *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates the beginning of **Ben Solo**'s [Jedi training](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") to [15 ABY](/wiki/15_ABY "15 ABY"). His earliest known usage of the [lightsaber](/wiki/Lightsaber "Lightsaber") was an encounter with the [Knights of Ren](/wiki/Knights_of_Ren "Knights of Ren") in [*The Rise of Kylo Ren* 2](/wiki/The_Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2 "The Rise of Kylo Ren 2"), which dates to around [19 ABY](/wiki/19_ABY "19 ABY") per *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")*. Therefore, Solo built the lightsaber between 15 [ABY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system") and around 19 ABY. 118.
